BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP manos tu śatarūpāyāṃ tisraḥ kanyāś ca jajñire
BhP ākūtir devahūtiś ca prasūtir iti viśrutāḥ
BhP ākūtiṃ rucaye prādād api bhrātṛmatīṃ nṛpaḥ
BhP putrikādharmam āśritya śatarūpānumoditaḥ
BhP prajāpatiḥ sa bhagavān rucis tasyām ajījanat
BhP mithunaṃ brahmavarcasvī parameṇa samādhinā
BhP yas tayoḥ puruṣaḥ sākṣād viṣṇur yajñasvarūpadhṛk
BhP yā strī sā dakṣiṇā bhūter aṃśabhūtānapāyinī
BhP āninye svagṛhaṃ putryāḥ putraṃ vitatarociṣam
BhP svāyambhuvo mudā yukto rucir jagrāha dakṣiṇām
BhP tāṃ kāmayānāṃ bhagavān uvāha yajuṣāṃ patiḥ
BhP tuṣṭāyāṃ toṣam āpanno ' janayad dvādaśātmajān
BhP toṣaḥ pratoṣaḥ santoṣo bhadraḥ śāntir iḍaspatiḥ
BhP idhmaḥ kavir vibhuḥ svahnaḥ sudevo rocano dviṣaṭ
BhP tuṣitā nāma te devā āsan svāyambhuvāntare
BhP marīcimiśrā ṛṣayo yajñaḥ suragaṇeśvaraḥ
BhP priyavratottānapādau manuputrau mahaujasau
BhP tatputrapautranaptṝṇām anuvṛttaṃ tadantaram
BhP devahūtim adāt tāta kardamāyātmajāṃ manuḥ
BhP tatsambandhi śrutaprāyaṃ bhavatā gadato mama
BhP dakṣāya brahmaputrāya prasūtiṃ bhagavān manuḥ
BhP prāyacchad yatkṛtaḥ sargas trilokyāṃ vitato mahān
BhP yāḥ kardamasutāḥ proktā nava brahmarṣipatnayaḥ
BhP tāsāṃ prasūtiprasavaṃ procyamānaṃ nibodha me
BhP patnī marīces tu kalā suṣuve kardamātmajā
BhP kaśyapaṃ pūrṇimānaṃ ca yayor āpūritaṃ jagat
BhP pūrṇimāsūta virajaṃ viśvagaṃ ca parantapa
BhP devakulyāṃ hareḥ pāda śaucād yābhūt sarid divaḥ
BhP atreḥ patny anasūyā trīñ jajñe suyaśasaḥ sutān
BhP dattaṃ durvāsasaṃ somam ātmeśabrahmasambhavān
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP atrer gṛhe suraśreṣṭhāḥ sthityutpattyantahetavaḥ
BhP kiñcic cikīrṣavo jātā etad ākhyāhi me guro
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP brahmaṇā coditaḥ sṛṣṭāv atrir brahmavidāṃ varaḥ
BhP saha patnyā yayāv ṛkṣaṃ kulādriṃ tapasi sthitaḥ
BhP tasmin prasūnastabaka palāśāśokakānane
BhP vārbhiḥ sravadbhir udghuṣṭe nirvindhyāyāḥ samantataḥ
BhP prāṇāyāmena saṃyamya mano varṣaśataṃ muniḥ
BhP atiṣṭhad ekapādena nirdvandvo 'nilabhojanaḥ
BhP śaraṇaṃ taṃ prapadye 'haṃ ya eva jagadīśvaraḥ
BhP prajām ātmasamāṃ mahyaṃ prayacchatv iti cintayan
BhP tapyamānaṃ tribhuvanaṃ prāṇāyāmaidhasāgninā
BhP nirgatena muner mūrdhnaḥ samīkṣya prabhavas trayaḥ
BhP apsaromunigandharva siddhavidyādharoragaiḥ
BhP vitāyamānayaśasas tadāśramapadaṃ yayuḥ
BhP tatprādurbhāvasaṃyoga vidyotitamanā muniḥ
BhP uttiṣṭhann ekapādena dadarśa vibudharṣabhān
BhP praṇamya daṇḍavad bhūmāv upatasthe 'rhaṇāñjaliḥ
BhP vṛṣahaṃsasuparṇasthān svaiḥ svaiś cihnaiś ca cihnitān
BhP kṛpāvalokena hasad vadanenopalambhitān
BhP tadrociṣā pratihate nimīlya munir akṣiṇī
BhP cetas tatpravaṇaṃ yuñjann astāvīt saṃhatāñjaliḥ
BhP ślakṣṇayā sūktayā vācā sarvalokagarīyasaḥ
BhP atrir uvāca
BhP viśvodbhavasthitilayeṣu vibhajyamānair
BhP māyāguṇair anuyugaṃ vigṛhītadehāḥ
BhP te brahmaviṣṇugiriśāḥ praṇato 'smy ahaṃ vas
BhP tebhyaḥ ka eva bhavatāṃ ma ihopahūtaḥ
BhP eko mayeha bhagavān vividhapradhānaiś
BhP cittīkṛtaḥ prajananāya kathaṃ nu yūyam
BhP atrāgatās tanubhṛtāṃ manaso 'pi dūrād
BhP brūta prasīdata mahān iha vismayo me
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā trayas te vibudharṣabhāḥ
BhP pratyāhuḥ ślakṣṇayā vācā prahasya tam ṛṣiṃ prabho
BhP devā ūcuḥ
BhP yathā kṛtas te saṅkalpo bhāvyaṃ tenaiva nānyathā
BhP satsaṅkalpasya te brahman yad vai dhyāyati te vayam
BhP athāsmadaṃśabhūtās te ātmajā lokaviśrutāḥ
BhP bhavitāro 'ṅga bhadraṃ te visrapsyanti ca te yaśaḥ
BhP evaṃ kāmavaraṃ dattvā pratijagmuḥ sureśvarāḥ
BhP sabhājitās tayoḥ samyag dampatyor miṣatos tataḥ
BhP somo 'bhūd brahmaṇo 'ṃśena datto viṣṇos tu yogavit
BhP durvāsāḥ śaṅkarasyāṃśo nibodhāṅgirasaḥ prajāḥ
BhP śraddhā tv aṅgirasaḥ patnī catasro 'sūta kanyakāḥ
BhP sinīvālī kuhū rākā caturthy anumatis tathā
BhP tatputrāv aparāv āstāṃ khyātau svārociṣe 'ntare
BhP utathyo bhagavān sākṣād brahmiṣṭhaś ca bṛhaspatiḥ
BhP pulastyo 'janayat patnyām agastyaṃ ca havirbhuvi
BhP so 'nyajanmani dahrāgnir viśravāś ca mahātapāḥ
BhP tasya yakṣapatir devaḥ kuberas tv iḍaviḍāsutaḥ
BhP rāvaṇaḥ kumbhakarṇaś ca tathānyasyāṃ vibhīṣaṇaḥ
BhP pulahasya gatir bhāryā trīn asūta satī sutān
BhP karmaśreṣṭhaṃ varīyāṃsaṃ sahiṣṇuṃ ca mahāmate
BhP krator api kriyā bhāryā vālakhilyān asūyata
BhP ṛṣīn ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi jvalato brahmatejasā
BhP ūrjāyāṃ jajñire putrā vasiṣṭhasya parantapa
BhP citraketupradhānās te sapta brahmarṣayo 'malāḥ
BhP citraketuḥ surociś ca virajā mitra eva ca
BhP ulbaṇo vasubhṛdyāno dyumān śaktyādayo 'pare
BhP cittis tv atharvaṇaḥ patnī lebhe putraṃ dhṛtavratam
BhP dadhyañcam aśvaśirasaṃ bhṛgor vaṃśaṃ nibodha me
BhP bhṛguḥ khyātyāṃ mahābhāgaḥ patnyāṃ putrān ajījanat
BhP dhātāraṃ ca vidhātāraṃ śriyaṃ ca bhagavatparām
BhP āyatiṃ niyatiṃ caiva sute merus tayor adāt
BhP tābhyāṃ tayor abhavatāṃ mṛkaṇḍaḥ prāṇa eva ca
BhP mārkaṇḍeyo mṛkaṇḍasya prāṇād vedaśirā muniḥ
BhP kaviś ca bhārgavo yasya bhagavān uśanā sutaḥ
BhP ta ete munayaḥ kṣattar lokān sargair abhāvayan
BhP eṣa kardamadauhitra santānaḥ kathitas tava
BhP śṛṇvataḥ śraddadhānasya sadyaḥ pāpaharaḥ paraḥ
BhP prasūtiṃ mānavīṃ dakṣa upayeme hy ajātmajaḥ
BhP tasyāṃ sasarja duhitṝḥ ṣoḍaśāmalalocanāḥ
BhP trayodaśādād dharmāya tathaikām agnaye vibhuḥ
BhP pitṛbhya ekāṃ yuktebhyo bhavāyaikāṃ bhavacchide
BhP śraddhā maitrī dayā śāntis tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyonnatiḥ
BhP buddhir medhā titikṣā hrīr mūrtir dharmasya patnayaḥ
BhP śraddhāsūta śubhaṃ maitrī prasādam abhayaṃ dayā
BhP śāntiḥ sukhaṃ mudaṃ tuṣṭiḥ smayaṃ puṣṭir asūyata
BhP yogaṃ kriyonnatir darpam arthaṃ buddhir asūyata
BhP medhā smṛtiṃ titikṣā tu kṣemaṃ hrīḥ praśrayaṃ sutam
BhP mūrtiḥ sarvaguṇotpattir naranārāyaṇāv ṛṣī
BhP yayor janmany ado viśvam abhyanandat sunirvṛtam
BhP manāṃsi kakubho vātāḥ praseduḥ sarito 'drayaḥ
BhP divy avādyanta tūryāṇi petuḥ kusumavṛṣṭayaḥ
BhP munayas tuṣṭuvus tuṣṭā jagur gandharvakinnarāḥ
BhP nṛtyanti sma striyo devya āsīt paramamaṅgalam
BhP devā brahmādayaḥ sarve upatasthur abhiṣṭavaiḥ
BhP devā ūcuḥ
BhP yo māyayā viracitaṃ nijayātmanīdaṃ
BhP khe rūpabhedam iva tatpraticakṣaṇāya
BhP etena dharmasadane ṛṣimūrtinādya
BhP prāduścakāra puruṣāya namaḥ parasmai
BhP so 'yaṃ sthitivyatikaropaśamāya sṛṣṭān
BhP sattvena naḥ suragaṇān anumeyatattvaḥ
BhP dṛśyād adabhrakaruṇena vilokanena
BhP yac chrīniketam amalaṃ kṣipatāravindam
BhP evaṃ suragaṇais tāta bhagavantāv abhiṣṭutau
BhP labdhāvalokair yayatur arcitau gandhamādanam
BhP tāv imau vai bhagavato harer aṃśāv ihāgatau
BhP bhāravyayāya ca bhuvaḥ kṛṣṇau yadukurūdvahau
BhP svāhābhimāninaś cāgner ātmajāṃs trīn ajījanat
BhP pāvakaṃ pavamānaṃ ca śuciṃ ca hutabhojanam
BhP tebhyo 'gnayaḥ samabhavan catvāriṃśac ca pañca ca
BhP ta evaikonapañcāśat sākaṃ pitṛpitāmahaiḥ
BhP vaitānike karmaṇi yan nāmabhir brahmavādibhiḥ
BhP āgneyya iṣṭayo yajñe nirūpyante 'gnayas tu te
BhP agniṣvāttā barhiṣadaḥ saumyāḥ pitara ājyapāḥ
BhP sāgnayo 'nagnayas teṣāṃ patnī dākṣāyaṇī svadhā
BhP tebhyo dadhāra kanye dve vayunāṃ dhāriṇīṃ svadhā
BhP ubhe te brahmavādinyau jñānavijñānapārage
BhP bhavasya patnī tu satī bhavaṃ devam anuvratā
BhP ātmanaḥ sadṛśaṃ putraṃ na lebhe guṇaśīlataḥ
BhP pitary apratirūpe sve bhavāyānāgase ruṣā
BhP aprauḍhaivātmanātmānam ajahād yogasaṃyutā
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP bhave śīlavatāṃ śreṣṭhe dakṣo duhitṛvatsalaḥ
BhP vidveṣam akarot kasmād anādṛtyātmajāṃ satīm
BhP kas taṃ carācaraguruṃ nirvairaṃ śāntavigraham
BhP ātmārāmaṃ kathaṃ dveṣṭi jagato daivataṃ mahat
BhP etad ākhyāhi me brahman jāmātuḥ śvaśurasya ca
BhP vidveṣas tu yataḥ prāṇāṃs tatyaje dustyajān satī
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP purā viśvasṛjāṃ satre sametāḥ paramarṣayaḥ
BhP tathāmaragaṇāḥ sarve sānugā munayo 'gnayaḥ
BhP tatra praviṣṭam ṛṣayo dṛṣṭvārkam iva rociṣā
BhP bhrājamānaṃ vitimiraṃ kurvantaṃ tan mahat sadaḥ
BhP udatiṣṭhan sadasyās te svadhiṣṇyebhyaḥ sahāgnayaḥ
BhP ṛte viriñcāṃ śarvaṃ ca tadbhāsākṣiptacetasaḥ
BhP sadasaspatibhir dakṣo bhagavān sādhu satkṛtaḥ
BhP ajaṃ lokaguruṃ natvā niṣasāda tadājñayā
BhP prāṅniṣaṇṇaṃ mṛḍaṃ dṛṣṭvā nāmṛṣyat tadanādṛtaḥ
BhP uvāca vāmaṃ cakṣurbhyām abhivīkṣya dahann iva
BhP śrūyatāṃ brahmarṣayo me sahadevāḥ sahāgnayaḥ
BhP sādhūnāṃ bruvato vṛttaṃ nājñānān na ca matsarāt
BhP ayaṃ tu lokapālānāṃ yaśoghno nirapatrapaḥ
BhP sadbhir ācaritaḥ panthā yena stabdhena dūṣitaḥ
BhP eṣa me śiṣyatāṃ prāpto yan me duhitur agrahīt
BhP pāṇiṃ viprāgnimukhataḥ sāvitryā iva sādhuvat
BhP gṛhītvā mṛgaśāvākṣyāḥ pāṇiṃ markaṭalocanaḥ
BhP pratyutthānābhivādārhe vācāpy akṛta nocitam
BhP luptakriyāyāśucaye mānine bhinnasetave
BhP anicchann apy adāṃ bālāṃ śūdrāyevośatīṃ giram
BhP pretāvāseṣu ghoreṣu pretair bhūtagaṇair vṛtaḥ
BhP aṭaty unmattavan nagno vyuptakeśo hasan rudan
BhP citābhasmakṛtasnānaḥ pretasraṅnrasthibhūṣaṇaḥ
BhP śivāpadeśo hy aśivo matto mattajanapriyaḥ
BhP patiḥ pramathanāthānāṃ tamomātrātmakātmanām
BhP tasmā unmādanāthāya naṣṭaśaucāya durhṛde
BhP dattā bata mayā sādhvī codite parameṣṭhinā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP vinindyaivaṃ sa giriśam apratīpam avasthitam
BhP dakṣo 'thāpa upaspṛśya kruddhaḥ śaptuṃ pracakrame
BhP ayaṃ tu devayajana indropendrādibhir bhavaḥ
BhP saha bhāgaṃ na labhatāṃ devair devagaṇādhamaḥ
BhP niṣidhyamānaḥ sa sadasyamukhyair dakṣo giritrāya visṛjya śāpam
BhP tasmād viniṣkramya vivṛddhamanyur jagāma kauravya nijaṃ niketanam
BhP vijñāya śāpaṃ giriśānugāgraṇīr nandīśvaro roṣakaṣāyadūṣitaḥ
BhP dakṣāya śāpaṃ visasarja dāruṇaṃ ye cānvamodaṃs tadavācyatāṃ dvijāḥ
BhP ya etan martyam uddiśya bhagavaty apratidruhi
BhP druhyaty ajñaḥ pṛthagdṛṣṭis tattvato vimukho bhavet
BhP gṛheṣu kūṭadharmeṣu sakto grāmyasukhecchayā
BhP karmatantraṃ vitanute vedavādavipannadhīḥ
BhP buddhyā parābhidhyāyinyā vismṛtātmagatiḥ paśuḥ
BhP strīkāmaḥ so 'stv atitarāṃ dakṣo bastamukho 'cirāt
BhP vidyābuddhir avidyāyāṃ karmamayyām asau jaḍaḥ
BhP saṃsarantv iha ye cāmum anu śarvāvamāninam
BhP giraḥ śrutāyāḥ puṣpiṇyā madhugandhena bhūriṇā
BhP mathnā conmathitātmānaḥ sammuhyantu haradviṣaḥ
BhP sarvabhakṣā dvijā vṛttyai dhṛtavidyātapovratāḥ
BhP vittadehendriyārāmā yācakā vicarantv iha
BhP tasyaivaṃ vadataḥ śāpaṃ śrutvā dvijakulāya vai
BhP bhṛguḥ pratyasṛjac chāpaṃ brahmadaṇḍaṃ duratyayam
BhP bhavavratadharā ye ca ye ca tān samanuvratāḥ
BhP pāṣaṇḍinas te bhavantu sacchāstraparipanthinaḥ
BhP naṣṭaśaucā mūḍhadhiyo jaṭābhasmāsthidhāriṇaḥ
BhP viśantu śivadīkṣāyāṃ yatra daivaṃ surāsavam
BhP brahma ca brāhmaṇāṃś caiva yad yūyaṃ parinindatha
BhP setuṃ vidhāraṇaṃ puṃsām ataḥ pāṣaṇḍam āśritāḥ
BhP eṣa eva hi lokānāṃ śivaḥ panthāḥ sanātanaḥ
BhP yaṃ pūrve cānusantasthur yatpramāṇaṃ janārdanaḥ
BhP tad brahma paramaṃ śuddhaṃ satāṃ vartma sanātanam
BhP vigarhya yāta pāṣaṇḍaṃ daivaṃ vo yatra bhūtarāṭ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP tasyaivaṃ vadataḥ śāpaṃ bhṛgoḥ sa bhagavān bhavaḥ
BhP niścakrāma tataḥ kiñcid vimanā iva sānugaḥ
BhP te 'pi viśvasṛjaḥ satraṃ sahasraparivatsarān
BhP saṃvidhāya maheṣvāsa yatrejya ṛṣabho hariḥ
BhP āplutyāvabhṛthaṃ yatra gaṅgā yamunayānvitā
BhP virajenātmanā sarve svaṃ svaṃ dhāma yayus tataḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sadā vidviṣator evaṃ kālo vai dhriyamāṇayoḥ
BhP jāmātuḥ śvaśurasyāpi sumahān aticakrame
BhP yadābhiṣikto dakṣas tu brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā
BhP prajāpatīnāṃ sarveṣām ādhipatye smayo 'bhavat
BhP iṣṭvā sa vājapeyena brahmiṣṭhān abhibhūya ca
BhP bṛhaspatisavaṃ nāma samārebhe kratūttamam
BhP tasmin brahmarṣayaḥ sarve devarṣipitṛdevatāḥ
BhP āsan kṛtasvastyayanās tatpatnyaś ca sabhartṛkāḥ
BhP tad upaśrutya nabhasi khecarāṇāṃ prajalpatām
BhP satī dākṣāyaṇī devī pitṛyajñamahotsavam
BhP vrajantīḥ sarvato digbhya upadevavarastriyaḥ
BhP vimānayānāḥ sapreṣṭhā niṣkakaṇṭhīḥ suvāsasaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭvā svanilayābhyāśe lolākṣīr mṛṣṭakuṇḍalāḥ
BhP patiṃ bhūtapatiṃ devam autsukyād abhyabhāṣata
BhP saty uvāca
BhP prajāpates te śvaśurasya sāmprataṃ niryāpito yajñamahotsavaḥ kila
BhP vayaṃ ca tatrābhisarāma vāma te yady arthitāmī vibudhā vrajanti hi
BhP tasmin bhaginyo mama bhartṛbhiḥ svakair dhruvaṃ gamiṣyanti suhṛddidṛkṣavaḥ
BhP ahaṃ ca tasmin bhavatābhikāmaye sahopanītaṃ paribarham arhitum
BhP tatra svasṝr me nanu bhartṛsammitā mātṛṣvasṝḥ klinnadhiyaṃ ca mātaram
BhP drakṣye cirotkaṇṭhamanā maharṣibhir unnīyamānaṃ ca mṛḍādhvaradhvajam
BhP tvayy etad āścaryam ajātmamāyayā vinirmitaṃ bhāti guṇatrayātmakam
BhP tathāpy ahaṃ yoṣid atattvavic ca te dīnā didṛkṣe bhava me bhavakṣitim
BhP paśya prayāntīr abhavānyayoṣito 'py alaṅkṛtāḥ kāntasakhā varūthaśaḥ
BhP yāsāṃ vrajadbhiḥ śitikaṇṭha maṇḍitaṃ nabho vimānaiḥ kalahaṃsapāṇḍubhiḥ
BhP kathaṃ sutāyāḥ pitṛgehakautukaṃ niśamya dehaḥ suravarya neṅgate
BhP anāhutā apy abhiyanti sauhṛdaṃ bhartur guror dehakṛtaś ca ketanam
BhP tan me prasīdedam amartya vāñchitaṃ kartuṃ bhavān kāruṇiko batārhati
BhP tvayātmano 'rdhe 'ham adabhracakṣuṣā nirūpitā mānugṛhāṇa yācitaḥ
BhP ṛṣir uvāca
BhP evaṃ giritraḥ priyayābhibhāṣitaḥ pratyabhyadhatta prahasan suhṛtpriyaḥ
BhP saṃsmārito marmabhidaḥ kuvāgiṣūn yān āha ko viśvasṛjāṃ samakṣataḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP tvayoditaṃ śobhanam eva śobhane anāhutā apy abhiyanti bandhuṣu
BhP te yady anutpāditadoṣadṛṣṭayo balīyasānātmyamadena manyunā
BhP vidyātapovittavapurvayaḥkulaiḥ satāṃ guṇaiḥ ṣaḍbhir asattametaraiḥ
BhP smṛtau hatāyāṃ bhṛtamānadurdṛśaḥ stabdhā na paśyanti hi dhāma bhūyasām
BhP naitādṛśānāṃ svajanavyapekṣayā gṛhān pratīyād anavasthitātmanām
BhP ye 'bhyāgatān vakradhiyābhicakṣate āropitabhrūbhir amarṣaṇākṣibhiḥ
BhP tathāribhir na vyathate śilīmukhaiḥ śete 'rditāṅgo hṛdayena dūyatā
BhP svānāṃ yathā vakradhiyāṃ duruktibhir divāniśaṃ tapyati marmatāḍitaḥ
BhP vyaktaṃ tvam utkṛṣṭagateḥ prajāpateḥ priyātmajānām asi subhru me matā
BhP tathāpi mānaṃ na pituḥ prapatsyase madāśrayāt kaḥ paritapyate yataḥ
BhP pāpacyamānena hṛdāturendriyaḥ samṛddhibhiḥ pūruṣabuddhisākṣiṇām
BhP akalpa eṣām adhiroḍhum añjasā paraṃ padaṃ dveṣṭi yathāsurā harim
BhP pratyudgamapraśrayaṇābhivādanaṃ vidhīyate sādhu mithaḥ sumadhyame
BhP prājñaiḥ parasmai puruṣāya cetasā guhāśayāyaiva na dehamānine
BhP sattvaṃ viśuddhaṃ vasudevaśabditaṃ yad īyate tatra pumān apāvṛtaḥ
BhP sattve ca tasmin bhagavān vāsudevo hy adhokṣajo me namasā vidhīyate
BhP tat te nirīkṣyo na pitāpi dehakṛd dakṣo mama dviṭ tadanuvratāś ca ye
BhP yo viśvasṛgyajñagataṃ varoru mām anāgasaṃ durvacasākarot tiraḥ
BhP yadi vrajiṣyasy atihāya madvaco bhadraṃ bhavatyā na tato bhaviṣyati
BhP sambhāvitasya svajanāt parābhavo yadā sa sadyo maraṇāya kalpate
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP etāvad uktvā virarāma śaṅkaraḥ patnyaṅganāśaṃ hy ubhayatra cintayan
BhP suhṛddidṛkṣuḥ pariśaṅkitā bhavān niṣkrāmatī nirviśatī dvidhāsa sā
BhP suhṛddidṛkṣāpratighātadurmanāḥ snehād rudaty aśrukalātivihvalā
BhP bhavaṃ bhavāny apratipūruṣaṃ ruṣā pradhakṣyatīvaikṣata jātavepathuḥ
BhP tato viniḥśvasya satī vihāya taṃ śokena roṣeṇa ca dūyatā hṛdā
BhP pitror agāt straiṇavimūḍhadhīr gṛhān premṇātmano yo 'rdham adāt satāṃ priyaḥ
BhP tām anvagacchan drutavikramāṃ satīm ekāṃ trinetrānucarāḥ sahasraśaḥ
BhP sapārṣadayakṣā maṇimanmadādayaḥ purovṛṣendrās tarasā gatavyathāḥ
BhP tāṃ sārikākandukadarpaṇāmbuja śvetātapatravyajanasragādibhiḥ
BhP gītāyanair dundubhiśaṅkhaveṇubhir vṛṣendram āropya viṭaṅkitā yayuḥ
BhP ābrahmaghoṣorjitayajñavaiśasaṃ viprarṣijuṣṭaṃ vibudhaiś ca sarvaśaḥ
BhP mṛddārvayaḥkāñcanadarbhacarmabhir nisṛṣṭabhāṇḍaṃ yajanaṃ samāviśat
BhP tām āgatāṃ tatra na kaścanādriyad vimānitāṃ yajñakṛto bhayāj janaḥ
BhP ṛte svasṝr vai jananīṃ ca sādarāḥ premāśrukaṇṭhyaḥ pariṣasvajur mudā
BhP saudaryasampraśnasamarthavārtayā mātrā ca mātṛṣvasṛbhiś ca sādaram
BhP dattāṃ saparyāṃ varam āsanaṃ ca sā nādatta pitrāpratinanditā satī
BhP arudrabhāgaṃ tam avekṣya cādhvaraṃ pitrā ca deve kṛtahelanaṃ vibhau
BhP anādṛtā yajñasadasy adhīśvarī cukopa lokān iva dhakṣyatī ruṣā
BhP jagarha sāmarṣavipannayā girā śivadviṣaṃ dhūmapathaśramasmayam
BhP svatejasā bhūtagaṇān samutthitān nigṛhya devī jagato 'bhiśṛṇvataḥ
BhP devy uvāca
BhP na yasya loke 'sty atiśāyanaḥ priyas tathāpriyo dehabhṛtāṃ priyātmanaḥ
BhP tasmin samastātmani muktavairake ṛte bhavantaṃ katamaḥ pratīpayet
BhP doṣān pareṣāṃ hi guṇeṣu sādhavo gṛhṇanti kecin na bhavādṛśo dvija
BhP guṇāṃś ca phalgūn bahulīkariṣṇavo mahattamās teṣv avidad bhavān agham
BhP nāścaryam etad yad asatsu sarvadā mahadvinindā kuṇapātmavādiṣu
BhP serṣyaṃ mahāpūruṣapādapāṃsubhir nirastatejaḥsu tad eva śobhanam
BhP yad dvyakṣaraṃ nāma gireritaṃ nṛṇāṃ sakṛt prasaṅgād agham āśu hanti tat
BhP pavitrakīrtiṃ tam alaṅghyaśāsanaṃ bhavān aho dveṣṭi śivaṃ śivetaraḥ
BhP yatpādapadmaṃ mahatāṃ mano'libhir niṣevitaṃ brahmarasāsavārthibhiḥ
BhP lokasya yad varṣati cāśiṣo 'rthinas tasmai bhavān druhyati viśvabandhave
BhP kiṃ vā śivākhyam aśivaṃ na vidus tvad anye brahmādayas tam avakīrya jaṭāḥ śmaśāne
BhP tanmālyabhasmanṛkapāly avasat piśācair ye mūrdhabhir dadhati taccaraṇāvasṛṣṭam
BhP karṇau pidhāya nirayād yad akalpa īśe dharmāvitary asṛṇibhir nṛbhir asyamāne
BhP chindyāt prasahya ruśatīm asatīṃ prabhuś cej jihvām asūn api tato visṛjet sa dharmaḥ
BhP atas tavotpannam idaṃ kalevaraṃ na dhārayiṣye śitikaṇṭhagarhiṇaḥ
BhP jagdhasya mohād dhi viśuddhim andhaso jugupsitasyoddharaṇaṃ pracakṣate
BhP na vedavādān anuvartate matiḥ sva eva loke ramato mahāmuneḥ
BhP yathā gatir devamanuṣyayoḥ pṛthak sva eva dharme na paraṃ kṣipet sthitaḥ
BhP karma pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttam apy ṛtaṃ vede vivicyobhayaliṅgam āśritam
BhP virodhi tad yaugapadaikakartari dvayaṃ tathā brahmaṇi karma narcchati
BhP mā vaḥ padavyaḥ pitar asmadāsthitā yā yajñaśālāsu na dhūmavartmabhiḥ
BhP tadannatṛptair asubhṛdbhir īḍitā avyaktaliṅgā avadhūtasevitāḥ
BhP naitena dehena hare kṛtāgaso dehodbhavenālam alaṃ kujanmanā
BhP vrīḍā mamābhūt kujanaprasaṅgatas taj janma dhig yo mahatām avadyakṛt
BhP gotraṃ tvadīyaṃ bhagavān vṛṣadhvajo dākṣāyaṇīty āha yadā sudurmanāḥ
BhP vyapetanarmasmitam āśu tadāhaṃ vyutsrakṣya etat kuṇapaṃ tvadaṅgajam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ity adhvare dakṣam anūdya śatruhan kṣitāv udīcīṃ niṣasāda śāntavāk
BhP spṛṣṭvā jalaṃ pītadukūlasaṃvṛtā nimīlya dṛg yogapathaṃ samāviśat
BhP kṛtvā samānāv anilau jitāsanā sodānam utthāpya ca nābhicakrataḥ
BhP śanair hṛdi sthāpya dhiyorasi sthitaṃ kaṇṭhād bhruvor madhyam aninditānayat
BhP evaṃ svadehaṃ mahatāṃ mahīyasā muhuḥ samāropitam aṅkam ādarāt
BhP jihāsatī dakṣaruṣā manasvinī dadhāra gātreṣv anilāgnidhāraṇām
BhP tataḥ svabhartuś caraṇāmbujāsavaṃ jagadguroś cintayatī na cāparam
BhP dadarśa deho hatakalmaṣaḥ satī sadyaḥ prajajvāla samādhijāgninā
BhP tat paśyatāṃ khe bhuvi cādbhutaṃ mahad hā heti vādaḥ sumahān ajāyata
BhP hanta priyā daivatamasya devī jahāv asūn kena satī prakopitā
BhP aho anātmyaṃ mahad asya paśyata prajāpater yasya carācaraṃ prajāḥ
BhP jahāv asūn yadvimatātmajā satī manasvinī mānam abhīkṣṇam arhati
BhP so 'yaṃ durmarṣahṛdayo brahmadhruk ca loke 'pakīrtiṃ mahatīm avāpsyati
BhP yadaṅgajāṃ svāṃ puruṣadviḍ udyatāṃ na pratyaṣedhan mṛtaye 'parādhataḥ
BhP vadaty evaṃ jane satyā dṛṣṭvāsutyāgam adbhutam
BhP dakṣaṃ tatpārṣadā hantum udatiṣṭhann udāyudhāḥ
BhP teṣām āpatatāṃ vegaṃ niśāmya bhagavān bhṛguḥ
BhP yajñaghnaghnena yajuṣā dakṣiṇāgnau juhāva ha
BhP adhvaryuṇā hūyamāne devā utpetur ojasā
BhP ṛbhavo nāma tapasā somaṃ prāptāḥ sahasraśaḥ
BhP tair alātāyudhaiḥ sarve pramathāḥ sahaguhyakāḥ
BhP hanyamānā diśo bhejur uśadbhir brahmatejasā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP bhavo bhavānyā nidhanaṃ prajāpater asatkṛtāyā avagamya nāradāt
BhP svapārṣadasainyaṃ ca tadadhvararbhubhir vidrāvitaṃ krodham apāram ādadhe
BhP kruddhaḥ sudaṣṭauṣṭhapuṭaḥ sa dhūrjaṭir jaṭāṃ taḍidvahnisaṭograrociṣam
BhP utkṛtya rudraḥ sahasotthito hasan gambhīranādo visasarja tāṃ bhuvi
BhP tato 'tikāyas tanuvā spṛśan divaṃ sahasrabāhur ghanaruk trisūryadṛk
BhP karāladaṃṣṭro jvaladagnimūrdhajaḥ kapālamālī vividhodyatāyudhaḥ
BhP taṃ kiṃ karomīti gṛṇantam āha baddhāñjaliṃ bhagavān bhūtanāthaḥ
BhP dakṣaṃ sayajñaṃ jahi madbhaṭānāṃ tvam agraṇī rudra bhaṭāṃśako me
BhP ājñapta evaṃ kupitena manyunā sa devadevaṃ paricakrame vibhum
BhP menetadātmānam asaṅgaraṃhasā mahīyasāṃ tāta sahaḥ sahiṣṇum
BhP anvīyamānaḥ sa tu rudrapārṣadair bhṛśaṃ nadadbhir vyanadat subhairavam
BhP udyamya śūlaṃ jagadantakāntakaṃ samprādravad ghoṣaṇabhūṣaṇāṅghriḥ
BhP athartvijo yajamānaḥ sadasyāḥ kakubhy udīcyāṃ prasamīkṣya reṇum
BhP tamaḥ kim etat kuta etad rajo 'bhūd iti dvijā dvijapatnyaś ca dadhyuḥ
BhP vātā na vānti na hi santi dasyavaḥ prācīnabarhir jīvati hogradaṇḍaḥ
BhP gāvo na kālyanta idaṃ kuto rajo loko 'dhunā kiṃ pralayāya kalpate
BhP prasūtimiśrāḥ striya udvignacittā ūcur vipāko vṛjinasyaiva tasya
BhP yat paśyantīnāṃ duhitṝṇāṃ prajeśaḥ sutāṃ satīm avadadhyāv anāgām
BhP yas tv antakāle vyuptajaṭākalāpaḥ svaśūlasūcyarpitadiggajendraḥ
BhP vitatya nṛtyaty uditāstradordhvajān uccāṭṭahāsastanayitnubhinnadik
BhP amarṣayitvā tam asahyatejasaṃ manyuplutaṃ durnirīkṣyaṃ bhrukuṭyā

BhP bahv evam udvignadṛśocyamāne janena dakṣasya muhur mahātmanaḥ
BhP utpetur utpātatamāḥ sahasraśo bhayāvahā divi bhūmau ca paryak
BhP tāvat sa rudrānucarair mahāmakho nānāyudhair vāmanakair udāyudhaiḥ
BhP piṅgaiḥ piśaṅgair makarodarānanaiḥ paryādravadbhir vidurānvarudhyata
BhP kecid babhañjuḥ prāgvaṃśaṃ patnīśālāṃ tathāpare
BhP sada āgnīdhraśālāṃ ca tadvihāraṃ mahānasam
BhP rurujur yajñapātrāṇi tathaike 'gnīn anāśayan
BhP kuṇḍeṣv amūtrayan kecid bibhidur vedimekhalāḥ
BhP abādhanta munīn anye eke patnīr atarjayan
BhP apare jagṛhur devān pratyāsannān palāyitān
BhP bhṛguṃ babandha maṇimān vīrabhadraḥ prajāpatim
BhP caṇḍeśaḥ pūṣaṇaṃ devaṃ bhagaṃ nandīśvaro 'grahīt
BhP sarva evartvijo dṛṣṭvā sadasyāḥ sadivaukasaḥ
BhP tair ardyamānāḥ subhṛśaṃ grāvabhir naikadhādravan
BhP juhvataḥ sruvahastasya śmaśrūṇi bhagavān bhavaḥ
BhP bhṛgor luluñce sadasi yo 'hasac chmaśru darśayan
BhP bhagasya netre bhagavān pātitasya ruṣā bhuvi
BhP ujjahāra sadastho 'kṣṇā yaḥ śapantam asūsucat
BhP pūṣṇo hy apātayad dantān kāliṅgasya yathā balaḥ
BhP śapyamāne garimaṇi yo 'hasad darśayan dataḥ
BhP ākramyorasi dakṣasya śitadhāreṇa hetinā
BhP chindann api tad uddhartuṃ nāśaknot tryambakas tadā
BhP śastrair astrānvitair evam anirbhinnatvacaṃ haraḥ
BhP vismayaṃ param āpanno dadhyau paśupatiś ciram
BhP dṛṣṭvā saṃjñapanaṃ yogaṃ paśūnāṃ sa patir makhe
BhP yajamānapaśoḥ kasya kāyāt tenāharac chiraḥ
BhP sādhuvādas tadā teṣāṃ karma tat tasya paśyatām
BhP bhūtapretapiśācānāṃ anyeṣāṃ tadviparyayaḥ
BhP juhāvaitac chiras tasmin dakṣiṇāgnāv amarṣitaḥ
BhP taddevayajanaṃ dagdhvā prātiṣṭhad guhyakālayam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP atha devagaṇāḥ sarve rudrānīkaiḥ parājitāḥ
BhP śūlapaṭṭiśanistriṃśa gadāparighamudgaraiḥ
BhP sañchinnabhinnasarvāṅgāḥ sartviksabhyā bhayākulāḥ
BhP svayambhuve namaskṛtya kārtsnyenaitan nyavedayan
BhP upalabhya puraivaitad bhagavān abjasambhavaḥ
BhP nārāyaṇaś ca viśvātmā na kasyādhvaram īyatuḥ
BhP tad ākarṇya vibhuḥ prāha tejīyasi kṛtāgasi
BhP kṣemāya tatra sā bhūyān na prāyeṇa bubhūṣatām
BhP athāpi yūyaṃ kṛtakilbiṣā bhavaṃ ye barhiṣo bhāgabhājaṃ parāduḥ
BhP prasādayadhvaṃ pariśuddhacetasā kṣipraprasādaṃ pragṛhītāṅghripadmam
BhP āśāsānā jīvitam adhvarasya lokaḥ sapālaḥ kupite na yasmin
BhP tam āśu devaṃ priyayā vihīnaṃ kṣamāpayadhvaṃ hṛdi viddhaṃ duruktaiḥ
BhP nāhaṃ na yajño na ca yūyam anye ye dehabhājo munayaś ca tattvam
BhP viduḥ pramāṇaṃ balavīryayor vā yasyātmatantrasya ka upāyaṃ vidhitset
BhP sa ittham ādiśya surān ajas tu taiḥ samanvitaḥ pitṛbhiḥ saprajeśaiḥ
BhP yayau svadhiṣṇyān nilayaṃ puradviṣaḥ kailāsam adripravaraṃ priyaṃ prabhoḥ

BhP juṣṭaṃ kinnaragandharvair apsarobhir vṛtaṃ sadā

BhP nānādrumalatāgulmair nānāmṛgagaṇāvṛtaiḥ

BhP āhvayantam ivoddhastair dvijān kāmadughair drumaiḥ

BhP mandāraiḥ pārijātaiś ca saralaiś copaśobhitam
BhP tamālaiḥ śālatālaiś ca kovidārāsanārjunaiḥ
BhP cūtaiḥ kadambair nīpaiś ca nāgapunnāgacampakaiḥ
BhP pāṭalāśokabakulaiḥ kundaiḥ kurabakair api

BhP kubjakair mallikābhiś ca mādhavībhiś ca maṇḍitam
BhP panasodumbarāśvattha plakṣanyagrodhahiṅgubhiḥ
BhP bhūrjair oṣadhibhiḥ pūgai rājapūgaiś ca jambubhiḥ
BhP kharjūrāmrātakāmrādyaiḥ priyālamadhukeṅgudaiḥ
BhP drumajātibhir anyaiś ca rājitaṃ veṇukīcakaiḥ
BhP kumudotpalakahlāra śatapatravanarddhibhiḥ
BhP nalinīṣu kalaṃ kūjat khagavṛndopaśobhitam
BhP mṛgaiḥ śākhāmṛgaiḥ kroḍair mṛgendrair ṛkṣaśalyakaiḥ
BhP gavayaiḥ śarabhair vyāghrai rurubhir mahiṣādibhiḥ
BhP karṇāntraikapadāśvāsyair nirjuṣṭaṃ vṛkanābhibhiḥ
BhP kadalīkhaṇḍasaṃruddha nalinīpulinaśriyam
BhP paryastaṃ nandayā satyāḥ snānapuṇyatarodayā
BhP vilokya bhūteśagiriṃ vibudhā vismayaṃ yayuḥ
BhP dadṛśus tatra te ramyām alakāṃ nāma vai purīm
BhP vanaṃ saugandhikaṃ cāpi yatra tannāma paṅkajam
BhP nandā cālakanandā ca saritau bāhyataḥ puraḥ
BhP tīrthapādapadāmbhoja rajasātīva pāvane
BhP yayoḥ surastriyaḥ kṣattar avaruhya svadhiṣṇyataḥ
BhP krīḍanti puṃsaḥ siñcantyo vigāhya ratikarśitāḥ
BhP yayos tatsnānavibhraṣṭa navakuṅkumapiñjaram
BhP vitṛṣo 'pi pibanty ambhaḥ pāyayanto gajā gajīḥ
BhP tārahemamahāratna vimānaśatasaṅkulām
