BhP hitvā yakṣeśvarapurīṃ vanaṃ saugandhikaṃ ca tat
BhP drumaiḥ kāmadughair hṛdyaṃ citramālyaphalacchadaiḥ
BhP raktakaṇṭhakhagānīka svaramaṇḍitaṣaṭpadam
BhP kalahaṃsakulapreṣṭhaṃ kharadaṇḍajalāśayam
BhP vanakuñjarasaṅghṛṣṭa haricandanavāyunā
BhP adhi puṇyajanastrīṇāṃ muhur unmathayan manaḥ
BhP vaidūryakṛtasopānā vāpya utpalamālinīḥ
BhP prāptaṃ kimpuruṣair dṛṣṭvā ta ārād dadṛśur vaṭam
BhP sa yojanaśatotsedhaḥ pādonaviṭapāyataḥ
BhP paryakkṛtācalacchāyo nirnīḍas tāpavarjitaḥ
BhP tasmin mahāyogamaye mumukṣuśaraṇe surāḥ
BhP dadṛśuḥ śivam āsīnaṃ tyaktāmarṣam ivāntakam
BhP sanandanādyair mahāsiddhaiḥ śāntaiḥ saṃśāntavigraham
BhP upāsyamānaṃ sakhyā ca bhartrā guhyakarakṣasām
BhP vidyātapoyogapatham āsthitaṃ tam adhīśvaram
BhP carantaṃ viśvasuhṛdaṃ vātsalyāl lokamaṅgalam
BhP liṅgaṃ ca tāpasābhīṣṭaṃ bhasmadaṇḍajaṭājinam
BhP aṅgena sandhyābhrarucā candralekhāṃ ca bibhratam
BhP upaviṣṭaṃ darbhamayyāṃ bṛsyāṃ brahma sanātanam
BhP nāradāya pravocantaṃ pṛcchate śṛṇvatāṃ satām
BhP kṛtvorau dakṣiṇe savyaṃ pādapadmaṃ ca jānuni
BhP bāhuṃ prakoṣṭhe 'kṣamālām āsīnaṃ tarkamudrayā
BhP taṃ brahmanirvāṇasamādhim āśritaṃ vyupāśritaṃ giriśaṃ yogakakṣām
BhP salokapālā munayo manūnām ādyaṃ manuṃ prāñjalayaḥ praṇemuḥ
BhP sa tūpalabhyāgatam ātmayoniṃ surāsureśair abhivanditāṅghriḥ
BhP utthāya cakre śirasābhivandanam arhattamaḥ kasya yathaiva viṣṇuḥ
BhP tathāpare siddhagaṇā maharṣibhir ye vai samantād anu nīlalohitam
BhP namaskṛtaḥ prāha śaśāṅkaśekharaṃ kṛtapraṇāmaṃ prahasann ivātmabhūḥ
BhP brahmovāca
BhP āne tvām īśaṃ viśvasya jagato yonibījayoḥ
BhP śakteḥ śivasya ca paraṃ yat tad brahmā nirantaram
BhP tvam eva bhagavann etac chivaśaktyoḥ svarūpayoḥ
BhP viśvaṃ sṛjasi pāsy atsi krīḍann ūrṇapaṭo yathā
BhP tvam eva dharmārthadughābhipattaye dakṣeṇa sūtreṇa sasarjithādhvaram
BhP tvayaiva loke 'vasitāś ca setavo yān brāhmaṇāḥ śraddadhate dhṛtavratāḥ
BhP tvaṃ karmaṇāṃ maṅgala maṅgalānāṃ kartuḥ svalokaṃ tanuṣe svaḥ paraṃ vā
BhP amaṅgalānāṃ ca tamisram ulbaṇaṃ viparyayaḥ kena tad eva kasyacit
BhP na vai satāṃ tvaccaraṇārpitātmanāṃ bhūteṣu sarveṣv abhipaśyatāṃ tava
BhP bhūtāni cātmany apṛthagdidṛkṣatāṃ prāyeṇa roṣo 'bhibhaved yathā paśum
BhP pṛthagdhiyaḥ karmadṛśo durāśayāḥ parodayenārpitahṛdrujo 'niśam
BhP parān duruktair vitudanty aruntudās tān māvadhīd daivavadhān bhavadvidhaḥ
BhP yasmin yadā puṣkaranābhamāyayā durantayā spṛṣṭadhiyaḥ pṛthagdṛśaḥ
BhP kurvanti tatra hy anukampayā kṛpāṃ na sādhavo daivabalāt kṛte kramam
BhP bhavāṃs tu puṃsaḥ paramasya māyayā durantayāspṛṣṭamatiḥ samastadṛk
BhP tayā hatātmasv anukarmacetaḥsv anugrahaṃ kartum ihārhasi prabho
BhP kurv adhvarasyoddharaṇaṃ hatasya bhoḥ tvayāsamāptasya mano prajāpateḥ
BhP na yatra bhāgaṃ tava bhāgino daduḥ kuyājino yena makho ninīyate
BhP jīvatād yajamāno 'yaṃ prapadyetākṣiṇī bhagaḥ
BhP bhṛgoḥ śmaśrūṇi rohantu pūṣṇo dantāś ca pūrvavat
BhP devānāṃ bhagnagātrāṇām ṛtvijāṃ cāyudhāśmabhiḥ
BhP bhavatānugṛhītānām āśu manyo 'stv anāturam
BhP eṣa te rudra bhāgo 'stu yaducchiṣṭo 'dhvarasya vai
BhP yajñas te rudra bhāgena kalpatām adya yajñahan
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ity ajenānunītena bhavena parituṣyatā
BhP abhyadhāyi mahābāho prahasya śrūyatām iti
BhP mahādeva uvāca
BhP nāghaṃ prajeśa bālānāṃ varṇaye nānucintaye
BhP devamāyābhibhūtānāṃ daṇḍas tatra dhṛto mayā
BhP prajāpater dagdhaśīrṣṇo bhavatv ajamukhaṃ śiraḥ
BhP mitrasya cakṣuṣekṣeta bhāgaṃ svaṃ barhiṣo bhagaḥ
BhP pūṣā tu yajamānasya dadbhir jakṣatu piṣṭabhuk
BhP devāḥ prakṛtasarvāṅgā ye ma uccheṣaṇaṃ daduḥ
BhP bāhubhyām aśvinoḥ pūṣṇo hastābhyāṃ kṛtabāhavaḥ
BhP bhavantv adhvaryavaś cānye bastaśmaśrur bhṛgur bhavet
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP tadā sarvāṇi bhūtāni śrutvā mīḍhuṣṭamoditam
BhP parituṣṭātmabhis tāta sādhu sādhv ity athābruvan
BhP tato mīḍhvāṃsam āmantrya śunāsīrāḥ saharṣibhiḥ
BhP bhūyas tad devayajanaṃ samīḍhvadvedhaso yayuḥ
BhP vidhāya kārtsnyena ca tad yad āha bhagavān bhavaḥ
BhP sandadhuḥ kasya kāyena savanīyapaśoḥ śiraḥ
BhP sandhīyamāne śirasi dakṣo rudrābhivīkṣitaḥ
BhP sadyaḥ supta ivottasthau dadṛśe cāgrato mṛḍam
BhP tadā vṛṣadhvajadveṣa kalilātmā prajāpatiḥ
BhP śivāvalokād abhavac charaddhrada ivāmalaḥ
BhP bhavastavāya kṛtadhīr nāśaknod anurāgataḥ
BhP autkaṇṭhyād bāṣpakalayā samparetāṃ sutāṃ smaran
BhP kṛcchrāt saṃstabhya ca manaḥ premavihvalitaḥ sudhīḥ
BhP śaśaṃsa nirvyalīkena bhāveneśaṃ prajāpatiḥ
BhP dakṣa uvāca
BhP bhūyān anugraha aho bhavatā kṛto me
BhP daṇḍas tvayā mayi bhṛto yad api pralabdhaḥ
BhP na brahmabandhuṣu ca vāṃ bhagavann avajñā
BhP tubhyaṃ hareś ca kuta eva dhṛtavrateṣu
BhP vidyātapovratadharān mukhataḥ sma viprān
BhP brahmātmatattvam avituṃ prathamaṃ tvam asrāk
BhP tad brāhmaṇān parama sarvavipatsu pāsi
BhP pālaḥ paśūn iva vibho pragṛhītadaṇḍaḥ
BhP yo 'sau mayāviditatattvadṛśā sabhāyāṃ
BhP kṣipto duruktiviśikhair vigaṇayya tan mām
BhP arvāk patantam arhattamanindayāpād
BhP dṛṣṭyārdrayā sa bhagavān svakṛtena tuṣyet
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP kṣamāpyaivaṃ sa mīḍhvāṃsaṃ brahmaṇā cānumantritaḥ
BhP karma santānayām āsa sopādhyāyartvigādibhiḥ
BhP vaiṣṇavaṃ yajñasantatyai trikapālaṃ dvijottamāḥ
BhP puroḍāśaṃ niravapan vīrasaṃsargaśuddhaye
BhP adhvaryuṇāttahaviṣā yajamāno viśāmpate
BhP dhiyā viśuddhayā dadhyau tathā prādurabhūd dhariḥ
BhP tadā svaprabhayā teṣāṃ dyotayantyā diśo daśa
BhP muṣṇaṃs teja upānītas tārkṣyeṇa stotravājinā
BhP śyāmo hiraṇyaraśano 'rkakirīṭajuṣṭo
BhP nīlālakabhramaramaṇḍitakuṇḍalāsyaḥ
BhP śaṅkhābjacakraśaracāpagadāsicarma
BhP vyagrair hiraṇmayabhujair iva karṇikāraḥ
BhP vakṣasy adhiśritavadhūr vanamāly udāra
BhP hāsāvalokakalayā ramayaṃś ca viśvam
BhP pārśvabhramadvyajanacāmararājahaṃsaḥ
BhP śvetātapatraśaśinopari rajyamānaḥ
BhP tam upāgatam ālakṣya sarve suragaṇādayaḥ
BhP praṇemuḥ sahasotthāya brahmendratryakṣanāyakāḥ
BhP tattejasā hatarucaḥ sannajihvāḥ sasādhvasāḥ
BhP mūrdhnā dhṛtāñjalipuṭā upatasthur adhokṣajam
BhP apy arvāgvṛttayo yasya mahi tv ātmabhuvādayaḥ
BhP yathāmati gṛṇanti sma kṛtānugrahavigraham
BhP dakṣo gṛhītārhaṇasādanottamaṃ
BhP yajñeśvaraṃ viśvasṛjāṃ paraṃ gurum
BhP sunandanandādyanugair vṛtaṃ mudā
BhP gṛṇan prapede prayataḥ kṛtāñjaliḥ
BhP dakṣa uvāca
BhP śuddhaṃ svadhāmny uparatākhilabuddhyavasthaṃ
BhP cinmātram ekam abhayaṃ pratiṣidhya māyām
BhP tiṣṭhaṃs tayaiva puruṣatvam upetya tasyām
BhP āste bhavān apariśuddha ivātmatantraḥ
BhP ṛtvija ūcuḥ
BhP tattvaṃ na te vayam anañjana rudraśāpāt
BhP karmaṇy avagrahadhiyo bhagavan vidāmaḥ
BhP dharmopalakṣaṇam idaṃ trivṛd adhvarākhyaṃ
BhP jñātaṃ yadartham adhidaivam ado vyavasthāḥ
BhP sadasyā ūcuḥ
BhP utpattyadhvany aśaraṇa urukleśadurge 'ntakogra
BhP vyālānviṣṭe viṣayamṛgatṛṣy ātmagehorubhāraḥ
BhP dvandvaśvabhre khalamṛgabhaye śokadāve 'jñasārthaḥ
BhP pādaukas te śaraṇada kadā yāti kāmopasṛṣṭaḥ
BhP rudra uvāca
BhP tava varada varāṅghrāv āśiṣehākhilārthe
BhP hy api munibhir asaktair ādareṇārhaṇīye
BhP yadi racitadhiyaṃ māvidyaloko 'paviddhaṃ
BhP japati na gaṇaye tat tvatparānugraheṇa
BhP bhṛgur uvāca
BhP yan māyayā gahanayāpahṛtātmabodhā
BhP brahmādayas tanubhṛtas tamasi svapantaḥ
BhP nātmanśritaṃ tava vidanty adhunāpi tattvaṃ
BhP so 'yaṃ prasīdatu bhavān praṇatātmabandhuḥ
BhP brahmovāca
BhP naitat svarūpaṃ bhavato 'sau padārtha bhedagrahaiḥ puruṣo yāvad īkṣet
BhP jñānasya cārthasya guṇasya cāśrayo māyāmayād vyatirikto matas tvam
BhP indra uvāca
BhP idam apy acyuta viśvabhāvanaṃ vapur ānandakaraṃ manodṛśām
BhP suravidviṭkṣapaṇair udāyudhair bhujadaṇḍair upapannam aṣṭabhiḥ
BhP patnya ūcuḥ
BhP yajño 'yaṃ tava yajanāya kena sṛṣṭo vidhvastaḥ paśupatinādya dakṣakopāt
BhP taṃ nas tvaṃ śavaśayanābhaśāntamedhaṃ yajñātman nalinarucā dṛśā punīhi
BhP ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
BhP ananvitaṃ te bhagavan viceṣṭitaṃ yad ātmanā carasi hi karma nājyase
BhP vibhūtaye yata upasedur īśvarīṃ na manyate svayam anuvartatīṃ bhavān
BhP siddhā ūcuḥ
BhP ayaṃ tvatkathāmṛṣṭapīyūṣanadyāṃ manovāraṇaḥ kleśadāvāgnidagdhaḥ
BhP tṛṣārto 'vagāḍho na sasmāra dāvaṃ na niṣkrāmati brahmasampannavan naḥ
BhP yajamāny uvāca
BhP svāgataṃ te prasīdeśa tubhyaṃ namaḥ śrīnivāsa śriyā kāntayā trāhi naḥ
BhP tvām ṛte 'dhīśa nāṅgair makhaḥ śobhate śīrṣahīnaḥ kabandho yathā puruṣaḥ
BhP lokapālā ūcuḥ
BhP dṛṣṭaḥ kiṃ no dṛgbhir asadgrahais tvaṃ pratyagdraṣṭā dṛśyate yena viśvam
BhP māyā hy eṣā bhavadīyā hi bhūman yas tvaṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ pañcabhir bhāsi bhūtaiḥ
BhP yogeśvarā ūcuḥ
BhP preyān na te 'nyo 'sty amutas tvayi prabho viśvātmanīkṣen na pṛthag ya ātmanaḥ
BhP athāpi bhaktyeśa tayopadhāvatām ananyavṛttyānugṛhāṇa vatsala
BhP jagadudbhavasthitilayeṣu daivato bahubhidyamānaguṇayātmamāyayā
BhP racitātmabhedamataye svasaṃsthayā vinivartitabhramaguṇātmane namaḥ
BhP brahmovāca
BhP namas te śritasattvāya dharmādīnāṃ ca sūtaye
BhP nirguṇāya ca yatkāṣṭhāṃ nāhaṃ vedāpare 'pi ca
BhP agnir uvāca
BhP yattejasāhaṃ susamiddhatejā havyaṃ vahe svadhvara ājyasiktam
BhP taṃ yajñiyaṃ pañcavidhaṃ ca pañcabhiḥ sviṣṭaṃ yajurbhiḥ praṇato 'smi yajñam
BhP devā ūcuḥ
BhP purā kalpāpāye svakṛtam udarīkṛtya vikṛtaṃ
BhP tvam evādyas tasmin salila uragendrādhiśayane
BhP pumān śeṣe siddhair hṛdi vimṛśitādhyātmapadaviḥ
BhP sa evādyākṣṇor yaḥ pathi carasi bhṛtyān avasi naḥ
BhP gandharvā ūcuḥ
BhP aṃśāṃśās te deva marīcyādaya ete brahmendrādyā devagaṇā rudrapurogāḥ
BhP krīḍābhāṇḍaṃ viśvam idaṃ yasya vibhūman tasmai nityaṃ nātha namas te karavāma
BhP vidyādharā ūcuḥ
BhP tvanmāyayārtham abhipadya kalevare 'smin
BhP kṛtvā mamāham iti durmatir utpathaiḥ svaiḥ
BhP kṣipto 'py asadviṣayalālasa ātmamohaṃ
BhP yuṣmatkathāmṛtaniṣevaka udvyudasyet
BhP brāhmaṇā ūcuḥ
BhP tvaṃ kratus tvaṃ havis tvaṃ hutāśaḥ svayaṃ tvaṃ hi mantraḥ samiddarbhapātrāṇi ca
BhP tvaṃ sadasyartvijo dampatī devatā agnihotraṃ svadhā soma ājyaṃ paśuḥ
BhP tvaṃ purā gāṃ rasāyā mahāsūkaro daṃṣṭrayā padminīṃ vāraṇendro yathā
BhP stūyamāno nadal līlayā yogibhir vyujjahartha trayīgātra yajñakratuḥ
BhP sa prasīda tvam asmākam ākāṅkṣatāṃ darśanaṃ te paribhraṣṭasatkarmaṇām
BhP kīrtyamāne nṛbhir nāmni yajñeśa te yajñavighnāḥ kṣayaṃ yānti tasmai namaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti dakṣaḥ kavir yajñaṃ bhadra rudrābhimarśitam
BhP kīrtyamāne hṛṣīkeśe sanninye yajñabhāvane
BhP bhagavān svena bhāgena sarvātmā sarvabhāgabhuk
BhP dakṣaṃ babhāṣa ābhāṣya prīyamāṇa ivānagha
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP ahaṃ brahmā ca śarvaś ca jagataḥ kāraṇaṃ param
BhP ātmeśvara upadraṣṭā svayandṛg aviśeṣaṇaḥ
BhP ātmamāyāṃ samāviśya so 'haṃ guṇamayīṃ dvija
BhP sṛjan rakṣan haran viśvaṃ dadhre saṃjñāṃ kriyocitām
BhP tasmin brahmaṇy advitīye kevale paramātmani
BhP brahmarudrau ca bhūtāni bhedenājño 'nupaśyati
BhP yathā pumān na svāṅgeṣu śiraḥpāṇyādiṣu kvacit
BhP pārakyabuddhiṃ kurute evaṃ bhūteṣu matparaḥ
BhP trayāṇām ekabhāvānāṃ yo na paśyati vai bhidām
BhP sarvabhūtātmanāṃ brahman sa śāntim adhigacchati
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ bhagavatādiṣṭaḥ prajāpatipatir harim
BhP arcitvā kratunā svena devān ubhayato 'yajat
BhP rudraṃ ca svena bhāgena hy upādhāvat samāhitaḥ
BhP karmaṇodavasānena somapān itarān api
BhP udavasya sahartvigbhiḥ sasnāv avabhṛthaṃ tataḥ
BhP tasmā apy anubhāvena svenaivāvāptarādhase
BhP dharma eva matiṃ dattvā tridaśās te divaṃ yayuḥ
BhP evaṃ dākṣāyaṇī hitvā satī pūrvakalevaram
BhP jajñe himavataḥ kṣetre menāyām iti śuśruma
BhP tam eva dayitaṃ bhūya āvṛṅkte patim ambikā
BhP ananyabhāvaikagatiṃ śaktiḥ supteva pūruṣam
BhP etad bhagavataḥ śambhoḥ karma dakṣādhvaradruhaḥ
BhP śrutaṃ bhāgavatāc chiṣyād uddhavān me bṛhaspateḥ
BhP idaṃ pavitraṃ param īśaceṣṭitaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyam aghaughamarṣaṇam
BhP yo nityadākarṇya naro 'nukīrtayed dhunoty aghaṃ kaurava bhaktibhāvataḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sanakādyā nāradaś ca ṛbhur haṃso 'ruṇir yatiḥ
BhP naite gṛhān brahmasutā hy āvasann ūrdhvaretasaḥ
BhP mṛṣādharmasya bhāryāsīd dambhaṃ māyāṃ ca śatruhan
BhP asūta mithunaṃ tat tu nirṛtir jagṛhe 'prajaḥ
BhP tayoḥ samabhaval lobho nikṛtiś ca mahāmate
BhP tābhyāṃ krodhaś ca hiṃsā ca yad duruktiḥ svasā kaliḥ
BhP duruktau kalir ādhatta bhayaṃ mṛtyuṃ ca sattama
BhP tayoś ca mithunaṃ jajñe yātanā nirayas tathā
BhP saṅgraheṇa mayākhyātaḥ pratisargas tavānagha
BhP triḥ śrutvaitat pumān puṇyaṃ vidhunoty ātmano malam
BhP athātaḥ kīrtaye vaṃśaṃ puṇyakīrteḥ kurūdvaha
BhP svāyambhuvasyāpi manor harer aṃśāṃśajanmanaḥ
BhP priyavratottānapādau śatarūpāpateḥ sutau
BhP vāsudevasya kalayā rakṣāyāṃ jagataḥ sthitau
BhP jāye uttānapādasya sunītiḥ surucis tayoḥ
BhP suruciḥ preyasī patyur netarā yatsuto dhruvaḥ
BhP ekadā suruceḥ putram aṅkam āropya lālayan
BhP uttamaṃ nārurukṣantaṃ dhruvaṃ rājābhyanandata
BhP tathā cikīrṣamāṇaṃ taṃ sapatnyās tanayaṃ dhruvam
BhP suruciḥ śṛṇvato rājñaḥ serṣyam āhātigarvitā
BhP na vatsa nṛpater dhiṣṇyaṃ bhavān āroḍhum arhati
BhP na gṛhīto mayā yat tvaṃ kukṣāv api nṛpātmajaḥ
BhP bālo 'si bata nātmānam anyastrīgarbhasambhṛtam
BhP nūnaṃ veda bhavān yasya durlabhe 'rthe manorathaḥ
BhP tapasārādhya puruṣaṃ tasyaivānugraheṇa me
BhP garbhe tvaṃ sādhayātmānaṃ yadīcchasi nṛpāsanam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP mātuḥ sapatnyāḥ sa duruktividdhaḥ śvasan ruṣā daṇḍahato yathāhiḥ
BhP hitvā miṣantaṃ pitaraṃ sannavācaṃ jagāma mātuḥ prarudan sakāśam
BhP taṃ niḥśvasantaṃ sphuritādharoṣṭhaṃ sunītir utsaṅga udūhya bālam
BhP niśamya tatpauramukhān nitāntaṃ sā vivyathe yad gaditaṃ sapatnyā
BhP sotsṛjya dhairyaṃ vilalāpa śoka dāvāgninā dāvalateva bālā
BhP vākyaṃ sapatnyāḥ smaratī saroja śriyā dṛśā bāṣpakalām uvāha
BhP dīrghaṃ śvasantī vṛjinasya pāram apaśyatī bālakam āha bālā
BhP māmaṅgalaṃ tāta pareṣu maṃsthā bhuṅkte jano yat paraduḥkhadas tat
BhP satyaṃ surucyābhihitaṃ bhavān me yad durbhagāyā udare gṛhītaḥ
BhP stanyena vṛddhaś ca vilajjate yāṃ bhāryeti vā voḍhum iḍaspatir mām
BhP ātiṣṭha tat tāta vimatsaras tvam uktaṃ samātrāpi yad avyalīkam
BhP ārādhayādhokṣajapādapadmaṃ yadīcchase 'dhyāsanam uttamo yathā
BhP yasyāṅghripadmaṃ paricarya viśva vibhāvanāyāttaguṇābhipatteḥ
BhP ajo 'dhyatiṣṭhat khalu pārameṣṭhyaṃ padaṃ jitātmaśvasanābhivandyam
BhP tathā manur vo bhagavān pitāmaho yam ekamatyā purudakṣiṇair makhaiḥ
BhP iṣṭvābhipede duravāpam anyato bhaumaṃ sukhaṃ divyam athāpavargyam
BhP tam eva vatsāśraya bhṛtyavatsalaṃ mumukṣubhir mṛgyapadābjapaddhatim
BhP ananyabhāve nijadharmabhāvite manasy avasthāpya bhajasva pūruṣam
BhP nānyaṃ tataḥ padmapalāśalocanād duḥkhacchidaṃ te mṛgayāmi kañcana
BhP yo mṛgyate hastagṛhītapadmayā śriyetarair aṅga vimṛgyamāṇayā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ sañjalpitaṃ mātur ākarṇyārthāgamaṃ vacaḥ
BhP sanniyamyātmanātmānaṃ niścakrāma pituḥ purāt
BhP nāradas tad upākarṇya jñātvā tasya cikīrṣitam
BhP spṛṣṭvā mūrdhany aghaghnena pāṇinā prāha vismitaḥ
BhP aho tejaḥ kṣatriyāṇāṃ mānabhaṅgam amṛṣyatām
BhP bālo 'py ayaṃ hṛdā dhatte yat samātur asadvacaḥ
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP nādhunāpy avamānaṃ te sammānaṃ vāpi putraka
BhP lakṣayāmaḥ kumārasya saktasya krīḍanādiṣu
BhP vikalpe vidyamāne 'pi na hy asantoṣahetavaḥ
BhP puṃso moham ṛte bhinnā yal loke nijakarmabhiḥ
BhP parituṣyet tatas tāta tāvanmātreṇa pūruṣaḥ
BhP daivopasāditaṃ yāvad vīkṣyeśvaragatiṃ budhaḥ
BhP atha mātropadiṣṭena yogenāvarurutsasi
BhP yatprasādaṃ sa vai puṃsāṃ durārādhyo mato mama
BhP munayaḥ padavīṃ yasya niḥsaṅgenorujanmabhiḥ
BhP na vidur mṛgayanto 'pi tīvrayogasamādhinā
BhP ato nivartatām eṣa nirbandhas tava niṣphalaḥ
BhP yatiṣyati bhavān kāle śreyasāṃ samupasthite
BhP yasya yad daivavihitaṃ sa tena sukhaduḥkhayoḥ
BhP ātmānaṃ toṣayan dehī tamasaḥ pāram ṛcchati
BhP guṇādhikān mudaṃ lipsed anukrośaṃ guṇādhamāt
BhP maitrīṃ samānād anvicchen na tāpair abhibhūyate
BhP dhruva uvāca
BhP so 'yaṃ śamo bhagavatā sukhaduḥkhahatātmanām
BhP darśitaḥ kṛpayā puṃsāṃ durdarśo 'smadvidhais tu yaḥ
BhP athāpi me 'vinītasya kṣāttraṃ ghoram upeyuṣaḥ
BhP surucyā durvacobāṇair na bhinne śrayate hṛdi
BhP padaṃ tribhuvanotkṛṣṭaṃ jigīṣoḥ sādhu vartma me
BhP brūhy asmatpitṛbhir brahmann anyair apy anadhiṣṭhitam
BhP nūnaṃ bhavān bhagavato yo 'ṅgajaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ
BhP vitudann aṭate vīṇāṃ hitāya jagato 'rkavat
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ity udāhṛtam ākarṇya bhagavān nāradas tadā
BhP prītaḥ pratyāha taṃ bālaṃ sadvākyam anukampayā
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP jananyābhihitaḥ panthāḥ sa vai niḥśreyasasya te
BhP bhagavān vāsudevas taṃ bhaja taṃ pravaṇātmanā
BhP dharmārthakāmamokṣākhyaṃ ya icchec chreya ātmanaḥ
BhP ekaṃ hy eva hares tatra kāraṇaṃ pādasevanam
BhP tat tāta gaccha bhadraṃ te yamunāyās taṭaṃ śuci
BhP puṇyaṃ madhuvanaṃ yatra sānnidhyaṃ nityadā hareḥ
BhP snātvānusavanaṃ tasmin kālindyāḥ salile śive
BhP kṛtvocitāni nivasann ātmanaḥ kalpitāsanaḥ
BhP prāṇāyāmena trivṛtā prāṇendriyamanomalam
BhP śanair vyudasyābhidhyāyen manasā guruṇā gurum
BhP prasādābhimukhaṃ śaśvat prasannavadanekṣaṇam
BhP sunāsaṃ subhruvaṃ cāru kapolaṃ surasundaram
BhP taruṇaṃ ramaṇīyāṅgam aruṇoṣṭhekṣaṇādharam
BhP praṇatāśrayaṇaṃ nṛmṇaṃ śaraṇyaṃ karuṇārṇavam
BhP śrīvatsāṅkaṃ ghanaśyāmaṃ puruṣaṃ vanamālinam
BhP śaṅkhacakragadāpadmair abhivyaktacaturbhujam
BhP kirīṭinaṃ kuṇḍalinaṃ keyūravalayānvitam
BhP kaustubhābharaṇagrīvaṃ pītakauśeyavāsasam
BhP kāñcīkalāpaparyastaṃ lasatkāñcananūpuram
BhP darśanīyatamaṃ śāntaṃ manonayanavardhanam
BhP padbhyāṃ nakhamaṇiśreṇyā vilasadbhyāṃ samarcatām
BhP hṛtpadmakarṇikādhiṣṇyam ākramyātmany avasthitam
BhP smayamānam abhidhyāyet sānurāgāvalokanam
BhP niyatenaikabhūtena manasā varadarṣabham
BhP evaṃ bhagavato rūpaṃ subhadraṃ dhyāyato manaḥ
BhP nirvṛtyā parayā tūrṇaṃ sampannaṃ na nivartate
BhP japaś ca paramo guhyaḥ śrūyatāṃ me nṛpātmaja
BhP yaṃ saptarātraṃ prapaṭhan pumān paśyati khecarān
BhP oṃ namo bhagavate vāsudevāya
BhP mantreṇānena devasya kuryād dravyamayīṃ budhaḥ
BhP saparyāṃ vividhair dravyair deśakālavibhāgavit
BhP salilaiḥ śucibhir mālyair vanyair mūlaphalādibhiḥ
BhP śastāṅkurāṃśukaiś cārcet tulasyā priyayā prabhum
BhP labdhvā dravyamayīm arcāṃ kṣityambvādiṣu vārcayet
BhP ābhṛtātmā muniḥ śānto yatavāṅ mitavanyabhuk
BhP svecchāvatāracaritair acintyanijamāyayā
BhP kariṣyaty uttamaślokas tad dhyāyed dhṛdayaṅgamam
BhP paricaryā bhagavato yāvatyaḥ pūrvasevitāḥ
BhP tā mantrahṛdayenaiva prayuñjyān mantramūrtaye
BhP evaṃ kāyena manasā vacasā ca manogatam
BhP paricaryamāṇo bhagavān bhaktimatparicaryayā
BhP puṃsām amāyināṃ samyag bhajatāṃ bhāvavardhanaḥ
BhP śreyo diśaty abhimataṃ yad dharmādiṣu dehinām
BhP viraktaś cendriyaratau bhaktiyogena bhūyasā
BhP taṃ nirantarabhāvena bhajetāddhā vimuktaye
BhP ity uktas taṃ parikramya praṇamya ca nṛpārbhakaḥ
BhP yayau madhuvanaṃ puṇyaṃ hareś caraṇacarcitam
BhP tapovanaṃ gate tasmin praviṣṭo 'ntaḥpuraṃ muniḥ
BhP arhitārhaṇako rājñā sukhāsīna uvāca tam
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP rājan kiṃ dhyāyase dīrghaṃ mukhena pariśuṣyatā
BhP kiṃ vā na riṣyate kāmo dharmo vārthena saṃyutaḥ
BhP rājovāca
BhP suto me bālako brahman straiṇenākaruṇātmanā
BhP nirvāsitaḥ pañcavarṣaḥ saha mātrā mahān kaviḥ
BhP apy anāthaṃ vane brahman mā smādanty arbhakaṃ vṛkāḥ
BhP śrāntaṃ śayānaṃ kṣudhitaṃ parimlānamukhāmbujam
BhP aho me bata daurātmyaṃ strījitasyopadhāraya
BhP yo 'ṅkaṃ premṇārurukṣantaṃ nābhyanandam asattamaḥ
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP mā mā śucaḥ svatanayaṃ devaguptaṃ viśāmpate
BhP tatprabhāvam avijñāya prāvṛṅkte yadyaśo jagat
BhP suduṣkaraṃ karma kṛtvā lokapālair api prabhuḥ
BhP aiṣyaty acirato rājan yaśo vipulayaṃs tava
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti devarṣiṇā proktaṃ viśrutya jagatīpatiḥ
BhP rājalakṣmīm anādṛtya putram evānvacintayat
BhP tatrābhiṣiktaḥ prayatas tām upoṣya vibhāvarīm
BhP samāhitaḥ paryacarad ṛṣyādeśena pūruṣam
BhP trirātrānte trirātrānte kapitthabadarāśanaḥ
BhP ātmavṛttyanusāreṇa māsaṃ ninye 'rcayan harim
BhP dvitīyaṃ ca tathā māsaṃ ṣaṣṭhe ṣaṣṭhe 'rbhako dine
BhP tṛṇaparṇādibhiḥ śīrṇaiḥ kṛtānno 'bhyarcayan vibhum
BhP tṛtīyaṃ cānayan māsaṃ navame navame 'hani
BhP abbhakṣa uttamaślokam upādhāvat samādhinā
BhP caturtham api vai māsaṃ dvādaśe dvādaśe 'hani
BhP vāyubhakṣo jitaśvāso dhyāyan devam adhārayat
BhP pañcame māsy anuprāpte jitaśvāso nṛpātmajaḥ
BhP dhyāyan brahma padaikena tasthau sthāṇur ivācalaḥ
BhP sarvato mana ākṛṣya hṛdi bhūtendriyāśayam
BhP dhyāyan bhagavato rūpaṃ nādrākṣīt kiñcanāparam
BhP ādhāraṃ mahadādīnāṃ pradhānapuruṣeśvaram
BhP brahma dhārayamāṇasya trayo lokāś cakampire
BhP yadaikapādena sa pārthivārbhakas tasthau tadaṅguṣṭhanipīḍitā mahī
BhP nanāma tatrārdham ibhendradhiṣṭhitā tarīva savyetarataḥ pade pade
BhP tasminn abhidhyāyati viśvam ātmano dvāraṃ nirudhyāsum ananyayā dhiyā
BhP lokā nirucchvāsanipīḍitā bhṛśaṃ salokapālāḥ śaraṇaṃ yayur harim
BhP devā ūcuḥ
BhP naivaṃ vidāmo bhagavan prāṇarodhaṃ carācarasyākhilasattvadhāmnaḥ
BhP vidhehi tan no vṛjinād vimokṣaṃ prāptā vayaṃ tvāṃ śaraṇaṃ śaraṇyam
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP mā bhaiṣṭa bālaṃ tapaso duratyayān nivartayiṣye pratiyāta svadhāma
BhP yato hi vaḥ prāṇanirodha āsīd auttānapādir mayi saṅgatātmā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ta evam utsannabhayā urukrame kṛtāvanāmāḥ prayayus triviṣṭapam
BhP sahasraśīrṣāpi tato garutmatā madhor vanaṃ bhṛtyadidṛkṣayā gataḥ
BhP sa vai dhiyā yogavipākatīvrayā hṛtpadmakośe sphuritaṃ taḍitprabham
BhP tirohitaṃ sahasaivopalakṣya bahiḥsthitaṃ tadavasthaṃ dadarśa
BhP taddarśanenāgatasādhvasaḥ kṣitāv avandatāṅgaṃ vinamayya daṇḍavat
BhP dṛgbhyāṃ prapaśyan prapibann ivārbhakaś cumbann ivāsyena bhujair ivāśliṣan
BhP sa taṃ vivakṣantam atadvidaṃ harir jñātvāsya sarvasya ca hṛdy avasthitaḥ
BhP kṛtāñjaliṃ brahmamayena kambunā pasparśa bālaṃ kṛpayā kapole
BhP sa vai tadaiva pratipāditāṃ giraṃ daivīṃ parijñātaparātmanirṇayaḥ
BhP taṃ bhaktibhāvo 'bhyagṛṇād asatvaraṃ pariśrutoruśravasaṃ dhruvakṣitiḥ
BhP dhruva uvāca
BhP yo 'ntaḥ praviśya mama vācam imāṃ prasuptāṃ
BhP sañjīvayaty akhilaśaktidharaḥ svadhāmnā
BhP anyāṃś ca hastacaraṇaśravaṇatvagādīn
BhP prāṇān namo bhagavate puruṣāya tubhyam
BhP ekas tvam eva bhagavann idam ātmaśaktyā
BhP māyākhyayoruguṇayā mahadādyaśeṣam
BhP sṛṣṭvānuviśya puruṣas tadasadguṇeṣu
BhP nāneva dāruṣu vibhāvasuvad vibhāsi
BhP tvaddattayā vayunayedam acaṣṭa viśvaṃ
BhP suptaprabuddha iva nātha bhavatprapannaḥ
BhP tasyāpavargyaśaraṇaṃ tava pādamūlaṃ
BhP vismaryate kṛtavidā katham ārtabandho
BhP nūnaṃ vimuṣṭamatayas tava māyayā te
BhP ye tvāṃ bhavāpyayavimokṣaṇam anyahetoḥ
BhP arcanti kalpakataruṃ kuṇapopabhogyam
BhP icchanti yat sparśajaṃ niraye 'pi nṇām
BhP yā nirvṛtis tanubhṛtāṃ tava pādapadma
BhP dhyānād bhavajjanakathāśravaṇena vā syāt
BhP sā brahmaṇi svamahimany api nātha mā bhūt
BhP kiṃ tv antakāsilulitāt patatāṃ vimānāt
BhP bhaktiṃ muhuḥ pravahatāṃ tvayi me prasaṅgo
BhP bhūyād ananta mahatām amalāśayānām
BhP yenāñjasolbaṇam uruvyasanaṃ bhavābdhiṃ
BhP neṣye bhavadguṇakathāmṛtapānamattaḥ
BhP te na smaranty atitarāṃ priyam īśa martyaṃ
BhP ye cānv adaḥ sutasuhṛdgṛhavittadārāḥ
BhP ye tv abjanābha bhavadīyapadāravinda
BhP saugandhyalubdhahṛdayeṣu kṛtaprasaṅgāḥ
BhP tiryaṅnagadvijasarīsṛpadevadaitya
BhP martyādibhiḥ paricitaṃ sadasadviśeṣam
BhP rūpaṃ sthaviṣṭham aja te mahadādyanekaṃ
BhP nātaḥ paraṃ parama vedmi na yatra vādaḥ
BhP kalpānta etad akhilaṃ jaṭhareṇa gṛhṇan
BhP śete pumān svadṛg anantasakhas tadaṅke
BhP yannābhisindhuruhakāñcanalokapadma
BhP garbhe dyumān bhagavate praṇato 'smi tasmai
BhP tvaṃ nityamuktapariśuddhavibuddha ātmā
BhP kūṭastha ādipuruṣo bhagavāṃs tryadhīśaḥ
BhP yadbuddhyavasthitim akhaṇḍitayā svadṛṣṭyā
BhP draṣṭā sthitāv adhimakho vyatirikta āsse
BhP yasmin viruddhagatayo hy aniśaṃ patanti
BhP vidyādayo vividhaśaktaya ānupūrvyāt
BhP tad brahma viśvabhavam ekam anantam ādyam
BhP ānandamātram avikāram ahaṃ prapadye
BhP satyāśiṣo hi bhagavaṃs tava pādapadmam
BhP āśīs tathānubhajataḥ puruṣārthamūrteḥ
BhP apy evam arya bhagavān paripāti dīnān
BhP vāśreva vatsakam anugrahakātaro 'smān
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP athābhiṣṭuta evaṃ vai satsaṅkalpena dhīmatā
BhP bhṛtyānurakto bhagavān pratinandyedam abravīt
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP vedāhaṃ te vyavasitaṃ hṛdi rājanyabālaka
BhP tat prayacchāmi bhadraṃ te durāpam api suvrata
BhP nānyair adhiṣṭhitaṃ bhadra yad bhrājiṣṇu dhruvakṣiti
BhP yatra graharkṣatārāṇāṃ jyotiṣāṃ cakram āhitam
BhP meḍhyāṃ gocakravat sthāsnu parastāt kalpavāsinām
BhP dharmo 'gniḥ kaśyapaḥ śukro munayo ye vanaukasaḥ
BhP caranti dakṣiṇīkṛtya bhramanto yat satārakāḥ
BhP prasthite tu vanaṃ pitrā dattvā gāṃ dharmasaṃśrayaḥ
BhP ṣaṭtriṃśadvarṣasāhasraṃ rakṣitāvyāhatendriyaḥ
BhP tvadbhrātary uttame naṣṭe mṛgayāyāṃ tu tanmanāḥ
BhP anveṣantī vanaṃ mātā dāvāgniṃ sā pravekṣyati
BhP iṣṭvā māṃ yajñahṛdayaṃ yajñaiḥ puṣkaladakṣiṇaiḥ
BhP bhuktvā cehāśiṣaḥ satyā ante māṃ saṃsmariṣyasi
BhP tato gantāsi matsthānaṃ sarvalokanamaskṛtam
BhP upariṣṭād ṛṣibhyas tvaṃ yato nāvartate gataḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ity arcitaḥ sa bhagavān atidiśyātmanaḥ padam
BhP bālasya paśyato dhāma svam agād garuḍadhvajaḥ
BhP so 'pi saṅkalpajaṃ viṣṇoḥ pādasevopasāditam
BhP prāpya saṅkalpanirvāṇaṃ nātiprīto 'bhyagāt puram
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP sudurlabhaṃ yat paramaṃ padaṃ harer māyāvinas taccaraṇārcanārjitam
BhP labdhvāpy asiddhārtham ivaikajanmanā kathaṃ svam ātmānam amanyatārthavit
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP mātuḥ sapatnyā vāgbāṇair hṛdi viddhas tu tān smaran
BhP naicchan muktipater muktiṃ tasmāt tāpam upeyivān
BhP dhruva uvāca
BhP samādhinā naikabhavena yat padaṃ viduḥ sanandādaya ūrdhvaretasaḥ
BhP māsair ahaṃ ṣaḍbhir amuṣya pādayoś chāyām upetyāpagataḥ pṛthaṅmatiḥ
BhP aho bata mamānātmyaṃ mandabhāgyasya paśyata
BhP bhavacchidaḥ pādamūlaṃ gatvā yāce yad antavat
BhP matir vidūṣitā devaiḥ patadbhir asahiṣṇubhiḥ
BhP yo nāradavacas tathyaṃ nāgrāhiṣam asattamaḥ
BhP daivīṃ māyām upāśritya prasupta iva bhinnadṛk
BhP tapye dvitīye 'py asati bhrātṛbhrātṛvyahṛdrujā
BhP mayaitat prārthitaṃ vyarthaṃ cikitseva gatāyuṣi
BhP prasādya jagadātmānaṃ tapasā duṣprasādanam
BhP bhavacchidam ayāce 'haṃ bhavaṃ bhāgyavivarjitaḥ
BhP svārājyaṃ yacchato mauḍhyān māno me bhikṣito bata
BhP īśvarāt kṣīṇapuṇyena phalīkārān ivādhanaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP na vai mukundasya padāravindayo rajojuṣas tāta bhavādṛśā janāḥ
BhP vāñchanti taddāsyam ṛte 'rtham ātmano yadṛcchayā labdhamanaḥsamṛddhayaḥ
BhP ākarṇyātmajam āyāntaṃ samparetya yathāgatam
BhP rājā na śraddadhe bhadram abhadrasya kuto mama
BhP śraddhāya vākyaṃ devarṣer harṣavegena dharṣitaḥ
BhP vārtāhartur atiprīto hāraṃ prādān mahādhanam
BhP sadaśvaṃ ratham āruhya kārtasvarapariṣkṛtam
BhP brāhmaṇaiḥ kulavṛddhaiś ca paryasto 'mātyabandhubhiḥ
BhP śaṅkhadundubhinādena brahmaghoṣeṇa veṇubhiḥ
BhP niścakrāma purāt tūrṇam ātmajābhīkṣaṇotsukaḥ
BhP sunītiḥ suruciś cāsya mahiṣyau rukmabhūṣite
BhP āruhya śibikāṃ sārdham uttamenābhijagmatuḥ
BhP taṃ dṛṣṭvopavanābhyāśa āyāntaṃ tarasā rathāt
BhP avaruhya nṛpas tūrṇam āsādya premavihvalaḥ
BhP parirebhe 'ṅgajaṃ dorbhyāṃ dīrghotkaṇṭhamanāḥ śvasan
BhP viṣvaksenāṅghrisaṃsparśa hatāśeṣāghabandhanam
BhP athājighran muhur mūrdhni śītair nayanavāribhiḥ
BhP snāpayām āsa tanayaṃ jātoddāmamanorathaḥ
BhP abhivandya pituḥ pādāv āśīrbhiś cābhimantritaḥ
BhP nanāma mātarau śīrṣṇā satkṛtaḥ sajjanāgraṇīḥ
BhP surucis taṃ samutthāpya pādāvanatam arbhakam
BhP pariṣvajyāha jīveti bāṣpagadgadayā girā
BhP yasya prasanno bhagavānguṇair maitryādibhir hariḥ
BhP tasmai namanti bhūtāni nimnam āpa iva svayam
BhP uttamaś ca dhruvaś cobhāv anyonyaṃ premavihvalau
BhP aṅgasaṅgād utpulakāv asraughaṃ muhur ūhatuḥ
BhP sunītir asya jananī prāṇebhyo 'pi priyaṃ sutam
BhP upaguhya jahāv ādhiṃ tadaṅgasparśanirvṛtā
BhP payaḥ stanābhyāṃ susrāva netrajaiḥ salilaiḥ śivaiḥ
BhP tadābhiṣicyamānābhyāṃ vīra vīrasuvo muhuḥ
BhP tāṃ śaśaṃsur janā rājñīṃ diṣṭyā te putra ārtihā
BhP pratilabdhaś ciraṃ naṣṭo rakṣitā maṇḍalaṃ bhuvaḥ
BhP abhyarcitas tvayā nūnaṃ bhagavān praṇatārtihā
BhP yadanudhyāyino dhīrā mṛtyuṃ jigyuḥ sudurjayam
BhP lālyamānaṃ janair evaṃ dhruvaṃ sabhrātaraṃ nṛpaḥ
BhP āropya kariṇīṃ hṛṣṭaḥ stūyamāno 'viśat puram
BhP tatra tatropasaṅkḷptair lasanmakaratoraṇaiḥ
BhP savṛndaiḥ kadalīstambhaiḥ pūgapotaiś ca tadvidhaiḥ
BhP cūtapallavavāsaḥsraṅ muktādāmavilambibhiḥ
BhP upaskṛtaṃ pratidvāram apāṃ kumbhaiḥ sadīpakaiḥ
BhP prākārair gopurāgāraiḥ śātakumbhaparicchadaiḥ
BhP sarvato 'laṅkṛtaṃ śrīmad vimānaśikharadyubhiḥ
BhP mṛṣṭacatvararathyāṭṭa mārgaṃ candanacarcitam
BhP lājākṣataiḥ puṣpaphalais taṇḍulair balibhir yutam
BhP dhruvāya pathi dṛṣṭāya tatra tatra purastriyaḥ
BhP siddhārthākṣatadadhyambu dūrvāpuṣpaphalāni ca
BhP upajahruḥ prayuñjānā vātsalyād āśiṣaḥ satīḥ
BhP śṛṇvaṃs tadvalgugītāni prāviśad bhavanaṃ pituḥ
BhP mahāmaṇivrātamaye sa tasmin bhavanottame
BhP lālito nitarāṃ pitrā nyavasad divi devavat
BhP payaḥphenanibhāḥ śayyā dāntā rukmaparicchadāḥ
BhP āsanāni mahārhāṇi yatra raukmā upaskarāḥ
BhP yatra sphaṭikakuḍyeṣu mahāmārakateṣu ca
BhP maṇipradīpā ābhānti lalanāratnasaṃyutāḥ
BhP udyānāni ca ramyāṇi vicitrair amaradrumaiḥ
BhP kūjadvihaṅgamithunair gāyanmattamadhuvrataiḥ
BhP vāpyo vaidūryasopānāḥ padmotpalakumudvatīḥ
BhP haṃsakāraṇḍavakulair juṣṭāś cakrāhvasārasaiḥ
BhP uttānapādo rājarṣiḥ prabhāvaṃ tanayasya tam
BhP śrutvā dṛṣṭvādbhutatamaṃ prapede vismayaṃ param
BhP vīkṣyoḍhavayasaṃ taṃ ca prakṛtīnāṃ ca sammatam
BhP anuraktaprajaṃ rājā dhruvaṃ cakre bhuvaḥ patim
BhP ātmānaṃ ca pravayasam ākalayya viśāmpatiḥ
BhP vanaṃ viraktaḥ prātiṣṭhad vimṛśann ātmano gatim
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP prajāpater duhitaraṃ śiśumārasya vai dhruvaḥ
BhP upayeme bhramiṃ nāma tatsutau kalpavatsarau
BhP ilāyām api bhāryāyāṃ vāyoḥ putryāṃ mahābalaḥ
BhP putram utkalanāmānaṃ yoṣidratnam ajījanat
BhP uttamas tv akṛtodvāho mṛgayāyāṃ balīyasā
BhP hataḥ puṇyajanenādrau tanmātāsya gatiṃ gatā
BhP dhruvo bhrātṛvadhaṃ śrutvā kopāmarṣaśucārpitaḥ
BhP jaitraṃ syandanam āsthāya gataḥ puṇyajanālayam
BhP gatvodīcīṃ diśaṃ rājā rudrānucarasevitām
BhP dadarśa himavaddroṇyāṃ purīṃ guhyakasaṅkulām
BhP dadhmau śaṅkhaṃ bṛhadbāhuḥ khaṃ diśaś cānunādayan
BhP yenodvignadṛśaḥ kṣattar upadevyo 'trasan bhṛśam
BhP tato niṣkramya balina upadevamahābhaṭāḥ
BhP asahantas tanninādam abhipetur udāyudhāḥ
BhP sa tān āpatato vīra ugradhanvā mahārathaḥ
BhP ekaikaṃ yugapat sarvān ahan bāṇais tribhis tribhiḥ
BhP te vai lalāṭalagnais tair iṣubhiḥ sarva eva hi
BhP matvā nirastam ātmānam āśaṃsan karma tasya tat
BhP te 'pi cāmum amṛṣyantaḥ pādasparśam ivoragāḥ
BhP śarair avidhyan yugapad dviguṇaṃ pracikīrṣavaḥ
BhP tataḥ parighanistriṃśaiḥ prāsaśūlaparaśvadhaiḥ
BhP śaktyṛṣṭibhir bhuśuṇḍībhiś citravājaiḥ śarair api
BhP abhyavarṣan prakupitāḥ sarathaṃ sahasārathim
BhP icchantas tat pratīkartum ayutānāṃ trayodaśa
BhP auttānapādiḥ sa tadā śastravarṣeṇa bhūriṇā
BhP na evādṛśyatācchanna āsāreṇa yathā giriḥ
BhP hāhākāras tadaivāsīt siddhānāṃ divi paśyatām
BhP hato 'yaṃ mānavaḥ sūryo magnaḥ puṇyajanārṇave
BhP nadatsu yātudhāneṣu jayakāśiṣv atho mṛdhe
BhP udatiṣṭhad rathas tasya nīhārād iva bhāskaraḥ
BhP dhanur visphūrjayan divyaṃ dviṣatāṃ khedam udvahan
BhP astraughaṃ vyadhamad bāṇair ghanānīkam ivānilaḥ
BhP tasya te cāpanirmuktā bhittvā varmāṇi rakṣasām
BhP kāyān āviviśus tigmā girīn aśanayo yathā
BhP bhallaiḥ sañchidyamānānāṃ śirobhiś cārukuṇḍalaiḥ
BhP ūrubhir hematālābhair dorbhir valayavalgubhiḥ
BhP hārakeyūramukuṭair uṣṇīṣaiś ca mahādhanaiḥ
BhP āstṛtās tā raṇabhuvo rejur vīramanoharāḥ
BhP hatāvaśiṣṭā itare raṇājirād rakṣogaṇāḥ kṣatriyavaryasāyakaiḥ
BhP prāyo vivṛkṇāvayavā vidudruvur mṛgendravikrīḍitayūthapā iva
BhP apaśyamānaḥ sa tadātatāyinaṃ mahāmṛdhe kañcana mānavottamaḥ
BhP purīṃ didṛkṣann api nāviśad dviṣāṃ na māyināṃ veda cikīrṣitaṃ janaḥ
BhP iti bruvaṃś citrarathaḥ svasārathiṃ yattaḥ pareṣāṃ pratiyogaśaṅkitaḥ
BhP śuśrāva śabdaṃ jaladher iveritaṃ nabhasvato dikṣu rajo 'nvadṛśyata
BhP kṣaṇenācchāditaṃ vyoma ghanānīkena sarvataḥ
BhP visphurattaḍitā dikṣu trāsayatstanayitnunā
BhP vavṛṣū rudhiraughāsṛk pūyaviṇmūtramedasaḥ
BhP nipetur gaganād asya kabandhāny agrato 'nagha
BhP tataḥ khe 'dṛśyata girir nipetuḥ sarvatodiśam
BhP gadāparighanistriṃśa musalāḥ sāśmavarṣiṇaḥ
BhP ahayo 'śaniniḥśvāsā vamanto 'gniṃ ruṣākṣibhiḥ
BhP abhyadhāvan gajā mattāḥ siṃhavyāghrāś ca yūthaśaḥ
BhP samudra ūrmibhir bhīmaḥ plāvayan sarvato bhuvam
BhP āsasāda mahāhrādaḥ kalpānta iva bhīṣaṇaḥ
BhP evaṃvidhāny anekāni trāsanāny amanasvinām
BhP sasṛjus tigmagataya āsuryā māyayāsurāḥ
BhP dhruve prayuktām asurais tāṃ māyām atidustarām
BhP niśamya tasya munayaḥ śam āśaṃsan samāgatāḥ
BhP munaya ūcuḥ
BhP auttānapāda bhagavāṃs tava śārṅgadhanvā
BhP devaḥ kṣiṇotv avanatārtiharo vipakṣān
BhP yannāmadheyam abhidhāya niśamya cāddhā
BhP loko 'ñjasā tarati dustaram aṅga mṛtyum
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP niśamya gadatām evam ṛṣīṇāṃ dhanuṣi dhruvaḥ
BhP sandadhe 'stram upaspṛśya yan nārāyaṇanirmitam
BhP sandhīyamāna etasmin māyā guhyakanirmitāḥ
BhP kṣipraṃ vineśur vidura kleśā jñānodaye yathā
BhP tasyārṣāstraṃ dhanuṣi prayuñjataḥ suvarṇapuṅkhāḥ kalahaṃsavāsasaḥ
BhP viniḥsṛtā āviviśur dviṣadbalaṃ yathā vanaṃ bhīmaravāḥ śikhaṇḍinaḥ
BhP tais tigmadhāraiḥ pradhane śilīmukhair itas tataḥ puṇyajanā upadrutāḥ
BhP tam abhyadhāvan kupitā udāyudhāḥ suparṇam unnaddhaphaṇā ivāhayaḥ
BhP sa tān pṛṣatkair abhidhāvato mṛdhe nikṛttabāhūruśirodharodarān
BhP nināya lokaṃ param arkamaṇḍalaṃ vrajanti nirbhidya yam ūrdhvaretasaḥ
BhP tān hanyamānān abhivīkṣya guhyakān anāgasaś citrarathena bhūriśaḥ
BhP auttānapādiṃ kṛpayā pitāmaho manur jagādopagataḥ saharṣibhiḥ
BhP manur uvāca
BhP alaṃ vatsātiroṣeṇa tamodvāreṇa pāpmanā
BhP yena puṇyajanān etān avadhīs tvam anāgasaḥ
BhP nāsmatkulocitaṃ tāta karmaitat sadvigarhitam
BhP vadho yad upadevānām ārabdhas te 'kṛtainasām
BhP nanv ekasyāparādhena prasaṅgād bahavo hatāḥ
BhP bhrātur vadhābhitaptena tvayāṅga bhrātṛvatsala
BhP nāyaṃ mārgo hi sādhūnāṃ hṛṣīkeśānuvartinām
BhP yad ātmānaṃ parāg gṛhya paśuvad bhūtavaiśasam
BhP sarvabhūtātmabhāvena bhūtāvāsaṃ hariṃ bhavān
BhP ārādhyāpa durārādhyaṃ viṣṇos tat paramaṃ padam
BhP sa tvaṃ harer anudhyātas tatpuṃsām api sammataḥ
BhP kathaṃ tv avadyaṃ kṛtavān anuśikṣan satāṃ vratam
BhP titikṣayā karuṇayā maitryā cākhilajantuṣu
BhP samatvena ca sarvātmā bhagavān samprasīdati
BhP samprasanne bhagavati puruṣaḥ prākṛtair guṇaiḥ
BhP vimukto jīvanirmukto brahma nirvāṇam ṛcchati
BhP bhūtaiḥ pañcabhir ārabdhair yoṣit puruṣa eva hi
BhP tayor vyavāyāt sambhūtir yoṣitpuruṣayor iha
BhP evaṃ pravartate sargaḥ sthitiḥ saṃyama eva ca
BhP guṇavyatikarād rājan māyayā paramātmanaḥ
BhP nimittamātraṃ tatrāsīn nirguṇaḥ puruṣarṣabhaḥ
BhP vyaktāvyaktam idaṃ viśvaṃ yatra bhramati lohavat
BhP sa khalv idaṃ bhagavān kālaśaktyā guṇapravāheṇa vibhaktavīryaḥ
BhP karoty akartaiva nihanty ahantā ceṣṭā vibhūmnaḥ khalu durvibhāvyā
BhP so 'nanto 'ntakaraḥ kālo 'nādir ādikṛd avyayaḥ
BhP janaṃ janena janayan mārayan mṛtyunāntakam
BhP na vai svapakṣo 'sya vipakṣa eva vā parasya mṛtyor viśataḥ samaṃ prajāḥ
BhP taṃ dhāvamānam anudhāvanty anīśā yathā rajāṃsy anilaṃ bhūtasaṅghāḥ
BhP āyuṣo 'pacayaṃ jantos tathaivopacayaṃ vibhuḥ
BhP ubhābhyāṃ rahitaḥ svastho duḥsthasya vidadhāty asau
BhP kecit karma vadanty enaṃ svabhāvam apare nṛpa
BhP eke kālaṃ pare daivaṃ puṃsaḥ kāmam utāpare
BhP avyaktasyāprameyasya nānāśaktyudayasya ca
BhP na vai cikīrṣitaṃ tāta ko vedātha svasambhavam
BhP na caite putraka bhrātur hantāro dhanadānugāḥ
BhP visargādānayos tāta puṃso daivaṃ hi kāraṇam
BhP sa eva viśvaṃ sṛjati sa evāvati hanti ca
BhP athāpi hy anahaṅkārān nājyate guṇakarmabhiḥ
BhP eṣa bhūtāni bhūtātmā bhūteśo bhūtabhāvanaḥ
BhP svaśaktyā māyayā yuktaḥ sṛjaty atti ca pāti ca
BhP tam eva mṛtyum amṛtaṃ tāta daivaṃ sarvātmanopehi jagatparāyaṇam
BhP yasmai baliṃ viśvasṛjo haranti gāvo yathā vai nasi dāmayantritāḥ
BhP yaḥ pañcavarṣo jananīṃ tvaṃ vihāya mātuḥ sapatnyā vacasā bhinnamarmā
BhP vanaṃ gatas tapasā pratyagakṣam ārādhya lebhe mūrdhni padaṃ trilokyāḥ
BhP tam enam aṅgātmani muktavigrahe vyapāśritaṃ nirguṇam ekam akṣaram
BhP ātmānam anviccha vimuktam ātmadṛg yasminn idaṃ bhedam asat pratīyate
BhP tvaṃ pratyagātmani tadā bhagavaty ananta ānandamātra upapannasamastaśaktau
BhP bhaktiṃ vidhāya paramāṃ śanakair avidyā granthiṃ vibhetsyasi mamāham iti prarūḍham
BhP saṃyaccha roṣaṃ bhadraṃ te pratīpaṃ śreyasāṃ param
BhP śrutena bhūyasā rājann agadena yathāmayam
BhP yenopasṛṣṭāt puruṣāl loka udvijate bhṛśam
BhP na budhas tadvaśaṃ gacched icchann abhayam ātmanaḥ
BhP helanaṃ giriśabhrātur dhanadasya tvayā kṛtam
BhP yaj jaghnivān puṇyajanān bhrātṛghnān ity amarṣitaḥ
BhP taṃ prasādaya vatsāśu sannatyā praśrayoktibhiḥ
BhP na yāvan mahatāṃ tejaḥ kulaṃ no 'bhibhaviṣyati
BhP evaṃ svāyambhuvaḥ pautram anuśāsya manur dhruvam
BhP tenābhivanditaḥ sākam ṛṣibhiḥ svapuraṃ yayau
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP dhruvaṃ nivṛttaṃ pratibuddhya vaiśasād apetamanyuṃ bhagavān dhaneśvaraḥ
BhP tatrāgataś cāraṇayakṣakinnaraiḥ saṃstūyamāno nyavadat kṛtāñjalim
BhP dhanada uvāca
BhP bho bhoḥ kṣatriyadāyāda parituṣṭo 'smi te 'nagha
BhP yat tvaṃ pitāmahādeśād vairaṃ dustyajam atyajaḥ
BhP na bhavān avadhīd yakṣān na yakṣā bhrātaraṃ tava
BhP kāla eva hi bhūtānāṃ prabhur apyayabhāvayoḥ
BhP ahaṃ tvam ity apārthā dhīr ajñānāt puruṣasya hi
BhP svāpnīvābhāty ataddhyānād yayā bandhaviparyayau
BhP tad gaccha dhruva bhadraṃ te bhagavantam adhokṣajam
BhP sarvabhūtātmabhāvena sarvabhūtātmavigraham
BhP bhajasva bhajanīyāṅghrim abhavāya bhavacchidam
BhP yuktaṃ virahitaṃ śaktyā guṇamayyātmamāyayā
BhP vṛṇīhi kāmaṃ nṛpa yan manogataṃ mattas tvam auttānapade 'viśaṅkitaḥ
BhP varaṃ varārho 'mbujanābhapādayor anantaraṃ tvāṃ vayam aṅga śuśruma
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sa rājarājena varāya codito dhruvo mahābhāgavato mahāmatiḥ
BhP harau sa vavre 'calitāṃ smṛtiṃ yayā taraty ayatnena duratyayaṃ tamaḥ
BhP tasya prītena manasā tāṃ dattvaiḍaviḍas tataḥ
BhP paśyato 'ntardadhe so 'pi svapuraṃ pratyapadyata
BhP athāyajata yajñeśaṃ kratubhir bhūridakṣiṇaiḥ
BhP dravyakriyādevatānāṃ karma karmaphalapradam
BhP sarvātmany acyute 'sarve tīvraughāṃ bhaktim udvahan
BhP dadarśātmani bhūteṣu tam evāvasthitaṃ vibhum
BhP tam evaṃ śīlasampannaṃ brahmaṇyaṃ dīnavatsalam
BhP goptāraṃ dharmasetūnāṃ menire pitaraṃ prajāḥ
BhP ṣaṭtriṃśadvarṣasāhasraṃ śaśāsa kṣitimaṇḍalam
BhP bhogaiḥ puṇyakṣayaṃ kurvann abhogair aśubhakṣayam
BhP evaṃ bahusavaṃ kālaṃ mahātmāvicalendriyaḥ
BhP trivargaupayikaṃ nītvā putrāyādān nṛpāsanam
BhP manyamāna idaṃ viśvaṃ māyāracitam ātmani
BhP avidyāracitasvapnagandharvanagaropamam
BhP ātmastryapatyasuhṛdo balam ṛddhakośam
BhP antaḥpuraṃ parivihārabhuvaś ca ramyāḥ
BhP bhūmaṇḍalaṃ jaladhimekhalam ākalayya
BhP kālopasṛṣṭam iti sa prayayau viśālām
BhP tasyāṃ viśuddhakaraṇaḥ śivavār vigāhya
BhP baddhvāsanaṃ jitamarun manasāhṛtākṣaḥ
BhP sthūle dadhāra bhagavatpratirūpa etad
BhP dhyāyaṃs tad avyavahito vyasṛjat samādhau
BhP bhaktiṃ harau bhagavati pravahann ajasram
BhP ānandabāṣpakalayā muhur ardyamānaḥ
BhP viklidyamānahṛdayaḥ pulakācitāṅgo
BhP nātmānam asmarad asāv iti muktaliṅgaḥ
BhP sa dadarśa vimānāgryaṃ nabhaso 'vatarad dhruvaḥ
BhP vibhrājayad daśa diśo rākāpatim ivoditam
BhP tatrānu devapravarau caturbhujau
BhP śyāmau kiśorāv aruṇāmbujekṣaṇau
BhP sthitāv avaṣṭabhya gadāṃ suvāsasau
BhP kirīṭahārāṅgadacārukuṇḍalau
BhP vijñāya tāv uttamagāyakiṅkarāv
BhP abhyutthitaḥ sādhvasavismṛtakramaḥ
BhP nanāma nāmāni gṛṇan madhudviṣaḥ
BhP pārṣatpradhānāv iti saṃhatāñjaliḥ
BhP taṃ kṛṣṇapādābhiniviṣṭacetasaṃ
BhP baddhāñjaliṃ praśrayanamrakandharam
BhP sunandanandāv upasṛtya sasmitaṃ
BhP pratyūcatuḥ puṣkaranābhasammatau
BhP sunandanandāv ūcatuḥ
BhP bho bho rājan subhadraṃ te vācaṃ no 'vahitaḥ śṛṇu
BhP yaḥ pañcavarṣas tapasā bhavān devam atītṛpat
BhP tasyākhilajagaddhātur āvāṃ devasya śārṅgiṇaḥ
BhP pārṣadāv iha samprāptau netuṃ tvāṃ bhagavatpadam
BhP sudurjayaṃ viṣṇupadaṃ jitaṃ tvayā yat sūrayo 'prāpya vicakṣate param
BhP ātiṣṭha tac candradivākarādayo graharkṣatārāḥ pariyanti dakṣiṇam
BhP anāsthitaṃ te pitṛbhir anyair apy aṅga karhicit
BhP ātiṣṭha jagatāṃ vandyaṃ tad viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam
BhP etad vimānapravaram uttamaślokamaulinā
BhP upasthāpitam āyuṣmann adhiroḍhuṃ tvam arhasi
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP niśamya vaikuṇṭhaniyojyamukhyayor madhucyutaṃ vācam urukramapriyaḥ
BhP kṛtābhiṣekaḥ kṛtanityamaṅgalo munīn praṇamyāśiṣam abhyavādayat
BhP parītyābhyarcya dhiṣṇyāgryaṃ pārṣadāv abhivandya ca
BhP iyeṣa tad adhiṣṭhātuṃ bibhrad rūpaṃ hiraṇmayam
BhP tadottānapadaḥ putro dadarśāntakam āgatam
BhP mṛtyor mūrdhni padaṃ dattvā ārurohādbhutaṃ gṛham
BhP tadā dundubhayo nedur mṛdaṅgapaṇavādayaḥ
BhP gandharvamukhyāḥ prajaguḥ petuḥ kusumavṛṣṭayaḥ
BhP sa ca svarlokam ārokṣyan sunītiṃ jananīṃ dhruvaḥ
BhP anvasmarad agaṃ hitvā dīnāṃ yāsye triviṣṭapam
BhP iti vyavasitaṃ tasya vyavasāya surottamau
BhP darśayām āsatur devīṃ puro yānena gacchatīm
BhP tatra tatra praśaṃsadbhiḥ pathi vaimānikaiḥ suraiḥ
BhP avakīryamāṇo dadṛśe kusumaiḥ kramaśo grahān
BhP trilokīṃ devayānena so 'tivrajya munīn api
BhP parastād yad dhruvagatir viṣṇoḥ padam athābhyagāt
BhP yad bhrājamānaṃ svarucaiva sarvato lokās trayo hy anu vibhrājanta ete
BhP yan nāvrajan jantuṣu ye 'nanugrahā vrajanti bhadrāṇi caranti ye 'niśam
BhP śāntāḥ samadṛśaḥ śuddhāḥ sarvabhūtānurañjanāḥ
BhP yānty añjasācyutapadam acyutapriyabāndhavāḥ
BhP ity uttānapadaḥ putro dhruvaḥ kṛṣṇaparāyaṇaḥ
BhP abhūt trayāṇāṃ lokānāṃ cūḍāmaṇir ivāmalaḥ
BhP gambhīravego 'nimiṣaṃ jyotiṣāṃ cakram āhitam
BhP yasmin bhramati kauravya meḍhyām iva gavāṃ gaṇaḥ
BhP mahimānaṃ vilokyāsya nārado bhagavān ṛṣiḥ
BhP ātodyaṃ vitudañ ślokān satre 'gāyat pracetasām
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP nūnaṃ sunīteḥ patidevatāyās tapaḥprabhāvasya sutasya tāṃ gatim
BhP dṛṣṭvābhyupāyān api vedavādino naivādhigantuṃ prabhavanti kiṃ nṛpāḥ
BhP yaḥ pañcavarṣo gurudāravākśarair bhinnena yāto hṛdayena dūyatā
BhP vanaṃ madādeśakaro 'jitaṃ prabhuṃ jigāya tadbhaktaguṇaiḥ parājitam
BhP yaḥ kṣatrabandhur bhuvi tasyādhirūḍham anv ārurukṣed api varṣapūgaiḥ
BhP ṣaṭpañcavarṣo yad ahobhir alpaiḥ prasādya vaikuṇṭham avāpa tatpadam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP etat te 'bhihitaṃ sarvaṃ yat pṛṣṭo 'ham iha tvayā
BhP dhruvasyoddāmayaśasaś caritaṃ sammataṃ satām
BhP dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ svastyayanaṃ mahat
BhP svargyaṃ dhrauvyaṃ saumanasyaṃ praśasyam aghamarṣaṇam
BhP śrutvaitac chraddhayābhīkṣṇam acyutapriyaceṣṭitam
BhP bhaved bhaktir bhagavati yayā syāt kleśasaṅkṣayaḥ
BhP mahattvam icchatāṃ tīrthaṃ śrotuḥ śīlādayo guṇāḥ
BhP yatra tejas tad icchūnāṃ māno yatra manasvinām
BhP prayataḥ kīrtayet prātaḥ samavāye dvijanmanām
BhP sāyaṃ ca puṇyaślokasya dhruvasya caritaṃ mahat
BhP paurṇamāsyāṃ sinīvālyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ śravaṇe 'thavā
BhP dinakṣaye vyatīpāte saṅkrame 'rkadine 'pi vā
BhP śrāvayec chraddadhānānāṃ tīrthapādapadāśrayaḥ
BhP necchaṃs tatrātmanātmānaṃ santuṣṭa iti sidhyati
BhP jñānam ajñātatattvāya yo dadyāt satpathe 'mṛtam
BhP kṛpālor dīnanāthasya devās tasyānugṛhṇate
BhP idaṃ mayā te 'bhihitaṃ kurūdvaha dhruvasya vikhyātaviśuddhakarmaṇaḥ
BhP hitvārbhakaḥ krīḍanakāni mātur gṛhaṃ ca viṣṇuṃ śaraṇaṃ yo jagāma
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP niśamya kauṣāraviṇopavarṇitaṃ dhruvasya vaikuṇṭhapadādhirohaṇam
BhP prarūḍhabhāvo bhagavaty adhokṣaje praṣṭuṃ punas taṃ viduraḥ pracakrame
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP ke te pracetaso nāma kasyāpatyāni suvrata
BhP kasyānvavāye prakhyātāḥ kutra vā satram āsata
BhP manye mahābhāgavataṃ nāradaṃ devadarśanam
BhP yena proktaḥ kriyāyogaḥ paricaryāvidhir hareḥ
BhP svadharmaśīlaiḥ puruṣair bhagavān yajñapūruṣaḥ
BhP ijyamāno bhaktimatā nāradeneritaḥ kila
BhP yās tā devarṣiṇā tatra varṇitā bhagavatkathāḥ
BhP mahyaṃ śuśrūṣave brahman kārtsnyenācaṣṭum arhasi
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP dhruvasya cotkalaḥ putraḥ pitari prasthite vanam
BhP sārvabhaumaśriyaṃ naicchad adhirājāsanaṃ pituḥ
BhP sa janmanopaśāntātmā niḥsaṅgaḥ samadarśanaḥ
BhP dadarśa loke vitatam ātmānaṃ lokam ātmani
BhP ātmānaṃ brahma nirvāṇaṃ pratyastamitavigraham
BhP avabodharasaikātmyam ānandam anusantatam
BhP avyavacchinnayogāgni dagdhakarmamalāśayaḥ
BhP svarūpam avarundhāno nātmano 'nyaṃ tadaikṣata
BhP jaḍāndhabadhironmatta mūkākṛtir atanmatiḥ
BhP lakṣitaḥ pathi bālānāṃ praśāntārcir ivānalaḥ
BhP matvā taṃ jaḍam unmattaṃ kulavṛddhāḥ samantriṇaḥ
BhP vatsaraṃ bhūpatiṃ cakrur yavīyāṃsaṃ bhrameḥ sutam
BhP svarvīthir vatsarasyeṣṭā bhāryāsūta ṣaḍātmajān
BhP puṣpārṇaṃ tigmaketuṃ ca iṣam ūrjaṃ vasuṃ jayam
BhP puṣpārṇasya prabhā bhāryā doṣā ca dve babhūvatuḥ
BhP prātar madhyandinaṃ sāyam iti hy āsan prabhāsutāḥ
BhP pradoṣo niśitho vyuṣṭa iti doṣāsutās trayaḥ
BhP vyuṣṭaḥ sutaṃ puṣkariṇyāṃ sarvatejasam ādadhe
BhP sa cakṣuḥ sutam ākūtyāṃ patnyāṃ manum avāpa ha
BhP manor asūta mahiṣī virajān naḍvalā sutān
BhP puruṃ kutsaṃ tritaṃ dyumnaṃ satyavantam ṛtaṃ vratam
BhP agniṣṭomam atīrātraṃ pradyumnaṃ śibim ulmukam
BhP ulmuko 'janayat putrān puṣkariṇyāṃ ṣaḍ uttamān
BhP aṅgaṃ sumanasaṃ khyātiṃ kratum aṅgirasaṃ gayam
BhP sunīthāṅgasya yā patnī suṣuve venam ulbaṇam
BhP yaddauḥśīlyāt sa rājarṣir nirviṇṇo niragāt purāt
BhP yam aṅga śepuḥ kupitā vāgvajrā munayaḥ kila
BhP gatāsos tasya bhūyas te mamanthur dakṣiṇaṃ karam
BhP arājake tadā loke dasyubhiḥ pīḍitāḥ prajāḥ
BhP jāto nārāyaṇāṃśena pṛthur ādyaḥ kṣitīśvaraḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP tasya śīlanidheḥ sādhor brahmaṇyasya mahātmanaḥ
BhP rājñaḥ katham abhūd duṣṭā prajā yad vimanā yayau
BhP kiṃ vāṃho vena uddiśya brahmadaṇḍam ayūyujan
BhP daṇḍavratadhare rājñi munayo dharmakovidāḥ
BhP nāvadhyeyaḥ prajāpālaḥ prajābhir aghavān api
BhP yad asau lokapālānāṃ bibharty ojaḥ svatejasā
BhP etad ākhyāhi me brahman sunīthātmajaceṣṭitam
BhP śraddadhānāya bhaktāya tvaṃ parāvaravittamaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP aṅgo 'śvamedhaṃ rājarṣir ājahāra mahākratum
BhP nājagmur devatās tasminn āhūtā brahmavādibhiḥ
BhP tam ūcur vismitās tatra yajamānam athartvijaḥ
BhP havīṃṣi hūyamānāni na te gṛhṇanti devatāḥ
BhP rājan havīṃṣy aduṣṭāni śraddhayāsāditāni te
BhP chandāṃsy ayātayāmāni yojitāni dhṛtavrataiḥ
BhP na vidāmeha devānāṃ helanaṃ vayam aṇv api
BhP yan na gṛhṇanti bhāgān svān ye devāḥ karmasākṣiṇaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP aṅgo dvijavacaḥ śrutvā yajamānaḥ sudurmanāḥ
BhP tat praṣṭuṃ vyasṛjad vācaṃ sadasyāṃs tadanujñayā
BhP nāgacchanty āhutā devā na gṛhṇanti grahān iha
BhP sadasaspatayo brūta kim avadyaṃ mayā kṛtam
BhP sadasaspataya ūcuḥ
BhP naradeveha bhavato nāghaṃ tāvan manāk sthitam
BhP asty ekaṃ prāktanam aghaṃ yad ihedṛk tvam aprajaḥ
BhP tathā sādhaya bhadraṃ te ātmānaṃ suprajaṃ nṛpa
BhP iṣṭas te putrakāmasya putraṃ dāsyati yajñabhuk
BhP tathā svabhāgadheyāni grahīṣyanti divaukasaḥ
BhP yad yajñapuruṣaḥ sākṣād apatyāya harir vṛtaḥ
BhP tāṃs tān kāmān harir dadyād yān yān kāmayate janaḥ
BhP ārādhito yathaivaiṣa tathā puṃsāṃ phalodayaḥ
BhP iti vyavasitā viprās tasya rājñaḥ prajātaye
BhP puroḍāśaṃ niravapan śipiviṣṭāya viṣṇave
BhP tasmāt puruṣa uttasthau hemamāly amalāmbaraḥ
BhP hiraṇmayena pātreṇa siddham ādāya pāyasam
BhP sa viprānumato rājā gṛhītvāñjalinaudanam
BhP avaghrāya mudā yuktaḥ prādāt patnyā udāradhīḥ
BhP sā tat puṃsavanaṃ rājñī prāśya vai patyur ādadhe
BhP garbhaṃ kāla upāvṛtte kumāraṃ suṣuve 'prajā
BhP sa bāla eva puruṣo mātāmaham anuvrataḥ
BhP adharmāṃśodbhavaṃ mṛtyuṃ tenābhavad adhārmikaḥ
BhP sa śarāsanam udyamya mṛgayur vanagocaraḥ
BhP hanty asādhur mṛgān dīnān veno 'sāv ity arauj janaḥ
BhP ākrīḍe krīḍato bālān vayasyān atidāruṇaḥ
BhP prasahya niranukrośaḥ paśumāram amārayat
BhP taṃ vicakṣya khalaṃ putraṃ śāsanair vividhair nṛpaḥ
BhP yadā na śāsituṃ kalpo bhṛśam āsīt sudurmanāḥ
BhP prāyeṇābhyarcito devo ye 'prajā gṛhamedhinaḥ
BhP kadapatyabhṛtaṃ duḥkhaṃ ye na vindanti durbharam
BhP yataḥ pāpīyasī kīrtir adharmaś ca mahān nṛṇām
BhP yato virodhaḥ sarveṣāṃ yata ādhir anantakaḥ
BhP kas taṃ prajāpadeśaṃ vai mohabandhanam ātmanaḥ
BhP paṇḍito bahu manyeta yadarthāḥ kleśadā gṛhāḥ
BhP kadapatyaṃ varaṃ manye sadapatyāc chucāṃ padāt
BhP nirvidyeta gṛhān martyo yatkleśanivahā gṛhāḥ
BhP evaṃ sa nirviṇṇamanā nṛpo gṛhān niśītha utthāya mahodayodayāt
BhP alabdhanidro 'nupalakṣito nṛbhir hitvā gato venasuvaṃ prasuptām
BhP vijñāya nirvidya gataṃ patiṃ prajāḥ purohitāmātyasuhṛdgaṇādayaḥ
BhP vicikyur urvyām atiśokakātarā yathā nigūḍhaṃ puruṣaṃ kuyoginaḥ
BhP alakṣayantaḥ padavīṃ prajāpater hatodyamāḥ pratyupasṛtya te purīm
BhP ṛṣīn sametān abhivandya sāśravo nyavedayan paurava bhartṛviplavam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP bhṛgvādayas te munayo lokānāṃ kṣemadarśinaḥ
BhP goptary asati vai nṝṇāṃ paśyantaḥ paśusāmyatām
BhP vīramātaram āhūya sunīthāṃ brahmavādinaḥ
BhP prakṛtyasammataṃ venam abhyaṣiñcan patiṃ bhuvaḥ
BhP śrutvā nṛpāsanagataṃ venam atyugraśāsanam
BhP nililyur dasyavaḥ sadyaḥ sarpatrastā ivākhavaḥ
BhP sa ārūḍhanṛpasthāna unnaddho 'ṣṭavibhūtibhiḥ
BhP avamene mahābhāgān stabdhaḥ sambhāvitaḥ svataḥ
BhP evaṃ madāndha utsikto niraṅkuśa iva dvipaḥ
BhP paryaṭan ratham āsthāya kampayann iva rodasī
BhP na yaṣṭavyaṃ na dātavyaṃ na hotavyaṃ dvijāḥ kvacit
BhP iti nyavārayad dharmaṃ bherīghoṣeṇa sarvaśaḥ
BhP venasyāvekṣya munayo durvṛttasya viceṣṭitam
BhP vimṛśya lokavyasanaṃ kṛpayocuḥ sma satriṇaḥ
BhP aho ubhayataḥ prāptaṃ lokasya vyasanaṃ mahat
BhP dāruṇy ubhayato dīpte iva taskarapālayoḥ
BhP arājakabhayād eṣa kṛto rājātadarhaṇaḥ
BhP tato 'py āsīd bhayaṃ tv adya kathaṃ syāt svasti dehinām
BhP aher iva payaḥpoṣaḥ poṣakasyāpy anarthabhṛt
BhP venaḥ prakṛtyaiva khalaḥ sunīthāgarbhasambhavaḥ
BhP nirūpitaḥ prajāpālaḥ sa jighāṃsati vai prajāḥ
BhP tathāpi sāntvayemāmuṃ nāsmāṃs tatpātakaṃ spṛśet
BhP tadvidvadbhir asadvṛtto veno 'smābhiḥ kṛto nṛpaḥ
BhP sāntvito yadi no vācaṃ na grahīṣyaty adharmakṛt
BhP lokadhikkārasandagdhaṃ dahiṣyāmaḥ svatejasā
BhP evam adhyavasāyainaṃ munayo gūḍhamanyavaḥ
BhP upavrajyābruvan venaṃ sāntvayitvā ca sāmabhiḥ
BhP munaya ūcuḥ
BhP nṛpavarya nibodhaitad yat te vijñāpayāma bhoḥ
BhP āyuḥśrībalakīrtīnāṃ tava tāta vivardhanam
BhP dharma ācaritaḥ puṃsāṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyabuddhibhiḥ
BhP lokān viśokān vitaraty athānantyam asaṅginām
BhP sa te mā vinaśed vīra prajānāṃ kṣemalakṣaṇaḥ
BhP yasmin vinaṣṭe nṛpatir aiśvaryād avarohati
BhP rājann asādhvamātyebhyaś corādibhyaḥ prajā nṛpaḥ
BhP rakṣan yathā baliṃ gṛhṇann iha pretya ca modate
BhP yasya rāṣṭre pure caiva bhagavān yajñapūruṣaḥ
BhP ijyate svena dharmeṇa janair varṇāśramānvitaiḥ
BhP tasya rājño mahābhāga bhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ
BhP parituṣyati viśvātmā tiṣṭhato nijaśāsane
BhP tasmiṃs tuṣṭe kim aprāpyaṃjagatām īśvareśvare
BhP lokāḥ sapālā hy etasmai haranti balim ādṛtāḥ
BhP taṃ sarvalokāmarayajñasaṅgrahaṃ trayīmayaṃ dravyamayaṃ tapomayam
BhP yajñair vicitrair yajato bhavāya te rājan svadeśān anuroddhum arhasi
BhP yajñena yuṣmadviṣaye dvijātibhir vitāyamānena surāḥ kalā hareḥ
BhP sviṣṭāḥ sutuṣṭāḥ pradiśanti vāñchitaṃ taddhelanaṃ nārhasi vīra ceṣṭitum
BhP vena uvāca
BhP bāliśā bata yūyaṃ vā adharme dharmamāninaḥ
BhP ye vṛttidaṃ patiṃ hitvā jāraṃ patim upāsate
BhP avajānanty amī mūḍhā nṛparūpiṇam īśvaram
BhP nānuvindanti te bhadram iha loke paratra ca
BhP ko yajñapuruṣo nāma yatra vo bhaktir īdṛśī
BhP bhartṛsnehavidūrāṇāṃ yathā jāre kuyoṣitām
BhP viṣṇur viriñco giriśa indro vāyur yamo raviḥ
BhP parjanyo dhanadaḥ somaḥ kṣitir agnir apāmpatiḥ
BhP ete cānye ca vibudhāḥ prabhavo varaśāpayoḥ
BhP dehe bhavanti nṛpateḥ sarvadevamayo nṛpaḥ
BhP tasmān māṃ karmabhir viprā yajadhvaṃ gatamatsarāḥ
BhP baliṃ ca mahyaṃ harata matto 'nyaḥ ko 'grabhuk pumān
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP itthaṃ viparyayamatiḥ pāpīyān utpathaṃ gataḥ
BhP anunīyamānas tadyācñāṃ na cakre bhraṣṭamaṅgalaḥ
BhP iti te 'satkṛtās tena dvijāḥ paṇḍitamāninā
BhP bhagnāyāṃ bhavyayācñāyāṃ tasmai vidura cukrudhuḥ
BhP hanyatāṃ hanyatām eṣa pāpaḥ prakṛtidāruṇaḥ
BhP jīvan jagad asāv āśu kurute bhasmasād dhruvam
BhP nāyam arhaty asadvṛtto naradevavarāsanam
BhP yo 'dhiyajñapatiṃ viṣṇuṃ vinindaty anapatrapaḥ
BhP ko vainaṃ paricakṣīta venam ekam ṛte 'śubham
BhP prāpta īdṛśam aiśvaryaṃ yadanugrahabhājanaḥ
BhP itthaṃ vyavasitā hantum ṛṣayo rūḍhamanyavaḥ
BhP nijaghnur huṅkṛtair venaṃ hatam acyutanindayā
BhP ṛṣibhiḥ svāśramapadaṃ gate putrakalevaram
BhP sunīthā pālayām āsa vidyāyogena śocatī
BhP ekadā munayas te tu sarasvatsalilāplutāḥ
BhP hutvāgnīn satkathāś cakrur upaviṣṭāḥ sarittaṭe
BhP vīkṣyotthitāṃs tadotpātān āhur lokabhayaṅkarān
BhP apy abhadram anāthāyā dasyubhyo na bhaved bhuvaḥ
BhP evaṃ mṛśanta ṛṣayo dhāvatāṃ sarvatodiśam
BhP pāṃsuḥ samutthito bhūriś corāṇām abhilumpatām
BhP tad upadravam ājñāya lokasya vasu lumpatām
BhP bhartary uparate tasminn anyonyaṃ ca jighāṃsatām
BhP coraprāyaṃ janapadaṃ hīnasattvam arājakam
BhP lokān nāvārayañ chaktā api taddoṣadarśinaḥ
BhP brāhmaṇaḥ samadṛk śānto dīnānāṃ samupekṣakaḥ
BhP sravate brahma tasyāpi bhinnabhāṇḍāt payo yathā
BhP nāṅgasya vaṃśo rājarṣer eṣa saṃsthātum arhati
BhP amoghavīryā hi nṛpā vaṃśe 'smin keśavāśrayāḥ
BhP viniścityaivam ṛṣayo vipannasya mahīpateḥ
BhP mamanthur ūruṃ tarasā tatrāsīd bāhuko naraḥ
BhP kākakṛṣṇo 'tihrasvāṅgo hrasvabāhur mahāhanuḥ
BhP hrasvapān nimnanāsāgro raktākṣas tāmramūrdhajaḥ
BhP taṃ tu te 'vanataṃ dīnaṃ kiṃ karomīti vādinam
BhP niṣīdety abruvaṃs tāta sa niṣādas tato 'bhavat
BhP tasya vaṃśyās tu naiṣādā girikānanagocarāḥ
BhP yenāharaj jāyamāno venakalmaṣam ulbaṇam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP atha tasya punar viprair aputrasya mahīpateḥ
BhP bāhubhyāṃ mathyamānābhyāṃ mithunaṃ samapadyata
BhP tad dṛṣṭvā mithunaṃ jātam ṛṣayo brahmavādinaḥ
BhP ūcuḥ paramasantuṣṭā viditvā bhagavatkalām
BhP ṛṣaya ūcuḥ
BhP eṣa viṣṇor bhagavataḥ kalā bhuvanapālinī
BhP iyaṃ ca lakṣmyāḥ sambhūtiḥ puruṣasyānapāyinī
BhP ayaṃ tu prathamo rājñāṃ pumān prathayitā yaśaḥ
BhP pṛthur nāma mahārājo bhaviṣyati pṛthuśravāḥ
BhP iyaṃ ca sudatī devī guṇabhūṣaṇabhūṣaṇā
BhP arcir nāma varārohā pṛthum evāvarundhatī
BhP eṣa sākṣād dharer aṃśojāto lokarirakṣayā
BhP iyaṃ ca tatparā hi śrīr anujajñe 'napāyinī
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP praśaṃsanti sma taṃ viprā gandharvapravarā jaguḥ
BhP mumucuḥ sumanodhārāḥ siddhā nṛtyanti svaḥstriyaḥ
BhP śaṅkhatūryamṛdaṅgādyā nedur dundubhayo divi
BhP tatra sarva upājagmur devarṣipitṝṇāṃ gaṇāḥ
BhP brahmā jagadgurur devaiḥ sahāsṛtya sureśvaraiḥ
BhP vainyasya dakṣiṇe haste dṛṣṭvā cihnaṃ gadābhṛtaḥ
BhP pādayor aravindaṃ ca taṃ vai mene hareḥ kalām
BhP yasyāpratihataṃ cakram aṃśaḥ sa parameṣṭhinaḥ
BhP tasyābhiṣeka ārabdho brāhmaṇair brahmavādibhiḥ
BhP ābhiṣecanikāny asmai ājahruḥ sarvato janāḥ
BhP saritsamudrā girayo nāgā gāvaḥ khagā mṛgāḥ
BhP dyauḥ kṣitiḥ sarvabhūtāni samājahrur upāyanam
BhP so 'bhiṣikto mahārājaḥ suvāsāḥ sādhvalaṅkṛtaḥ
BhP patnyārciṣālaṅkṛtayā vireje 'gnir ivāparaḥ
BhP tasmai jahāra dhanado haimaṃ vīra varāsanam
BhP varuṇaḥ salilasrāvam ātapatraṃ śaśiprabham
BhP vāyuś ca vālavyajane dharmaḥ kīrtimayīṃ srajam
BhP indraḥ kirīṭam utkṛṣṭaṃ daṇḍaṃ saṃyamanaṃ yamaḥ
BhP brahmā brahmamayaṃ varma bhāratī hāram uttamam
BhP hariḥ sudarśanaṃ cakraṃ tatpatny avyāhatāṃ śriyam
BhP daśacandram asiṃ rudraḥ śatacandraṃ tathāmbikā
BhP somo 'mṛtamayān aśvāṃs tvaṣṭā rūpāśrayaṃ ratham
BhP agnir ājagavaṃ cāpaṃ sūryo raśmimayān iṣūn
BhP bhūḥ pāduke yogamayyau dyauḥ puṣpāvalim anvaham
BhP nāṭyaṃ sugītaṃ vāditram antardhānaṃ ca khecarāḥ
BhP ṛṣayaś cāśiṣaḥ satyāḥ samudraḥ śaṅkham ātmajam
BhP sindhavaḥ parvatā nadyo rathavīthīr mahātmanaḥ
BhP sūto 'tha māgadho vandī taṃ stotum upatasthire
BhP stāvakāṃs tān abhipretya pṛthur vainyaḥ pratāpavān
BhP meghanirhrādayā vācā prahasann idam abravīt
BhP pṛthur uvāca
BhP bhoḥ sūta he māgadha saumya vandin loke 'dhunāspaṣṭaguṇasya me syāt
BhP kim āśrayo me stava eṣa yojyatāṃ mā mayy abhūvan vitathā giro vaḥ
BhP tasmāt parokṣe 'smadupaśrutāny alaṃ kariṣyatha stotram apīcyavācaḥ
BhP saty uttamaślokaguṇānuvāde jugupsitaṃ na stavayanti sabhyāḥ
BhP mahadguṇān ātmani kartum īśaḥ kaḥ stāvakaiḥ stāvayate 'sato 'pi
BhP te 'syābhaviṣyann iti vipralabdho janāvahāsaṃ kumatir na veda
BhP prabhavo hy ātmanaḥ stotraṃjugupsanty api viśrutāḥ
BhP hrīmantaḥ paramodārāḥ pauruṣaṃ vā vigarhitam
BhP vayaṃ tv aviditā loke sūtādyāpi varīmabhiḥ
BhP karmabhiḥ katham ātmānaṃ gāpayiṣyāma bālavat
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti bruvāṇaṃ nṛpatiṃ gāyakā municoditāḥ
BhP tuṣṭuvus tuṣṭamanasas tadvāgamṛtasevayā
BhP nālaṃ vayaṃ te mahimānuvarṇane yo devavaryo 'vatatāra māyayā
BhP venāṅgajātasya ca pauruṣāṇi te vācaspatīnām api babhramur dhiyaḥ
BhP athāpy udāraśravasaḥ pṛthor hareḥ kalāvatārasya kathāmṛtādṛtāḥ
BhP yathopadeśaṃ munibhiḥ pracoditāḥ ślāghyāni karmāṇi vayaṃ vitanmahi
BhP eṣa dharmabhṛtāṃ śreṣṭho lokaṃ dharme 'nuvartayan
BhP goptā ca dharmasetūnāṃ śāstā tatparipanthinām
BhP eṣa vai lokapālānāṃ bibharty ekas tanau tanūḥ
BhP kāle kāle yathābhāgaṃ lokayor ubhayor hitam
BhP vasu kāla upādatte kāle cāyaṃ vimuñcati
BhP samaḥ sarveṣu bhūteṣu pratapan sūryavad vibhuḥ
BhP titikṣaty akramaṃ vainya upary ākramatām api
BhP bhūtānāṃ karuṇaḥ śaśvad ārtānāṃ kṣitivṛttimān
BhP deve 'varṣaty asau devo naradevavapur hariḥ
BhP kṛcchraprāṇāḥ prajā hy eṣa rakṣiṣyaty añjasendravat
BhP āpyāyayaty asau lokaṃ vadanāmṛtamūrtinā
BhP sānurāgāvalokena viśadasmitacāruṇā
BhP avyaktavartmaiṣa nigūḍhakāryo gambhīravedhā upaguptavittaḥ
BhP anantamāhātmyaguṇaikadhāmā pṛthuḥ pracetā iva saṃvṛtātmā
BhP durāsado durviṣaha āsanno 'pi vidūravat
BhP naivābhibhavituṃ śakyo venāraṇyutthito 'nalaḥ
BhP antar bahiś ca bhūtānāṃ paśyan karmāṇi cāraṇaiḥ
BhP udāsīna ivādhyakṣo vāyur ātmeva dehinām
BhP nādaṇḍyaṃ daṇḍayaty eṣa sutam ātmadviṣām api
BhP daṇḍayaty ātmajam api daṇḍyaṃ dharmapathe sthitaḥ
BhP asyāpratihataṃ cakraṃ pṛthor āmānasācalāt
BhP vartate bhagavān arko yāvat tapati gogaṇaiḥ
BhP rañjayiṣyati yal lokam ayam ātmaviceṣṭitaiḥ
BhP athāmum āhū rājānaṃ manorañjanakaiḥ prajāḥ
BhP dṛḍhavrataḥ satyasandho brahmaṇyo vṛddhasevakaḥ
BhP śaraṇyaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ mānado dīnavatsalaḥ
BhP mātṛbhaktiḥ parastrīṣu patnyām ardha ivātmanaḥ
BhP prajāsu pitṛvat snigdhaḥ kiṅkaro brahmavādinām
BhP dehinām ātmavatpreṣṭhaḥ suhṛdāṃ nandivardhanaḥ
BhP muktasaṅgaprasaṅgo 'yaṃ daṇḍapāṇir asādhuṣu
BhP ayaṃ tu sākṣād bhagavāṃs tryadhīśaḥ kūṭastha ātmā kalayāvatīrṇaḥ
BhP yasminn avidyāracitaṃ nirarthakaṃ paśyanti nānātvam api pratītam
BhP ayaṃ bhuvo maṇḍalam odayādrer goptaikavīro naradevanāthaḥ
BhP āsthāya jaitraṃ ratham āttacāpaḥ paryasyate dakṣiṇato yathārkaḥ
BhP asmai nṛpālāḥ kila tatra tatra baliṃ hariṣyanti salokapālāḥ
BhP maṃsyanta eṣāṃ striya ādirājaṃ cakrāyudhaṃ tadyaśa uddharantyaḥ
BhP ayaṃ mahīṃ gāṃ duduhe 'dhirājaḥ prajāpatir vṛttikaraḥ prajānām
BhP yo līlayādrīn svaśarāsakoṭyā bhindan samāṃ gām akarod yathendraḥ
BhP visphūrjayann ājagavaṃ dhanuḥ svayaṃ yadācarat kṣmām aviṣahyam ājau
BhP tadā nililyur diśi diśy asanto lāṅgūlam udyamya yathā mṛgendraḥ
BhP eṣo 'śvamedhāñ śatam ājahāra sarasvatī prādurabhāvi yatra
BhP ahārṣīd yasya hayaṃ purandaraḥ śatakratuś carame vartamāne
BhP eṣa svasadmopavane sametya sanatkumāraṃ bhagavantam ekam
BhP ārādhya bhaktyālabhatāmalaṃ taj jñānaṃ yato brahma paraṃ vidanti
BhP tatra tatra giras tās tā iti viśrutavikramaḥ
BhP śroṣyaty ātmāśritā gāthāḥ pṛthuḥ pṛthuparākramaḥ
BhP diśo vijityāpratiruddhacakraḥ svatejasotpāṭitalokaśalyaḥ
BhP surāsurendrair upagīyamāna mahānubhāvo bhavitā patir bhuvaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ sa bhagavān vainyaḥ khyāpito guṇakarmabhiḥ
BhP chandayām āsa tān kāmaiḥ pratipūjyābhinandya ca
BhP brāhmaṇapramukhān varṇān bhṛtyāmātyapurodhasaḥ
BhP paurān jānapadān śreṇīḥ prakṛtīḥ samapūjayat
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP kasmād dadhāra gorūpaṃ dharitrī bahurūpiṇī
BhP yāṃ dudoha pṛthus tatra ko vatso dohanaṃ ca kim
BhP prakṛtyā viṣamā devī kṛtā tena samā katham
BhP tasya medhyaṃ hayaṃ devaḥ kasya hetor apāharat
BhP sanatkumārād bhagavato brahman brahmaviduttamāt
BhP labdhvā jñānaṃ savijñānaṃ rājarṣiḥ kāṃ gatiṃ gataḥ
BhP yac cānyad api kṛṣṇasya bhavān bhagavataḥ prabhoḥ
BhP śravaḥ suśravasaḥ puṇyaṃ pūrvadehakathāśrayam
BhP bhaktāya me 'nuraktāya tava cādhokṣajasya ca
BhP vaktum arhasi yo 'duhyad vainyarūpeṇa gām imām
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP codito vidureṇaivaṃ vāsudevakathāṃ prati
BhP praśasya taṃ prītamanā maitreyaḥ pratyabhāṣata
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP yadābhiṣiktaḥ pṛthur aṅga viprair āmantrito janatāyāś ca pālaḥ
BhP prajā niranne kṣitipṛṣṭha etya kṣutkṣāmadehāḥ patim abhyavocan
BhP vayaṃ rājañ jāṭhareṇābhitaptā yathāgninā koṭarasthena vṛkṣāḥ
BhP tvām adya yātāḥ śaraṇaṃ śaraṇyaṃ yaḥ sādhito vṛttikaraḥ patir naḥ
BhP tan no bhavān īhatu rātave 'nnaṃ kṣudhārditānāṃ naradevadeva
BhP yāvan na naṅkṣyāmaha ujjhitorjā vārtāpatis tvaṃ kila lokapālaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP pṛthuḥ prajānāṃ karuṇaṃ niśamya paridevitam
BhP dīrghaṃ dadhyau kuruśreṣṭha nimittaṃ so 'nvapadyata
BhP iti vyavasito buddhyā pragṛhītaśarāsanaḥ
BhP sandadhe viśikhaṃ bhūmeḥ kruddhas tripurahā yathā
BhP pravepamānā dharaṇī niśāmyodāyudhaṃ ca tam
BhP gauḥ saty apādravad bhītā mṛgīva mṛgayudrutā
BhP tām anvadhāvat tad vainyaḥ kupito 'tyaruṇekṣaṇaḥ
BhP śaraṃ dhanuṣi sandhāya yatra yatra palāyate
BhP sā diśo vidiśo devī rodasī cāntaraṃ tayoḥ
BhP dhāvantī tatra tatrainaṃ dadarśānūdyatāyudham
BhP loke nāvindata trāṇaṃ vainyān mṛtyor iva prajāḥ
BhP trastā tadā nivavṛte hṛdayena vidūyatā
BhP uvāca ca mahābhāgaṃ dharmajñāpannavatsala
BhP trāhi mām api bhūtānāṃ pālane 'vasthito bhavān
BhP sa tvaṃ jighāṃsase kasmād dīnām akṛtakilbiṣām
BhP ahaniṣyat kathaṃ yoṣāṃ dharmajña iti yo mataḥ
BhP praharanti na vai strīṣu kṛtāgaḥsv api jantavaḥ
BhP kim uta tvadvidhā rājan karuṇā dīnavatsalāḥ
BhP māṃ vipāṭyājarāṃ nāvaṃ yatra viśvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam
BhP ātmānaṃ ca prajāś cemāḥ katham ambhasi dhāsyasi
BhP pṛthur uvāca
BhP vasudhe tvāṃ vadhiṣyāmi macchāsanaparāṅmukhīm
BhP bhāgaṃ barhiṣi yā vṛṅkte na tanoti ca no vasu
BhP yavasaṃ jagdhy anudinaṃ naiva dogdhy audhasaṃ payaḥ
BhP tasyām evaṃ hi duṣṭāyāṃ daṇḍo nātra na śasyate
BhP tvaṃ khalv oṣadhibījāni prāk sṛṣṭāni svayambhuvā
BhP na muñcasy ātmaruddhāni mām avajñāya mandadhīḥ
BhP amūṣāṃ kṣutparītānām ārtānāṃ paridevitam
BhP śamayiṣyāmi madbāṇair bhinnāyās tava medasā
BhP pumān yoṣid uta klība ātmasambhāvano 'dhamaḥ
BhP bhūteṣu niranukrośo nṛpāṇāṃ tadvadho 'vadhaḥ
BhP tvāṃ stabdhāṃ durmadāṃ nītvā māyāgāṃ tilaśaḥ śaraiḥ
BhP ātmayogabalenemā dhārayiṣyāmy ahaṃ prajāḥ
BhP evaṃ manyumayīṃ mūrtiṃ kṛtāntam iva bibhratam
BhP praṇatā prāñjaliḥ prāha mahī sañjātavepathuḥ
BhP dharovāca
BhP namaḥ parasmai puruṣāya māyayā vinyastanānātanave guṇātmane
BhP namaḥ svarūpānubhavena nirdhuta dravyakriyākārakavibhramormaye
BhP yenāham ātmāyatanaṃ vinirmitā dhātrā yato 'yaṃ guṇasargasaṅgrahaḥ
BhP sa eva māṃ hantum udāyudhaḥ svarāḍ upasthito 'nyaṃ śaraṇaṃ kam āśraye
BhP ya etad ādāv asṛjac carācaraṃ svamāyayātmāśrayayāvitarkyayā
BhP tayaiva so 'yaṃ kila goptum udyataḥ kathaṃ nu māṃ dharmaparo jighāṃsati
BhP nūnaṃ bateśasya samīhitaṃ janais tanmāyayā durjayayākṛtātmabhiḥ
BhP na lakṣyate yas tv akarod akārayad yo 'neka ekaḥ parataś ca īśvaraḥ
BhP sargādi yo 'syānuruṇaddhi śaktibhir dravyakriyākārakacetanātmabhiḥ
BhP tasmai samunnaddhaniruddhaśaktaye namaḥ parasmai puruṣāya vedhase
BhP sa vai bhavān ātmavinirmitaṃ jagad bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇātmakaṃ vibho
BhP saṃsthāpayiṣyann aja māṃ rasātalād abhyujjahārāmbhasa ādisūkaraḥ
BhP apām upasthe mayi nāvy avasthitāḥ prajā bhavān adya rirakṣiṣuḥ kila
BhP sa vīramūrtiḥ samabhūd dharādharo yo māṃ payasy ugraśaro jighāṃsasi
BhP nūnaṃ janair īhitam īśvarāṇām asmadvidhais tadguṇasargamāyayā
BhP na jñāyate mohitacittavartmabhis tebhyo namo vīrayaśaskarebhyaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP itthaṃ pṛthum abhiṣṭūya ruṣā prasphuritādharam
BhP punar āhāvanir bhītā saṃstabhyātmānam ātmanā
BhP sanniyacchābhibho manyuṃ nibodha śrāvitaṃ ca me
BhP sarvataḥ sāram ādatte yathā madhukaro budhaḥ
BhP asmin loke 'thavāmuṣmin munibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ
BhP dṛṣṭā yogāḥ prayuktāś ca puṃsāṃ śreyaḥprasiddhaye
BhP tān ātiṣṭhati yaḥ samyag upāyān pūrvadarśitān
BhP avaraḥ śraddhayopeta upeyān vindate 'ñjasā
BhP tān anādṛtya yo 'vidvān arthān ārabhate svayam
BhP tasya vyabhicaranty arthā ārabdhāś ca punaḥ punaḥ
BhP purā sṛṣṭā hy oṣadhayo brahmaṇā yā viśāmpate
BhP bhujyamānā mayā dṛṣṭā asadbhir adhṛtavrataiḥ
BhP apālitānādṛtā ca bhavadbhir lokapālakaiḥ
BhP corībhūte 'tha loke 'haṃ yajñārthe 'grasam oṣadhīḥ
BhP nūnaṃ tā vīrudhaḥ kṣīṇā mayi kālena bhūyasā
BhP tatra yogena dṛṣṭena bhavān ādātum arhati
BhP vatsaṃ kalpaya me vīra yenāhaṃ vatsalā tava
BhP dhokṣye kṣīramayān kāmān anurūpaṃ ca dohanam
BhP dogdhāraṃ ca mahābāho bhūtānāṃ bhūtabhāvana
BhP annam īpsitam ūrjasvad bhagavān vāñchate yadi
BhP samāṃ ca kuru māṃ rājan devavṛṣṭaṃ yathā payaḥ
BhP apartāv api bhadraṃ te upāvarteta me vibho
BhP iti priyaṃ hitaṃ vākyaṃ bhuva ādāya bhūpatiḥ
BhP vatsaṃ kṛtvā manuṃ pāṇāv aduhat sakalauṣadhīḥ
BhP tathāpare ca sarvatra sāram ādadate budhāḥ
BhP tato 'nye ca yathākāmaṃ duduhuḥ pṛthubhāvitām
BhP ṛṣayo duduhur devīm indriyeṣv atha sattama
BhP vatsaṃ bṛhaspatiṃ kṛtvā payaś chandomayaṃ śuci
BhP kṛtvā vatsaṃ suragaṇā indraṃ somam adūduhan
BhP hiraṇmayena pātreṇa vīryam ojo balaṃ payaḥ
BhP daiteyā dānavā vatsaṃ prahlādam asurarṣabham
BhP vidhāyādūduhan kṣīram ayaḥpātre surāsavam
BhP gandharvāpsaraso 'dhukṣan pātre padmamaye payaḥ
BhP vatsaṃ viśvāvasuṃ kṛtvā gāndharvaṃ madhu saubhagam
BhP vatsena pitaro 'ryamṇā kavyaṃ kṣīram adhukṣata
BhP āmapātre mahābhāgāḥ śraddhayā śrāddhadevatāḥ
BhP prakalpya vatsaṃ kapilaṃ siddhāḥ saṅkalpanāmayīm
BhP siddhiṃ nabhasi vidyāṃ ca ye ca vidyādharādayaḥ
BhP anye ca māyino māyām antardhānādbhutātmanām
BhP mayaṃ prakalpya vatsaṃ te duduhur dhāraṇāmayīm
BhP yakṣarakṣāṃsi bhūtāni piśācāḥ piśitāśanāḥ
BhP bhūteśavatsā duduhuḥ kapāle kṣatajāsavam
BhP tathāhayo dandaśūkāḥ sarpā nāgāś ca takṣakam
BhP vidhāya vatsaṃ duduhur bilapātre viṣaṃ payaḥ
BhP paśavo yavasaṃ kṣīraṃ vatsaṃ kṛtvā ca govṛṣam
BhP araṇyapātre cādhukṣan mṛgendreṇa ca daṃṣṭriṇaḥ
BhP kravyādāḥ prāṇinaḥ kravyaṃ duduhuḥ sve kalevare
BhP suparṇavatsā vihagāś caraṃ cācaram eva ca
BhP vaṭavatsā vanaspatayaḥ pṛthag rasamayaṃ payaḥ
BhP girayo himavadvatsā nānādhātūn svasānuṣu
BhP sarve svamukhyavatsena sve sve pātre pṛthak payaḥ
BhP sarvakāmadughāṃ pṛthvīṃ duduhuḥ pṛthubhāvitām
BhP evaṃ pṛthvādayaḥ pṛthvīm annādāḥ svannam ātmanaḥ
BhP dohavatsādibhedena kṣīrabhedaṃ kurūdvaha
BhP tato mahīpatiḥ prītaḥ sarvakāmadughāṃ pṛthuḥ
BhP duhitṛtve cakāremāṃ premṇā duhitṛvatsalaḥ
BhP cūrṇayan svadhanuṣkoṭyā girikūṭāni rājarāṭ
BhP bhūmaṇḍalam idaṃ vainyaḥ prāyaś cakre samaṃ vibhuḥ
BhP athāsmin bhagavān vainyaḥ prajānāṃ vṛttidaḥ pitā
BhP nivāsān kalpayāṃ cakre tatra tatra yathārhataḥ
BhP grāmān puraḥ pattanāni durgāṇi vividhāni ca
BhP ghoṣān vrajān saśibirān ākarān kheṭakharvaṭān
BhP prāk pṛthor iha naivaiṣā puragrāmādikalpanā
BhP yathāsukhaṃ vasanti sma tatra tatrākutobhayāḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP athādīkṣata rājā tu hayamedhaśatena saḥ
BhP brahmāvarte manoḥ kṣetre yatra prācī sarasvatī
BhP tad abhipretya bhagavān karmātiśayam ātmanaḥ
BhP śatakratur na mamṛṣe pṛthor yajñamahotsavam
BhP yatra yajñapatiḥ sākṣād bhagavān harir īśvaraḥ
BhP anvabhūyata sarvātmā sarvalokaguruḥ prabhuḥ
BhP anvito brahmaśarvābhyāṃ lokapālaiḥ sahānugaiḥ
BhP upagīyamāno gandharvair munibhiś cāpsarogaṇaiḥ
BhP siddhā vidyādharā daityā dānavā guhyakādayaḥ
BhP sunandanandapramukhāḥ pārṣadapravarā hareḥ
BhP kapilo nārado datto yogeśāḥ sanakādayaḥ
BhP tam anvīyur bhāgavatā ye ca tatsevanotsukāḥ
BhP yatra dharmadughā bhūmiḥ sarvakāmadughā satī
BhP dogdhi smābhīpsitān arthān yajamānasya bhārata
BhP ūhuḥ sarvarasān nadyaḥ kṣīradadhyannagorasān
BhP taravo bhūrivarṣmāṇaḥ prāsūyanta madhucyutaḥ
BhP sindhavo ratnanikarān girayo 'nnaṃ caturvidham
BhP upāyanam upājahruḥ sarve lokāḥ sapālakāḥ
BhP iti cādhokṣajeśasya pṛthos tu paramodayam
BhP asūyan bhagavān indraḥ pratighātam acīkarat
BhP carameṇāśvamedhena yajamāne yajuṣpatim
BhP vainye yajñapaśuṃ spardhann apovāha tirohitaḥ
BhP tam atrir bhagavān aikṣat tvaramāṇaṃ vihāyasā
BhP āmuktam iva pākhaṇḍaṃ yo 'dharme dharmavibhramaḥ
BhP atriṇā codito hantuṃ pṛthuputro mahārathaḥ
BhP anvadhāvata saṅkruddhas tiṣṭha tiṣṭheti cābravīt
BhP taṃ tādṛśākṛtiṃ vīkṣya mene dharmaṃ śarīriṇam
BhP jaṭilaṃ bhasmanācchannaṃ tasmai bāṇaṃ na muñcati
BhP vadhān nivṛttaṃ taṃ bhūyo hantave 'trir acodayat
BhP jahi yajñahanaṃ tāta mahendraṃ vibudhādhamam
BhP evaṃ vainyasutaḥ proktas tvaramāṇaṃ vihāyasā
BhP anvadravad abhikruddho rāvaṇaṃ gṛdhrarāḍ iva
BhP so 'śvaṃ rūpaṃ ca tad dhitvā tasmā antarhitaḥ svarāṭ
BhP vīraḥ svapaśum ādāya pitur yajñam upeyivān
BhP tat tasya cādbhutaṃ karma vicakṣya paramarṣayaḥ
BhP nāmadheyaṃ dadus tasmai vijitāśva iti prabho
BhP upasṛjya tamas tīvraṃ jahārāśvaṃ punar hariḥ
BhP caṣālayūpataś channo hiraṇyaraśanaṃ vibhuḥ
BhP atriḥ sandarśayām āsa tvaramāṇaṃ vihāyasā
BhP kapālakhaṭvāṅgadharaṃ vīro nainam abādhata
BhP atriṇā coditas tasmai sandadhe viśikhaṃ ruṣā
BhP so 'śvaṃ rūpaṃ ca tad dhitvā tasthāv antarhitaḥ svarāṭ
BhP vīraś cāśvam upādāya pitṛyajñam athāvrajat
BhP tad avadyaṃ hare rūpaṃ jagṛhur jñānadurbalāḥ
BhP yāni rūpāṇi jagṛhe indro hayajihīrṣayā
BhP tāni pāpasya khaṇḍāni liṅgaṃ khaṇḍam ihocyate
BhP evam indre haraty aśvaṃ vainyayajñajighāṃsayā
BhP tadgṛhītavisṛṣṭeṣu pākhaṇḍeṣu matir nṛṇām
BhP dharma ity upadharmeṣu nagnaraktapaṭādiṣu
BhP prāyeṇa sajjate bhrāntyā peśaleṣu ca vāgmiṣu
BhP tad abhijñāya bhagavān pṛthuḥ pṛthuparākramaḥ
BhP indrāya kupito bāṇam ādattodyatakārmukaḥ
BhP tam ṛtvijaḥ śakravadhābhisandhitaṃ vicakṣya duṣprekṣyam asahyaraṃhasam
BhP nivārayām āsur aho mahāmate na yujyate 'trānyavadhaḥ pracoditāt
BhP vayaṃ marutvantam ihārthanāśanaṃ hvayāmahe tvacchravasā hatatviṣam
BhP ayātayāmopahavair anantaraṃ prasahya rājan juhavāma te 'hitam
BhP ity āmantrya kratupatiṃ vidurāsyartvijo ruṣā
BhP srugghastān juhvato 'bhyetya svayambhūḥ pratyaṣedhata
BhP na vadhyo bhavatām indro yad yajño bhagavattanuḥ
BhP yaṃ jighāṃsatha yajñena yasyeṣṭās tanavaḥ surāḥ
BhP tad idaṃ paśyata mahad dharmavyatikaraṃ dvijāḥ
BhP indreṇānuṣṭhitaṃ rājñaḥ karmaitad vijighāṃsatā
BhP pṛthukīrteḥ pṛthor bhūyāt tarhy ekonaśatakratuḥ
BhP alaṃ te kratubhiḥ sviṣṭair yad bhavān mokṣadharmavit
BhP naivātmane mahendrāya roṣam āhartum arhasi
BhP ubhāv api hi bhadraṃ te uttamaślokavigrahau
BhP māsmin mahārāja kṛthāḥ sma cintāṃ niśāmayāsmadvaca ādṛtātmā
BhP yad dhyāyato daivahataṃ nu kartuṃ mano 'tiruṣṭaṃ viśate tamo 'ndham
BhP kratur viramatām eṣa deveṣu duravagrahaḥ
BhP dharmavyatikaro yatra pākhaṇḍair indranirmitaiḥ
BhP ebhir indropasaṃsṛṣṭaiḥ pākhaṇḍair hāribhir janam
BhP hriyamāṇaṃ vicakṣvainaṃ yas te yajñadhrug aśvamuṭ
BhP bhavān paritrātum ihāvatīrṇo dharmaṃ janānāṃ samayānurūpam
BhP venāpacārād avaluptam adya taddehato viṣṇukalāsi vainya
BhP sa tvaṃ vimṛśyāsya bhavaṃ prajāpate saṅkalpanaṃ viśvasṛjāṃ pipīpṛhi
BhP aindrīṃ ca māyām upadharmamātaraṃ pracaṇḍapākhaṇḍapathaṃ prabho jahi
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP itthaṃ sa lokaguruṇā samādiṣṭo viśāmpatiḥ
BhP tathā ca kṛtvā vātsalyaṃ maghonāpi ca sandadhe
BhP kṛtāvabhṛthasnānāya pṛthave bhūrikarmaṇe
BhP varān dadus te varadā ye tadbarhiṣi tarpitāḥ
BhP viprāḥ satyāśiṣas tuṣṭāḥ śraddhayā labdhadakṣiṇāḥ
BhP āśiṣo yuyujuḥ kṣattar ādirājāya satkṛtāḥ
BhP tvayāhūtā mahābāho sarva eva samāgatāḥ
BhP pūjitā dānamānābhyāṃ pitṛdevarṣimānavāḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP bhagavān api vaikuṇṭhaḥ sākaṃ maghavatā vibhuḥ
BhP yajñair yajñapatis tuṣṭo yajñabhuk tam abhāṣata
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP eṣa te 'kārṣīd bhaṅgaṃ hayamedhaśatasya ha
BhP kṣamāpayata ātmānam amuṣya kṣantum arhasi
BhP sudhiyaḥ sādhavo loke naradeva narottamāḥ
BhP nābhidruhyanti bhūtebhyo yarhi nātmā kalevaram
BhP puruṣā yadi muhyanti tvādṛśā devamāyayā
BhP śrama eva paraṃ jāto dīrghayā vṛddhasevayā
BhP ataḥ kāyam imaṃ vidvān avidyākāmakarmabhiḥ
BhP ārabdha iti naivāsmin pratibuddho 'nuṣajjate
BhP asaṃsaktaḥ śarīre 'sminn amunotpādite gṛhe
BhP apatye draviṇe vāpi kaḥ kuryān mamatāṃ budhaḥ
BhP ekaḥ śuddhaḥ svayaṃjyotir nirguṇo 'sau guṇāśrayaḥ
BhP sarvago 'nāvṛtaḥ sākṣī nirātmātmātmanaḥ paraḥ
BhP ya evaṃ santam ātmānam ātmasthaṃ veda pūruṣaḥ
BhP nājyate prakṛtistho 'pi tadguṇaiḥ sa mayi sthitaḥ
BhP yaḥ svadharmeṇa māṃ nityaṃ nirāśīḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ
BhP bhajate śanakais tasya mano rājan prasīdati
BhP parityaktaguṇaḥ samyag darśano viśadāśayaḥ
BhP śāntiṃ me samavasthānaṃ brahma kaivalyam aśnute
BhP udāsīnam ivādhyakṣaṃ dravyajñānakriyātmanām
BhP kūṭastham imam ātmānaṃ yo vedāpnoti śobhanam
BhP bhinnasya liṅgasya guṇapravāho dravyakriyākārakacetanātmanaḥ
BhP dṛṣṭāsu sampatsu vipatsu sūrayo na vikriyante mayi baddhasauhṛdāḥ
BhP samaḥ samānottamamadhyamādhamaḥ sukhe ca duḥkhe ca jitendriyāśayaḥ
BhP mayopakḷptākhilalokasaṃyuto vidhatsva vīrākhilalokarakṣaṇam
BhP śreyaḥ prajāpālanam eva rājño yat sāmparāye sukṛtāt ṣaṣṭham aṃśam
BhP hartānyathā hṛtapuṇyaḥ prajānām arakṣitā karahāro 'gham atti
BhP evaṃ dvijāgryānumatānuvṛtta dharmapradhāno 'nyatamo 'vitāsyāḥ
BhP hrasvena kālena gṛhopayātān draṣṭāsi siddhān anuraktalokaḥ
BhP varaṃ ca mat kañcana mānavendra vṛṇīṣva te 'haṃ guṇaśīlayantritaḥ
BhP nāhaṃ makhair vai sulabhas tapobhir yogena vā yat samacittavartī
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sa itthaṃ lokaguruṇā viṣvaksenena viśvajit
BhP anuśāsita ādeśaṃ śirasā jagṛhe hareḥ
BhP spṛśantaṃ pādayoḥ premṇā vrīḍitaṃ svena karmaṇā
BhP śatakratuṃ pariṣvajya vidveṣaṃ visasarja ha
BhP bhagavān atha viśvātmā pṛthunopahṛtārhaṇaḥ
BhP samujjihānayā bhaktyā gṛhītacaraṇāmbujaḥ
BhP prasthānābhimukho 'py enam anugrahavilambitaḥ
BhP paśyan padmapalāśākṣo na pratasthe suhṛt satām
BhP sa ādirājo racitāñjalir hariṃ vilokituṃ nāśakad aśrulocanaḥ
BhP na kiñcanovāca sa bāṣpaviklavo hṛdopaguhyāmum adhād avasthitaḥ
BhP athāvamṛjyāśrukalā vilokayann atṛptadṛggocaram āha pūruṣam
BhP padā spṛśantaṃ kṣitim aṃsa unnate vinyastahastāgram uraṅgavidviṣaḥ
BhP pṛthur uvāca
BhP varān vibho tvad varadeśvarād budhaḥ kathaṃ vṛṇīte guṇavikriyātmanām
BhP ye nārakāṇām api santi dehināṃ tān īśa kaivalyapate vṛṇe na ca
BhP na kāmaye nātha tad apy ahaṃ kvacin na yatra yuṣmaccaraṇāmbujāsavaḥ
BhP mahattamāntarhṛdayān mukhacyuto vidhatsva karṇāyutam eṣa me varaḥ
BhP sa uttamaśloka mahanmukhacyuto bhavatpadāmbhojasudhā kaṇānilaḥ
BhP smṛtiṃ punar vismṛtatattvavartmanāṃ kuyogināṃ no vitaraty alaṃ varaiḥ
BhP yaśaḥ śivaṃ suśrava āryasaṅgame yadṛcchayā copaśṛṇoti te sakṛt
BhP kathaṃ guṇajño viramed vinā paśuṃ śrīr yat pravavre guṇasaṅgrahecchayā
BhP athābhaje tvākhilapūruṣottamaṃ guṇālayaṃ padmakareva lālasaḥ
BhP apy āvayor ekapatispṛdhoḥ kalir na syāt kṛtatvaccaraṇaikatānayoḥ
BhP jagajjananyāṃ jagadīśa vaiśasaṃ syād eva yatkarmaṇi naḥ samīhitam
BhP karoṣi phalgv apy uru dīnavatsalaḥ sva eva dhiṣṇye 'bhiratasya kiṃ tayā
BhP bhajanty atha tvām ata eva sādhavo vyudastamāyāguṇavibhramodayam
BhP bhavatpadānusmaraṇād ṛte satāṃ nimittam anyad bhagavan na vidmahe
BhP manye giraṃ te jagatāṃ vimohinīṃ varaṃ vṛṇīṣveti bhajantam āttha yat
BhP vācā nu tantyā yadi te jano 'sitaḥ kathaṃ punaḥ karma karoti mohitaḥ
BhP tvanmāyayāddhā jana īśa khaṇḍito yad anyad āśāsta ṛtātmano 'budhaḥ
BhP yathā cared bālahitaṃ pitā svayaṃ tathā tvam evārhasi naḥ samīhitum
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ity ādirājena nutaḥ sa viśvadṛk tam āha rājan mayi bhaktir astu te
BhP diṣṭyedṛśī dhīr mayi te kṛtā yayā māyāṃ madīyāṃ tarati sma dustyajām
BhP tat tvaṃ kuru mayādiṣṭam apramattaḥ prajāpate
BhP madādeśakaro lokaḥ sarvatrāpnoti śobhanam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti vainyasya rājarṣeḥ pratinandyārthavad vacaḥ
BhP pūjito 'nugṛhītvainaṃ gantuṃ cakre 'cyuto matim
BhP devarṣipitṛgandharva siddhacāraṇapannagāḥ
BhP kinnarāpsaraso martyāḥ khagā bhūtāny anekaśaḥ
BhP yajñeśvaradhiyā rājñā vāgvittāñjalibhaktitaḥ
BhP sabhājitā yayuḥ sarve vaikuṇṭhānugatās tataḥ
BhP bhagavān api rājarṣeḥ sopādhyāyasya cācyutaḥ
BhP harann iva mano 'muṣya svadhāma pratyapadyata
BhP adṛṣṭāya namaskṛtya nṛpaḥ sandarśitātmane
BhP avyaktāya ca devānāṃ devāya svapuraṃ yayau
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP mauktikaiḥ kusumasragbhir dukūlaiḥ svarṇatoraṇaiḥ
BhP mahāsurabhibhir dhūpair maṇḍitaṃ tatra tatra vai
BhP candanāgurutoyārdra rathyācatvaramārgavat
BhP puṣpākṣataphalais tokmair lājair arcirbhir arcitam
BhP savṛndaiḥ kadalīstambhaiḥ pūgapotaiḥ pariṣkṛtam
BhP tarupallavamālābhiḥ sarvataḥ samalaṅkṛtam
BhP prajās taṃ dīpabalibhiḥ sambhṛtāśeṣamaṅgalaiḥ
BhP abhīyur mṛṣṭakanyāś ca mṛṣṭakuṇḍalamaṇḍitāḥ
BhP śaṅkhadundubhighoṣeṇa brahmaghoṣeṇa cartvijām
BhP viveśa bhavanaṃ vīraḥ stūyamāno gatasmayaḥ
BhP pūjitaḥ pūjayām āsa tatra tatra mahāyaśāḥ
BhP paurāñ jānapadāṃs tāṃs tān prītaḥ priyavarapradaḥ
BhP sa evam ādīny anavadyaceṣṭitaḥ karmāṇi bhūyāṃsi mahān mahattamaḥ
BhP kurvan śaśāsāvanimaṇḍalaṃ yaśaḥ sphītaṃ nidhāyāruruhe paraṃ padam
BhP sūta uvāca
BhP tad ādirājasya yaśo vijṛmbhitaṃ guṇair aśeṣair guṇavatsabhājitam
BhP kṣattā mahābhāgavataḥ sadaspate kauṣāraviṃ prāha gṛṇantam arcayan
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP so 'bhiṣiktaḥ pṛthur viprair labdhāśeṣasurārhaṇaḥ
BhP bibhrat sa vaiṣṇavaṃ tejo bāhvor yābhyāṃ dudoha gām
BhP ko nv asya kīrtiṃ na śṛṇoty abhijño yadvikramocchiṣṭam aśeṣabhūpāḥ
BhP lokāḥ sapālā upajīvanti kāmam adyāpi tan me vada karma śuddham
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP gaṅgāyamunayor nadyor antarā kṣetram āvasan
BhP ārabdhān eva bubhuje bhogān puṇyajihāsayā
BhP sarvatrāskhalitādeśaḥ saptadvīpaikadaṇḍadhṛk
BhP anyatra brāhmaṇakulād anyatrācyutagotrataḥ
BhP ekadāsīn mahāsatra dīkṣā tatra divaukasām
BhP samājo brahmarṣīṇāṃ ca rājarṣīṇāṃ ca sattama
BhP tasminn arhatsu sarveṣu svarciteṣu yathārhataḥ
BhP utthitaḥ sadaso madhye tārāṇām uḍurāḍ iva
BhP prāṃśuḥ pīnāyatabhujo gauraḥ kañjāruṇekṣaṇaḥ
BhP sunāsaḥ sumukhaḥ saumyaḥ pīnāṃsaḥ sudvijasmitaḥ
BhP vyūḍhavakṣā bṛhacchroṇir valivalgudalodaraḥ
BhP āvartanābhir ojasvī kāñcanorur udagrapāt

BhP mahādhane dukūlāgrye paridhāyopavīya ca
BhP vyañjitāśeṣagātraśrīr niyame nyastabhūṣaṇaḥ
BhP kṛṣṇājinadharaḥ śrīmān kuśapāṇiḥ kṛtocitaḥ
BhP śiśirasnigdhatārākṣaḥ samaikṣata samantataḥ
BhP ūcivān idam urvīśaḥ sadaḥ saṃharṣayann iva
BhP cāru citrapadaṃ ślakṣṇaṃ mṛṣṭaṃ gūḍham aviklavam
BhP sarveṣām upakārārthaṃ tadā anuvadann iva
BhP rājovāca
BhP sabhyāḥ śṛṇuta bhadraṃ vaḥ sādhavo ya ihāgatāḥ
BhP satsu jijñāsubhir dharmam āvedyaṃ svamanīṣitam
BhP ahaṃ daṇḍadharo rājā prajānām iha yojitaḥ
BhP rakṣitā vṛttidaḥ sveṣu setuṣu sthāpitā pṛthak
BhP tasya me tadanuṣṭhānād yān āhur brahmavādinaḥ
BhP lokāḥ syuḥ kāmasandohā yasya tuṣyati diṣṭadṛk
BhP ya uddharet karaṃ rājā prajā dharmeṣv aśikṣayan
BhP prajānāṃ śamalaṃ bhuṅkte bhagaṃ ca svaṃ jahāti saḥ
BhP tat prajā bhartṛpiṇḍārthaṃ svārtham evānasūyavaḥ
BhP kurutādhokṣajadhiyas tarhi me 'nugrahaḥ kṛtaḥ
BhP yūyaṃ tad anumodadhvaṃ pitṛdevarṣayo 'malāḥ
BhP kartuḥ śāstur anujñātus tulyaṃ yat pretya tat phalam
BhP asti yajñapatir nāma keṣāñcid arhasattamāḥ
BhP ihāmutra ca lakṣyante jyotsnāvatyaḥ kvacid bhuvaḥ
BhP manor uttānapādasya dhruvasyāpi mahīpateḥ
BhP priyavratasya rājarṣer aṅgasyāsmatpituḥ pituḥ
BhP īdṛśānām athānyeṣām ajasya ca bhavasya ca
BhP prahlādasya baleś cāpi kṛtyam asti gadābhṛtā
BhP dauhitrādīn ṛte mṛtyoḥ śocyān dharmavimohitān
BhP vargasvargāpavargāṇāṃ prāyeṇaikātmyahetunā
BhP yatpādasevābhirucis tapasvinām aśeṣajanmopacitaṃ malaṃ dhiyaḥ
BhP sadyaḥ kṣiṇoty anvaham edhatī satī yathā padāṅguṣṭhaviniḥsṛtā sarit
BhP vinirdhutāśeṣamanomalaḥ pumān asaṅgavijñānaviśeṣavīryavān
BhP yadaṅghrimūle kṛtaketanaḥ punar na saṃsṛtiṃ kleśavahāṃ prapadyate
BhP tam eva yūyaṃ bhajatātmavṛttibhir manovacaḥkāyaguṇaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ
BhP amāyinaḥ kāmadughāṅghripaṅkajaṃ yathādhikārāvasitārthasiddhayaḥ
BhP asāv ihānekaguṇo 'guṇo 'dhvaraḥ pṛthagvidhadravyaguṇakriyoktibhiḥ
BhP sampadyate 'rthāśayaliṅganāmabhir viśuddhavijñānaghanaḥ svarūpataḥ
BhP pradhānakālāśayadharmasaṅgrahe śarīra eṣa pratipadya cetanām
BhP kriyāphalatvena vibhur vibhāvyate yathānalo dāruṣu tadguṇātmakaḥ
BhP aho mamāmī vitaranty anugrahaṃ hariṃ guruṃ yajñabhujām adhīśvaram
BhP svadharmayogena yajanti māmakā nirantaraṃ kṣoṇitale dṛḍhavratāḥ
BhP mā jātu tejaḥ prabhaven maharddhibhis titikṣayā tapasā vidyayā ca
BhP dedīpyamāne 'jitadevatānāṃ kule svayaṃ rājakulād dvijānām
BhP brahmaṇyadevaḥ puruṣaḥ purātano nityaṃ harir yaccaraṇābhivandanāt
BhP avāpa lakṣmīm anapāyinīṃ yaśo jagatpavitraṃ ca mahattamāgraṇīḥ
BhP yatsevayāśeṣaguhāśayaḥ svarāḍ viprapriyas tuṣyati kāmam īśvaraḥ
BhP tad eva taddharmaparair vinītaiḥ sarvātmanā brahmakulaṃ niṣevyatām
BhP pumān labhetānativelam ātmanaḥ prasīdato 'tyantaśamaṃ svataḥ svayam
BhP yannityasambandhaniṣevayā tataḥ paraṃ kim atrāsti mukhaṃ havirbhujām
BhP aśnāty anantaḥ khalu tattvakovidaiḥ śraddhāhutaṃ yanmukha ijyanāmabhiḥ
BhP na vai tathā cetanayā bahiṣkṛte hutāśane pāramahaṃsyaparyaguḥ
BhP yad brahma nityaṃ virajaṃ sanātanaṃ śraddhātapomaṅgalamaunasaṃyamaiḥ
BhP samādhinā bibhrati hārthadṛṣṭaye yatredam ādarśa ivāvabhāsate
BhP teṣām ahaṃ pādasarojareṇum āryā vaheyādhikirīṭam āyuḥ
BhP yaṃ nityadā bibhrata āśu pāpaṃ naśyaty amuṃ sarvaguṇā bhajanti
BhP guṇāyanaṃ śīladhanaṃ kṛtajñaṃ vṛddhāśrayaṃ saṃvṛṇate 'nu sampadaḥ
BhP prasīdatāṃ brahmakulaṃ gavāṃ ca janārdanaḥ sānucaraś ca mahyam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti bruvāṇaṃ nṛpatiṃ pitṛdevadvijātayaḥ
BhP tuṣṭuvur hṛṣṭamanasaḥ sādhuvādena sādhavaḥ
BhP putreṇa jayate lokān iti satyavatī śrutiḥ
BhP brahmadaṇḍahataḥ pāpo yad veno 'tyatarat tamaḥ
BhP hiraṇyakaśipuś cāpi bhagavannindayā tamaḥ
BhP vivikṣur atyagāt sūnoḥ prahlādasyānubhāvataḥ
BhP vīravarya pitaḥ pṛthvyāḥ samāḥ sañjīva śāśvatīḥ
BhP yasyedṛśy acyute bhaktiḥ sarvalokaikabhartari
BhP aho vayaṃ hy adya pavitrakīrte tvayaiva nāthena mukundanāthāḥ
BhP ya uttamaślokatamasya viṣṇor brahmaṇyadevasya kathāṃ vyanakti
BhP nātyadbhutam idaṃ nātha tavājīvyānuśāsanam
BhP prajānurāgo mahatāṃ prakṛtiḥ karuṇātmanām
BhP adya nas tamasaḥ pāras tvayopāsāditaḥ prabho
BhP bhrāmyatāṃ naṣṭadṛṣṭīnāṃ karmabhir daivasaṃjñitaiḥ
BhP namo vivṛddhasattvāya puruṣāya mahīyase
BhP yo brahma kṣatram āviśya bibhartīdaṃ svatejasā
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP janeṣu pragṛṇatsv evaṃ pṛthuṃ pṛthulavikramam
BhP tatropajagmur munayaś catvāraḥ sūryavarcasaḥ
BhP tāṃs tu siddheśvarān rājā vyomno 'vatarato 'rciṣā

BhP taddarśanodgatān prāṇān pratyāditsur ivotthitaḥ
BhP sasadasyānugo vainya indriyeśo guṇān iva
BhP gauravād yantritaḥ sabhyaḥ praśrayānatakandharaḥ
BhP vidhivat pūjayāṃ cakre gṛhītādhyarhaṇāsanān

BhP pṛthur uvāca
BhP aho ācaritaṃ kiṃ me maṅgalaṃ maṅgalāyanāḥ

BhP kiṃ tasya durlabhataram iha loke paratra ca

BhP naiva lakṣayate loko lokān paryaṭato 'pi yān
