BhP adhanā api te dhanyāḥ sādhavo gṛhamedhinaḥ
BhP yadgṛhā hy arhavaryāmbu tṛṇabhūmīśvarāvarāḥ
BhP vyālālayadrumā vai teṣv ariktākhilasampadaḥ
BhP yadgṛhās tīrthapādīya pādatīrthavivarjitāḥ
BhP svāgataṃ vo dvijaśreṣṭhā yadvratāni mumukṣavaḥ
BhP caranti śraddhayā dhīrā bālā eva bṛhanti ca
BhP kaccin naḥ kuśalaṃ nāthā indriyārthārthavedinām
BhP vyasanāvāpa etasmin patitānāṃ svakarmabhiḥ

BhP sampṛcche bhava etasmin kṣemaḥ kenāñjasā bhavet

BhP svānām anugrahāyemāṃ siddharūpī caraty ajaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP pṛthos tat sūktam ākarṇya sāraṃ suṣṭhu mitaṃ madhu
BhP smayamāna iva prītyā kumāraḥ pratyuvāca ha
BhP sanatkumāra uvāca
BhP sādhu pṛṣṭaṃ mahārāja sarvabhūtahitātmanā
BhP bhavatā viduṣā cāpi sādhūnāṃ matir īdṛśī
BhP saṅgamaḥ khalu sādhūnām ubhayeṣāṃ ca sammataḥ
BhP yatsambhāṣaṇasampraśnaḥ sarveṣāṃ vitanoti śam
BhP asty eva rājan bhavato madhudviṣaḥ pādāravindasya guṇānuvādane
BhP ratir durāpā vidhunoti naiṣṭhikī kāmaṃ kaṣāyaṃ malam antarātmanaḥ
BhP śāstreṣv iyān eva suniścito nṛṇāṃ kṣemasya sadhryagvimṛśeṣu hetuḥ
BhP asaṅga ātmavyatirikta ātmani dṛḍhā ratir brahmaṇi nirguṇe ca yā
BhP sā śraddhayā bhagavaddharmacaryayā jijñāsayādhyātmikayoganiṣṭhayā

BhP harer muhus tatparakarṇapūra guṇābhidhānena vijṛmbhamāṇayā
BhP bhaktyā hy asaṅgaḥ sadasaty anātmani syān nirguṇe brahmaṇi cāñjasā ratiḥ
BhP yadā ratir brahmaṇi naiṣṭhikī pumān ācāryavān jñānavirāgaraṃhasā
BhP dahaty avīryaṃ hṛdayaṃ jīvakośaṃ pañcātmakaṃ yonim ivotthito 'gniḥ
BhP dagdhāśayo muktasamastatadguṇo naivātmano bahir antar vicaṣṭe
BhP parātmanor yadvyavadhānaṃ purastāt svapne yathā puruṣas tadvināśe
BhP ātmānam indriyārthaṃ ca paraṃ yad ubhayor api
BhP saty āśaya upādhau vai pumān paśyati nānyadā
BhP nimitte sati sarvatra jalādāv api pūruṣaḥ
BhP ātmanaś ca parasyāpi bhidāṃ paśyati nānyadā
BhP indriyair viṣayākṛṣṭair ākṣiptaṃ dhyāyatāṃ manaḥ
BhP cetanāṃ harate buddheḥ stambas toyam iva hradāt
BhP bhraśyaty anusmṛtiś cittaṃ jñānabhraṃśaḥ smṛtikṣaye
BhP tadrodhaṃ kavayaḥ prāhur ātmāpahnavam ātmanaḥ
BhP nātaḥ parataro loke puṃsaḥ svārthavyatikramaḥ
BhP yadadhy anyasya preyastvam ātmanaḥ svavyatikramāt
BhP arthendriyārthābhidhyānaṃ sarvārthāpahnavo nṛṇām
BhP bhraṃśito jñānavijñānād yenāviśati mukhyatām
BhP na kuryāt karhicit saṅgaṃ tamas tīvraṃ titīriṣuḥ
BhP dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ yad atyantavighātakam
BhP tatrāpi mokṣa evārtha ātyantikatayeṣyate
BhP traivargyo 'rtho yato nityaṃ kṛtāntabhayasaṃyutaḥ
BhP pare 'vare ca ye bhāvā guṇavyatikarād anu
BhP na teṣāṃ vidyate kṣemam īśavidhvaṃsitāśiṣām
BhP tat tvaṃ narendra jagatām atha tasthūṣāṃ ca
BhP dehendriyāsudhiṣaṇātmabhir āvṛtānām

BhP pratyak cakāsti bhagavāṃs tam avehi so 'smi
BhP yasminn idaṃ sadasadātmatayā vibhāti
BhP māyā vivekavidhuti sraji vāhibuddhiḥ
BhP taṃ nityamuktapariśuddhaviśuddhatattvaṃ

BhP tadvan na riktamatayo yatayo 'pi ruddha
BhP srotogaṇās tam araṇaṃ bhaja vāsudevam
BhP kṛcchro mahān iha bhavārṇavam aplaveśāṃ

BhP kṛtvoḍupaṃ vyasanam uttara dustarārṇam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP sa evaṃ brahmaputreṇa kumāreṇātmamedhasā
BhP darśitātmagatiḥ samyak praśasyovāca taṃ nṛpaḥ
BhP rājovāca
BhP kṛto me 'nugrahaḥ pūrvaṃ hariṇārtānukampinā
BhP tam āpādayituṃ brahman bhagavan yūyam āgatāḥ
BhP niṣpāditaś ca kārtsnyena bhagavadbhir ghṛṇālubhiḥ
BhP sādhūcchiṣṭaṃ hi me sarvam ātmanā saha kiṃ dade
BhP prāṇā dārāḥ sutā brahman gṛhāś ca saparicchadāḥ
BhP rājyaṃ balaṃ mahī kośa iti sarvaṃ niveditam
BhP saināpatyaṃ ca rājyaṃ ca daṇḍanetṛtvam eva ca
BhP sarva lokādhipatyaṃ ca vedaśāstravid arhati
BhP svam eva brāhmaṇo bhuṅkte svaṃ vaste svaṃ dadāti ca
BhP tasyaivānugraheṇānnaṃ bhuñjate kṣatriyādayaḥ
BhP yair īdṛśī bhagavato gatir ātmavāda
BhP ekāntato nigamibhiḥ pratipāditā naḥ
BhP tuṣyantv adabhrakaruṇāḥ svakṛtena nityaṃ
BhP ko nāma tat pratikaroti vinodapātram
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ta ātmayogapataya ādirājena pūjitāḥ
BhP śīlaṃ tadīyaṃ śaṃsantaḥ khe 'bhavan miṣatāṃ nṛṇām
BhP vainyas tu dhuryo mahatāṃ saṃsthityādhyātmaśikṣayā
BhP āptakāmam ivātmānaṃ mena ātmany avasthitaḥ
BhP karmāṇi ca yathākālaṃ yathādeśaṃ yathābalam
BhP yathocitaṃ yathāvittam akarod brahmasātkṛtam
BhP phalaṃ brahmaṇi sannyasya nirviṣaṅgaḥ samāhitaḥ
BhP karmādhyakṣaṃ ca manvāna ātmānaṃ prakṛteḥ param

BhP nāsajjatendriyārtheṣu nirahammatir arkavat

BhP vijitāśvaṃ dhūmrakeśaṃ haryakṣaṃ draviṇaṃ vṛkam

BhP gopīthāya jagatsṛṣṭeḥ kāle sve sve 'cyutātmakaḥ
BhP manovāgvṛttibhiḥ saumyair guṇaiḥ saṃrañjayan prajāḥ

BhP sūryavad visṛjan gṛhṇan pratapaṃś ca bhuvo vasu
BhP durdharṣas tejasevāgnir mahendra iva durjayaḥ
BhP titikṣayā dharitrīva dyaur ivābhīṣṭado nṛṇām

BhP maitreya uvāca

BhP jagatas tasthuṣaś cāpi vṛttido dharmabhṛt satām
BhP niṣpāditeśvarādeśo yadartham iha jajñivān

BhP natvā divisthāṃs tridaśāṃs triḥ parītya viveśa vahniṃ dhyāyatī bhartṛpādau

BhP nadatsv amaratūryeṣu gṛṇanti sma parasparam
BhP devya ūcuḥ
BhP aho iyaṃ vadhūr dhanyā yā caivaṃ bhūbhujāṃ patim
BhP sarvātmanā patiṃ bheje yajñeśaṃ śrīr vadhūr iva
BhP saiṣā nūnaṃ vrajaty ūrdhvam anu vainyaṃ patiṃ satī
BhP paśyatāsmān atītyārcir durvibhāvyena karmaṇā

BhP itthambhūtānubhāvo 'sau pṛthuḥ sa bhagavattamaḥ
BhP kīrtitaṃ tasya caritam uddāmacaritasya te
BhP ya idaṃ sumahat puṇyaṃ śraddhayāvahitaḥ paṭhet
BhP śrāvayec chṛṇuyād vāpi sa pṛthoḥ padavīm iyāt
BhP brāhmaṇo brahmavarcasvī rājanyo jagatīpatiḥ
BhP vaiśyaḥ paṭhan viṭpatiḥ syāc chūdraḥ sattamatām iyāt
BhP triḥ kṛtva idam ākarṇya naro nāry athavādṛtā
BhP aprajaḥ suprajatamo nirdhano dhanavattamaḥ
BhP aspaṣṭakīrtiḥ suyaśā mūrkho bhavati paṇḍitaḥ
BhP idaṃ svastyayanaṃ puṃsām amaṅgalyanivāraṇam
BhP dhanyaṃ yaśasyam āyuṣyaṃ svargyaṃ kalimalāpaham
BhP dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ samyak siddhim abhīpsubhiḥ
BhP śraddhayaitad anuśrāvyaṃ caturṇāṃ kāraṇaṃ param
BhP vijayābhimukho rājā śrutvaitad abhiyāti yān
BhP baliṃ tasmai haranty agre rājānaḥ pṛthave yathā
BhP muktānyasaṅgo bhagavaty amalāṃ bhaktim udvahan
BhP vainyasya caritaṃ puṇyaṃ śṛṇuyāc chrāvayet paṭhet
BhP vaicitravīryābhihitaṃ mahanmāhātmyasūcakam
BhP asmin kṛtam atimartyaṃ pārthavīṃ gatim āpnuyāt
BhP anudinam idam ādareṇa śṛṇvan pṛthucaritaṃ prathayan vimuktasaṅgaḥ
BhP bhagavati bhavasindhupotapāde sa ca nipuṇāṃ labhate ratiṃ manuṣyaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP vijitāśvo 'dhirājāsīt pṛthuputraḥ pṛthuśravāḥ
BhP yavīyobhyo 'dadāt kāṣṭhā bhrātṛbhyo bhrātṛvatsalaḥ
BhP haryakṣāyādiśat prācīṃ dhūmrakeśāya dakṣiṇām
BhP pratīcīṃ vṛkasaṃjñāya turyāṃ draviṇase vibhuḥ
BhP antardhānagatiṃ śakrāl labdhvāntardhānasaṃjñitaḥ
BhP apatyatrayam ādhatta śikhaṇḍinyāṃ susammatam
BhP pāvakaḥ pavamānaś ca śucir ity agnayaḥ purā
BhP vasiṣṭhaśāpād utpannāḥ punar yogagatiṃ gatāḥ
BhP antardhāno nabhasvatyāṃ havirdhānam avindata
BhP ya indram aśvahartāraṃ vidvān api na jaghnivān
BhP rājñāṃ vṛttiṃ karādāna daṇḍaśulkādidāruṇām
BhP manyamāno dīrghasattra vyājena visasarja ha
BhP tatrāpi haṃsaṃ puruṣaṃ paramātmānam ātmadṛk
BhP yajaṃs tallokatām āpa kuśalena samādhinā
BhP havirdhānād dhavirdhānī vidurāsūta ṣaṭ sutān
BhP barhiṣadaṃ gayaṃ śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ satyaṃ jitavratam
BhP barhiṣat sumahābhāgo hāvirdhāniḥ prajāpatiḥ
BhP kriyākāṇḍeṣu niṣṇāto yogeṣu ca kurūdvaha
BhP yasyedaṃ devayajanam anuyajñaṃ vitanvataḥ
BhP prācīnāgraiḥ kuśair āsīd āstṛtaṃ vasudhātalam
BhP sāmudrīṃ devadevoktām upayeme śatadrutim
BhP yāṃ vīkṣya cārusarvāṅgīṃ kiśorīṃ suṣṭhvalaṅkṛtām
BhP parikramantīm udvāhe cakame 'gniḥ śukīm iva
BhP vibudhāsuragandharva munisiddhanaroragāḥ
BhP vijitāḥ sūryayā dikṣu kvaṇayantyaiva nūpuraiḥ
BhP prācīnabarhiṣaḥ putrāḥ śatadrutyāṃ daśābhavan
BhP tulyanāmavratāḥ sarve dharmasnātāḥ pracetasaḥ
BhP pitrādiṣṭāḥ prajāsarge tapase 'rṇavam āviśan
BhP daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tapasārcaṃs tapaspatim
BhP yad uktaṃ pathi dṛṣṭena giriśena prasīdatā
BhP tad dhyāyanto japantaś ca pūjayantaś ca saṃyatāḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP pracetasāṃ giritreṇa yathāsīt pathi saṅgamaḥ
BhP yad utāha haraḥ prītas tan no brahman vadārthavat
BhP saṅgamaḥ khalu viprarṣe śiveneha śarīriṇām
BhP durlabho munayo dadhyur asaṅgād yam abhīpsitam
BhP ātmārāmo 'pi yas tv asya lokakalpasya rādhase
BhP śaktyā yukto vicarati ghorayā bhagavān bhavaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP pracetasaḥ pitur vākyaṃ śirasādāya sādhavaḥ
BhP diśaṃ pratīcīṃ prayayus tapasy ādṛtacetasaḥ
BhP sasamudram upa vistīrṇam apaśyan sumahat saraḥ
BhP mahanmana iva svacchaṃ prasannasalilāśayam
BhP nīlaraktotpalāmbhoja kahlārendīvarākaram
BhP haṃsasārasacakrāhva kāraṇḍavanikūjitam
BhP mattabhramarasausvarya hṛṣṭaromalatāṅghripam
BhP padmakośarajo dikṣu vikṣipatpavanotsavam
BhP tatra gāndharvam ākarṇya divyamārgamanoharam
BhP visismyū rājaputrās te mṛdaṅgapaṇavādy anu
BhP tarhy eva sarasas tasmān niṣkrāmantaṃ sahānugam
BhP upagīyamānam amara pravaraṃ vibudhānugaiḥ
BhP taptahemanikāyābhaṃ śitikaṇṭhaṃ trilocanam
BhP prasādasumukhaṃ vīkṣya praṇemur jātakautukāḥ
BhP sa tān prapannārtiharo bhagavān dharmavatsalaḥ
BhP dharmajñān śīlasampannān prītaḥ prītān uvāca ha
BhP śrīrudra uvāca
BhP yūyaṃ vediṣadaḥ putrā viditaṃ vaś cikīrṣitam
BhP anugrahāya bhadraṃ va evaṃ me darśanaṃ kṛtam
BhP yaḥ paraṃ raṃhasaḥ sākṣāt triguṇāj jīvasaṃjñitāt
BhP bhagavantaṃ vāsudevaṃ prapannaḥ sa priyo hi me
BhP svadharmaniṣṭhaḥ śatajanmabhiḥ pumān viriñcatām eti tataḥ paraṃ hi mām
BhP avyākṛtaṃ bhāgavato 'tha vaiṣṇavaṃ padaṃ yathāhaṃ vibudhāḥ kalātyaye
BhP atha bhāgavatā yūyaṃ priyāḥ stha bhagavān yathā
BhP na mad bhāgavatānāṃ ca preyān anyo 'sti karhicit
BhP idaṃ viviktaṃ japtavyaṃ pavitraṃ maṅgalaṃ param
BhP niḥśreyasakaraṃ cāpi śrūyatāṃ tad vadāmi vaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP ity anukrośahṛdayo bhagavān āha tāñ chivaḥ
BhP baddhāñjalīn rājaputrān nārāyaṇaparo vacaḥ
BhP śrīrudra uvāca
BhP jitaṃ ta ātmavidvarya svastaye svastir astu me
BhP bhavatārādhasā rāddhaṃ sarvasmā ātmane namaḥ
BhP namaḥ paṅkajanābhāya bhūtasūkṣmendriyātmane
BhP vāsudevāya śāntāya kūṭasthāya svarociṣe
BhP saṅkarṣaṇāya sūkṣmāya durantāyāntakāya ca
BhP namo viśvaprabodhāya pradyumnāyāntarātmane
BhP namo namo 'niruddhāya hṛṣīkeśendriyātmane
BhP namaḥ paramahaṃsāya pūrṇāya nibhṛtātmane
BhP svargāpavargadvārāya nityaṃ śuciṣade namaḥ
BhP namo hiraṇyavīryāya cāturhotrāya tantave
BhP nama ūrja iṣe trayyāḥ pataye yajñaretase
BhP tṛptidāya ca jīvānāṃ namaḥ sarvarasātmane
BhP sarvasattvātmadehāya viśeṣāya sthavīyase
BhP namas trailokyapālāya saha ojobalāya ca
BhP arthaliṅgāya nabhase namo 'ntarbahirātmane
BhP namaḥ puṇyāya lokāya amuṣmai bhūrivarcase
BhP pravṛttāya nivṛttāya pitṛdevāya karmaṇe
BhP namo 'dharmavipākāya mṛtyave duḥkhadāya ca
BhP namas ta āśiṣām īśa manave kāraṇātmane
BhP namo dharmāya bṛhate kṛṣṇāyākuṇṭhamedhase
BhP puruṣāya purāṇāya sāṅkhyayogeśvarāya ca
BhP śaktitrayasametāya mīḍhuṣe 'haṅkṛtātmane
BhP cetaākūtirūpāya namo vāco vibhūtaye
BhP darśanaṃ no didṛkṣūṇāṃ dehi bhāgavatārcitam
BhP rūpaṃ priyatamaṃ svānāṃ sarvendriyaguṇāñjanam
BhP snigdhaprāvṛḍghanaśyāmaṃ sarvasaundaryasaṅgraham
BhP cārvāyatacaturbāhu sujātarucirānanam
BhP padmakośapalāśākṣaṃ sundarabhru sunāsikam
BhP sudvijaṃ sukapolāsyaṃ samakarṇavibhūṣaṇam
BhP prītiprahasitāpāṅgam alakai rūpaśobhitam
BhP lasatpaṅkajakiñjalka dukūlaṃ mṛṣṭakuṇḍalam
BhP sphuratkirīṭavalaya hāranūpuramekhalam
BhP śaṅkhacakragadāpadma mālāmaṇyuttamarddhimat
BhP siṃhaskandhatviṣo bibhrat saubhagagrīvakaustubham
BhP śriyānapāyinyā kṣipta nikaṣāśmorasollasat
BhP pūrarecakasaṃvigna valivalgudalodaram
BhP pratisaṅkrāmayad viśvaṃ nābhyāvartagabhīrayā
BhP śyāmaśroṇyadhirociṣṇu dukūlasvarṇamekhalam
BhP samacārvaṅghrijaṅghoru nimnajānusudarśanam
BhP padā śaratpadmapalāśarociṣā nakhadyubhir no 'ntaraghaṃ vidhunvatā
BhP pradarśaya svīyam apāstasādhvasaṃ padaṃ guro mārgagurus tamojuṣām
BhP etad rūpam anudhyeyam ātmaśuddhim abhīpsatām
BhP yadbhaktiyogo 'bhayadaḥ svadharmam anutiṣṭhatām
BhP bhavān bhaktimatā labhyo durlabhaḥ sarvadehinām
BhP svārājyasyāpy abhimata ekāntenātmavidgatiḥ
BhP taṃ durārādhyam ārādhya satām api durāpayā
BhP ekāntabhaktyā ko vāñchet pādamūlaṃ vinā bahiḥ
BhP yatra nirviṣṭam araṇaṃ kṛtānto nābhimanyate
BhP viśvaṃ vidhvaṃsayan vīrya śauryavisphūrjitabhruvā
BhP kṣaṇārdhenāpi tulaye na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam
BhP bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ
BhP athānaghāṅghres tava kīrtitīrthayor antarbahiḥsnānavidhūtapāpmanām
BhP bhūteṣv anukrośasusattvaśīlināṃ syāt saṅgamo 'nugraha eṣa nas tava
BhP na yasya cittaṃ bahirarthavibhramaṃ tamoguhāyāṃ ca viśuddham āviśat
BhP yadbhaktiyogānugṛhītam añjasā munir vicaṣṭe nanu tatra te gatim
BhP yatredaṃ vyajyate viśvaṃ viśvasminn avabhāti yat
BhP tat tvaṃ brahma paraṃ jyotir ākāśam iva vistṛtam
BhP yo māyayedaṃ pururūpayāsṛjad bibharti bhūyaḥ kṣapayaty avikriyaḥ
BhP yadbhedabuddhiḥ sad ivātmaduḥsthayā tvam ātmatantraṃ bhagavan pratīmahi
BhP kriyākalāpair idam eva yoginaḥ śraddhānvitāḥ sādhu yajanti siddhaye
BhP bhūtendriyāntaḥkaraṇopalakṣitaṃ vede ca tantre ca ta eva kovidāḥ
BhP tvam eka ādyaḥ puruṣaḥ suptaśaktis tayā rajaḥsattvatamo vibhidyate
BhP mahān ahaṃ khaṃ marud agnivārdharāḥ surarṣayo bhūtagaṇā idaṃ yataḥ
BhP sṛṣṭaṃ svaśaktyedam anupraviṣṭaś caturvidhaṃ puram ātmāṃśakena
BhP atho vidus taṃ puruṣaṃ santam antar bhuṅkte hṛṣīkair madhu sāraghaṃ yaḥ
BhP sa eṣa lokān aticaṇḍavego vikarṣasi tvaṃ khalu kālayānaḥ
BhP bhūtāni bhūtair anumeyatattvo ghanāvalīr vāyur ivāviṣahyaḥ
BhP pramattam uccair iti kṛtyacintayā pravṛddhalobhaṃ viṣayeṣu lālasam
BhP tvam apramattaḥ sahasābhipadyase kṣullelihāno 'hir ivākhum antakaḥ
BhP kas tvatpadābjaṃ vijahāti paṇḍito yas te 'vamānavyayamānaketanaḥ
BhP viśaṅkayāsmadgurur arcati sma yad vinopapattiṃ manavaś caturdaśa
BhP atha tvam asi no brahman paramātman vipaścitām
BhP viśvaṃ rudrabhayadhvastam akutaścidbhayā gatiḥ
BhP idaṃ japata bhadraṃ vo viśuddhā nṛpanandanāḥ
BhP svadharmam anutiṣṭhanto bhagavaty arpitāśayāḥ
BhP tam evātmānam ātmasthaṃ sarvabhūteṣv avasthitam
BhP pūjayadhvaṃ gṛṇantaś ca dhyāyantaś cāsakṛd dharim
BhP yogādeśam upāsādya dhārayanto munivratāḥ
BhP samāhitadhiyaḥ sarva etad abhyasatādṛtāḥ
BhP idam āha purāsmākaṃ bhagavān viśvasṛkpatiḥ
BhP bhṛgvādīnām ātmajānāṃ sisṛkṣuḥ saṃsisṛkṣatām
BhP te vayaṃ noditāḥ sarve prajāsarge prajeśvarāḥ
BhP anena dhvastatamasaḥ sisṛkṣmo vividhāḥ prajāḥ
BhP athedaṃ nityadā yukto japann avahitaḥ pumān
BhP acirāc chreya āpnoti vāsudevaparāyaṇaḥ
BhP śreyasām iha sarveṣāṃ jñānaṃ niḥśreyasaṃ param
BhP sukhaṃ tarati duṣpāraṃ jñānanaur vyasanārṇavam
BhP ya imaṃ śraddhayā yukto madgītaṃ bhagavatstavam
BhP adhīyāno durārādhyaṃ harim ārādhayaty asau
BhP vindate puruṣo 'muṣmād yad yad icchaty asatvaram
BhP madgītagītāt suprītāc chreyasām ekavallabhāt
BhP idaṃ yaḥ kalya utthāya prāñjaliḥ śraddhayānvitaḥ
BhP śṛṇuyāc chrāvayen martyo mucyate karmabandhanaiḥ
BhP gītaṃ mayedaṃ naradevanandanāḥ parasya puṃsaḥ paramātmanaḥ stavam
BhP japanta ekāgradhiyas tapo mahat caradhvam ante tata āpsyathepsitam
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti sandiśya bhagavān bārhiṣadair abhipūjitaḥ
BhP paśyatāṃ rājaputrāṇāṃ tatraivāntardadhe haraḥ
BhP rudragītaṃ bhagavataḥ stotraṃ sarve pracetasaḥ
BhP japantas te tapas tepur varṣāṇām ayutaṃ jale
BhP prācīnabarhiṣaṃ kṣattaḥ karmasv āsaktamānasam
BhP nārado 'dhyātmatattvajñaḥ kṛpāluḥ pratyabodhayat
BhP śreyas tvaṃ katamad rājan karmaṇātmana īhase
BhP duḥkhahāniḥ sukhāvāptiḥ śreyas tan neha ceṣyate
BhP rājovāca
BhP na jānāmi mahābhāga paraṃ karmāpaviddhadhīḥ
BhP brūhi me vimalaṃ jñānaṃ yena mucyeya karmabhiḥ
BhP gṛheṣu kūṭadharmeṣu putradāradhanārthadhīḥ
BhP na paraṃ vindate mūḍho bhrāmyan saṃsāravartmasu
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP bho bhoḥ prajāpate rājan paśūn paśya tvayādhvare
BhP saṃjñāpitāñ jīvasaṅghān nirghṛṇena sahasraśaḥ
BhP ete tvāṃ sampratīkṣante smaranto vaiśasaṃ tava
BhP samparetam ayaḥkūṭaiś chindanty utthitamanyavaḥ
BhP atra te kathayiṣye 'mum itihāsaṃ purātanam
BhP purañjanasya caritaṃ nibodha gadato mama
BhP āsīt purañjano nāma rājā rājan bṛhacchravāḥ
BhP tasyāvijñātanāmāsīt sakhāvijñātaceṣṭitaḥ
BhP so 'nveṣamāṇaḥ śaraṇaṃ babhrāma pṛthivīṃ prabhuḥ
BhP nānurūpaṃ yadāvindad abhūt sa vimanā iva
BhP na sādhu mene tāḥ sarvā bhūtale yāvatīḥ puraḥ
BhP kāmān kāmayamāno 'sau tasya tasyopapattaye
BhP sa ekadā himavato dakṣiṇeṣv atha sānuṣu
BhP dadarśa navabhir dvārbhiḥ puraṃ lakṣitalakṣaṇām
BhP prākāropavanāṭṭāla parikhair akṣatoraṇaiḥ
BhP svarṇaraupyāyasaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ saṅkulāṃ sarvato gṛhaiḥ
BhP nīlasphaṭikavaidūrya muktāmarakatāruṇaiḥ
BhP kḷptaharmyasthalīṃ dīptāṃ śriyā bhogavatīm iva
BhP sabhācatvararathyābhir ākrīḍāyatanāpaṇaiḥ
BhP caityadhvajapatākābhir yuktāṃ vidrumavedibhiḥ
BhP puryās tu bāhyopavane divyadrumalatākule
BhP nadadvihaṅgālikula kolāhalajalāśaye
BhP himanirjharavipruṣmat kusumākaravāyunā
BhP calatpravālaviṭapa nalinītaṭasampadi
BhP nānāraṇyamṛgavrātair anābādhe munivrataiḥ
BhP āhūtaṃ manyate pāntho yatra kokilakūjitaiḥ
BhP yadṛcchayāgatāṃ tatra dadarśa pramadottamām
BhP bhṛtyair daśabhir āyāntīm ekaikaśatanāyakaiḥ
BhP añcaśīrṣāhinā guptāṃ pratīhāreṇa sarvataḥ
BhP anveṣamāṇām ṛṣabham aprauḍhāṃ kāmarūpiṇīm
BhP sunāsāṃ sudatīṃ bālāṃ sukapolāṃ varānanām
BhP samavinyastakarṇābhyāṃ bibhratīṃ kuṇḍalaśriyam
BhP piśaṅganīvīṃ suśroṇīṃ śyāmāṃ kanakamekhalām
BhP padbhyāṃ kvaṇadbhyāṃ calantīṃ nūpurair devatām iva
BhP stanau vyañjitakaiśorau samavṛttau nirantarau
BhP vastrāntena nigūhantīṃ vrīḍayā gajagāminīm
BhP tām āha lalitaṃ vīraḥ savrīḍasmitaśobhanām
BhP snigdhenāpāṅgapuṅkhena spṛṣṭaḥ premodbhramadbhruvā
BhP kā tvaṃ kañjapalāśākṣi kasyāsīha kutaḥ sati
BhP imām upa purīṃ bhīru kiṃ cikīrṣasi śaṃsa me
BhP ka ete 'nupathā ye ta ekādaśa mahābhaṭāḥ
BhP etā vā lalanāḥ subhru ko 'yaṃ te 'hiḥ puraḥsaraḥ
BhP tvaṃ hrīr bhavāny asy atha vāg ramā patiṃ vicinvatī kiṃ munivad raho vane
BhP tvadaṅghrikāmāptasamastakāmaṃ kva padmakośaḥ patitaḥ karāgrāt
BhP nāsāṃ varorv anyatamā bhuvispṛk purīm imāṃ vīravareṇa sākam
BhP arhasy alaṅkartum adabhrakarmaṇā lokaṃ paraṃ śrīr iva yajñapuṃsā
BhP yad eṣa māpāṅgavikhaṇḍitendriyaṃ savrīḍabhāvasmitavibhramadbhruvā
BhP tvayopasṛṣṭo bhagavān manobhavaḥ prabādhate 'thānugṛhāṇa śobhane
BhP tvadānanaṃ subhru sutāralocanaṃ vyālambinīlālakavṛndasaṃvṛtam
BhP unnīya me darśaya valguvācakaṃ yad vrīḍayā nābhimukhaṃ śucismite
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP itthaṃ purañjanaṃ nārī yācamānam adhīravat
BhP abhyanandata taṃ vīraṃ hasantī vīra mohitā
BhP na vidāma vayaṃ samyak kartāraṃ puruṣarṣabha
BhP ātmanaś ca parasyāpi gotraṃ nāma ca yatkṛtam
BhP ihādya santam ātmānaṃ vidāma na tataḥ param
BhP yeneyaṃ nirmitā vīra purī śaraṇam ātmanaḥ
BhP ete sakhāyaḥ sakhyo me narā nāryaś ca mānada
BhP suptāyāṃ mayi jāgarti nāgo 'yaṃ pālayan purīm
BhP diṣṭyāgato 'si bhadraṃ te grāmyān kāmān abhīpsase
BhP udvahiṣyāmi tāṃs te 'haṃ svabandhubhir arindama
BhP imāṃ tvam adhitiṣṭhasva purīṃ navamukhīṃ vibho
BhP mayopanītān gṛhṇānaḥ kāmabhogān śataṃ samāḥ
BhP kaṃ nu tvadanyaṃ ramaye hy aratijñam akovidam
BhP asamparāyābhimukham aśvastanavidaṃ paśum
BhP dharmo hy atrārthakāmau ca prajānando 'mṛtaṃ yaśaḥ
BhP lokā viśokā virajā yān na kevalino viduḥ
BhP pitṛdevarṣimartyānāṃ bhūtānām ātmanaś ca ha
BhP kṣemyaṃ vadanti śaraṇaṃ bhave 'smin yad gṛhāśramaḥ
BhP kā nāma vīra vikhyātaṃ vadānyaṃ priyadarśanam
BhP na vṛṇīta priyaṃ prāptaṃ mādṛśī tvādṛśaṃ patim
BhP kasyā manas te bhuvi bhogibhogayoḥ striyā na sajjed bhujayor mahābhuja
BhP yo 'nāthavargādhim alaṃ ghṛṇoddhata smitāvalokena caraty apohitum
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP iti tau dampatī tatra samudya samayaṃ mithaḥ
BhP tāṃ praviśya purīṃ rājan mumudāte śataṃ samāḥ
BhP upagīyamāno lalitaṃ tatra tatra ca gāyakaiḥ
BhP krīḍan parivṛtaḥ strībhir hradinīm āviśac chucau
BhP saptopari kṛtā dvāraḥ puras tasyās tu dve adhaḥ
BhP pṛthagviṣayagatyarthaṃ tasyāṃ yaḥ kaścaneśvaraḥ
BhP pañca dvāras tu paurastyā dakṣiṇaikā tathottarā
BhP paścime dve amūṣāṃ te nāmāni nṛpa varṇaye
BhP khadyotāvirmukhī ca prāg dvārāv ekatra nirmite
BhP vibhrājitaṃ janapadaṃ yāti tābhyāṃ dyumatsakhaḥ
BhP nalinī nālinī ca prāg dvārāv ekatra nirmite
BhP avadhūtasakhas tābhyāṃ viṣayaṃ yāti saurabham
BhP mukhyā nāma purastād dvās tayāpaṇabahūdanau
BhP viṣayau yāti purarāḍ rasajñavipaṇānvitaḥ
BhP pitṛhūr nṛpa puryā dvār dakṣiṇena purañjanaḥ
BhP rāṣṭraṃ dakṣiṇapañcālaṃ yāti śrutadharānvitaḥ
BhP devahūr nāma puryā dvā uttareṇa purañjanaḥ
BhP rāṣṭram uttarapañcālaṃ yāti śrutadharānvitaḥ
BhP āsurī nāma paścād dvās tayā yāti purañjanaḥ
BhP grāmakaṃ nāma viṣayaṃ durmadena samanvitaḥ
BhP nirṛtir nāma paścād dvās tayā yāti purañjanaḥ
BhP vaiśasaṃ nāma viṣayaṃ lubdhakena samanvitaḥ
BhP andhāv amīṣāṃ paurāṇāṃ nirvākpeśaskṛtāv ubhau
BhP akṣaṇvatām adhipatis tābhyāṃ yāti karoti ca
BhP sa yarhy antaḥpuragato viṣūcīnasamanvitaḥ
BhP mohaṃ prasādaṃ harṣaṃ vā yāti jāyātmajodbhavam
BhP evaṃ karmasu saṃsaktaḥ kāmātmā vañcito 'budhaḥ
BhP mahiṣī yad yad īheta tat tad evānvavartata
BhP kvacit pibantyāṃ pibati madirāṃ madavihvalaḥ
BhP aśnantyāṃ kvacid aśnāti jakṣatyāṃ saha jakṣiti
BhP kvacid gāyati gāyantyāṃ rudatyāṃ rudati kvacit
BhP kvacid dhasantyāṃ hasati jalpantyām anu jalpati
BhP kvacid dhāvati dhāvantyāṃ tiṣṭhantyām anu tiṣṭhati
BhP anu śete śayānāyām anvāste kvacid āsatīm
BhP kvacic chṛṇoti śṛṇvantyāṃ paśyantyām anu paśyati
BhP kvacij jighrati jighrantyāṃ spṛśantyāṃ spṛśati kvacit
BhP kvacic ca śocatīṃ jāyām anu śocati dīnavat
BhP anu hṛṣyati hṛṣyantyāṃ muditām anu modate
BhP vipralabdho mahiṣyaivaṃ sarvaprakṛtivañcitaḥ
BhP necchann anukaroty ajñaḥ klaibyāt krīḍāmṛgo yathā
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP sa ekadā maheṣvāso rathaṃ pañcāśvam āśugam
BhP dvīṣaṃ dvicakram ekākṣaṃ triveṇuṃ pañcabandhuram
BhP ekaraśmy ekadamanam ekanīḍaṃ dvikūbaram
BhP pañcapraharaṇaṃ sapta varūthaṃ pañcavikramam
BhP haimopaskaram āruhya svarṇavarmākṣayeṣudhiḥ
BhP ekādaśacamūnāthaḥ pañcaprastham agād vanam
BhP cacāra mṛgayāṃ tatra dṛpta ātteṣukārmukaḥ
BhP vihāya jāyām atadarhāṃ mṛgavyasanalālasaḥ
BhP āsurīṃ vṛttim āśritya ghorātmā niranugrahaḥ
BhP nyahanan niśitair bāṇair vaneṣu vanagocarān
BhP tīrtheṣu pratidṛṣṭeṣu rājā medhyān paśūn vane
BhP yāvadartham alaṃ lubdho hanyād iti niyamyate
BhP ya evaṃ karma niyataṃ vidvān kurvīta mānavaḥ
BhP karmaṇā tena rājendra jñānena na sa lipyate
BhP anyathā karma kurvāṇo mānārūḍho nibadhyate
BhP guṇapravāhapatito naṣṭaprajño vrajaty adhaḥ
BhP tatra nirbhinnagātrāṇāṃ citravājaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ
BhP viplavo 'bhūd duḥkhitānāṃ duḥsahaḥ karuṇātmanām
BhP śaśān varāhān mahiṣān gavayān ruruśalyakān
BhP medhyān anyāṃś ca vividhān vinighnan śramam adhyagāt
BhP tataḥ kṣuttṛṭpariśrānto nivṛtto gṛham eyivān
BhP kṛtasnānocitāhāraḥ saṃviveśa gataklamaḥ
BhP ātmānam arhayāṃ cakre dhūpālepasragādibhiḥ
BhP sādhvalaṅkṛtasarvāṅgo mahiṣyām ādadhe manaḥ
BhP tṛpto hṛṣṭaḥ sudṛptaś ca kandarpākṛṣṭamānasaḥ
BhP na vyacaṣṭa varārohāṃ gṛhiṇīṃ gṛhamedhinīm
BhP antaḥpurastriyo 'pṛcchad vimanā iva vediṣat
BhP api vaḥ kuśalaṃ rāmāḥ seśvarīṇāṃ yathā purā
BhP na tathaitarhi rocante gṛheṣu gṛhasampadaḥ
BhP yadi na syād gṛhe mātā patnī vā patidevatā
BhP vyaṅge ratha iva prājñaḥ ko nāmāsīta dīnavat
BhP kva vartate sā lalanā majjantaṃ vyasanārṇave
BhP yā mām uddharate prajñāṃ dīpayantī pade pade
BhP rāmā ūcuḥ
BhP naranātha na jānīmas tvatpriyā yad vyavasyati
BhP bhūtale niravastāre śayānāṃ paśya śatruhan
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP purañjanaḥ svamahiṣīṃ nirīkṣyāvadhutāṃ bhuvi
BhP tatsaṅgonmathitajñāno vaiklavyaṃ paramaṃ yayau
BhP sāntvayan ślakṣṇayā vācā hṛdayena vidūyatā
BhP preyasyāḥ snehasaṃrambha liṅgam ātmani nābhyagāt
BhP anuninye 'tha śanakair vīro 'nunayakovidaḥ
BhP pasparśa pādayugalam āha cotsaṅgalālitām
BhP purañjana uvāca
BhP nūnaṃ tv akṛtapuṇyās te bhṛtyā yeṣv īśvarāḥ śubhe
BhP kṛtāgaḥsv ātmasāt kṛtvā śikṣādaṇḍaṃ na yuñjate
BhP paramo 'nugraho daṇḍo bhṛtyeṣu prabhuṇārpitaḥ
BhP bālo na veda tat tanvi bandhukṛtyam amarṣaṇaḥ
BhP sā tvaṃ mukhaṃ sudati subhrv anurāgabhāra vrīḍāvilambavilasaddhasitāvalokam
BhP nīlālakālibhir upaskṛtam unnasaṃ naḥ svānāṃ pradarśaya manasvini valguvākyam
BhP tasmin dadhe damam ahaṃ tava vīrapatni yo 'nyatra bhūsurakulāt kṛtakilbiṣas tam
BhP paśye na vītabhayam unmuditaṃ trilokyām anyatra vai muraripor itaratra dāsāt
BhP vaktraṃ na te vitilakaṃ malinaṃ viharṣaṃ saṃrambhabhīmam avimṛṣṭam apetarāgam
BhP paśye stanāv api śucopahatau sujātau bimbādharaṃ vigatakuṅkumapaṅkarāgam
BhP tan me prasīda suhṛdaḥ kṛtakilbiṣasya svairaṃ gatasya mṛgayāṃ vyasanāturasya
BhP kā devaraṃ vaśagataṃ kusumāstravega visrastapauṃsnam uśatī na bhajeta kṛtye
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP itthaṃ purañjanaṃ sadhryag vaśamānīya vibhramaiḥ
BhP purañjanī mahārāja reme ramayatī patim
BhP sa rājā mahiṣīṃ rājan susnātāṃ rucirānanām
BhP kṛtasvastyayanāṃ tṛptām abhyanandad upāgatām
BhP tayopagūḍhaḥ parirabdhakandharo raho 'numantrair apakṛṣṭacetanaḥ
BhP na kālaraṃho bubudhe duratyayaṃ divā niśeti pramadāparigrahaḥ
BhP śayāna unnaddhamado mahāmanā mahārhatalpe mahiṣībhujopadhiḥ
BhP tām eva vīro manute paraṃ yatas tamo'bhibhūto na nijaṃ paraṃ ca yat
BhP tayaivaṃ ramamāṇasya kāmakaśmalacetasaḥ
BhP kṣaṇārdham iva rājendra vyatikrāntaṃ navaṃ vayaḥ
BhP tasyām ajanayat putrān purañjanyāṃ purañjanaḥ
BhP śatāny ekādaśa virāḍ āyuṣo 'rdham athātyagāt
BhP duhitṝr daśottaraśataṃ pitṛmātṛyaśaskarīḥ
BhP śīlaudāryaguṇopetāḥ paurañjanyaḥ prajāpate
BhP sa pañcālapatiḥ putrān pitṛvaṃśavivardhanān
BhP dāraiḥ saṃyojayām āsa duhitṝḥ sadṛśair varaiḥ
BhP putrāṇāṃ cābhavan putrā ekaikasya śataṃ śatam
BhP yair vai paurañjano vaṃśaḥ pañcāleṣu samedhitaḥ
BhP teṣu tadrikthahāreṣu gṛhakośānujīviṣu
BhP nirūḍhena mamatvena viṣayeṣv anvabadhyata
BhP īje ca kratubhir ghorair dīkṣitaḥ paśumārakaiḥ
BhP devān pitṝn bhūtapatīn nānākāmo yathā bhavān
BhP yukteṣv evaṃ pramattasya kuṭumbāsaktacetasaḥ
BhP āsasāda sa vai kālo yo 'priyaḥ priyayoṣitām
BhP caṇḍavega iti khyāto gandharvādhipatir nṛpa
BhP gandharvās tasya balinaḥ ṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatrayam
BhP gandharvyas tādṛśīr asya maithunyaś ca sitāsitāḥ
BhP parivṛttyā vilumpanti sarvakāmavinirmitām
BhP te caṇḍavegānucarāḥ purañjanapuraṃ yadā
BhP hartum ārebhire tatra pratyaṣedhat prajāgaraḥ
BhP sa saptabhiḥ śatair eko viṃśatyā ca śataṃ samāḥ
BhP purañjanapurādhyakṣo gandharvair yuyudhe balī
BhP kṣīyamāṇe svasambandhe ekasmin bahubhir yudhā
BhP cintāṃ parāṃ jagāmārtaḥ sarāṣṭrapurabāndhavaḥ
BhP sa eva puryāṃ madhubhuk pañcāleṣu svapārṣadaiḥ
BhP upanītaṃ baliṃ gṛhṇan strījito nāvidad bhayam
BhP kālasya duhitā kācit trilokīṃ varam icchatī
BhP paryaṭantī na barhiṣman pratyanandata kaścana
BhP daurbhāgyenātmano loke viśrutā durbhageti sā
BhP yā tuṣṭā rājarṣaye tu vṛtādāt pūrave varam
BhP kadācid aṭamānā sā brahmalokān mahīṃ gatam
BhP vavre bṛhadvrataṃ māṃ tu jānatī kāmamohitā
BhP mayi saṃrabhya vipula madāc chāpaṃ suduḥsaham
BhP sthātum arhasi naikatra madyācñāvimukho mune
BhP tato vihatasaṅkalpā kanyakā yavaneśvaram
BhP mayopadiṣṭam āsādya vavre nāmnā bhayaṃ patim
BhP ṛṣabhaṃ yavanānāṃ tvāṃ vṛṇe vīrepsitaṃ patim
BhP saṅkalpas tvayi bhūtānāṃ kṛtaḥ kila na riṣyati
BhP dvāv imāv anuśocanti bālāv asadavagrahau
BhP yal lokaśāstropanataṃ na rāti na tad icchati
BhP atho bhajasva māṃ bhadra bhajantīṃ me dayāṃ kuru
BhP etāvān pauruṣo dharmo yad ārtān anukampate
BhP kālakanyoditavaco niśamya yavaneśvaraḥ
BhP cikīrṣur devaguhyaṃ sa sasmitaṃ tām abhāṣata
BhP mayā nirūpitas tubhyaṃ patir ātmasamādhinā
BhP nābhinandati loko 'yaṃ tvām abhadrām asammatām
BhP tvam avyaktagatir bhuṅkṣva lokaṃ karmavinirmitam
BhP yā hi me pṛtanāyuktā prajānāśaṃ praṇeṣyasi
BhP prajvāro 'yaṃ mama bhrātā tvaṃ ca me bhaginī bhava
BhP carāmy ubhābhyāṃ loke 'sminn avyakto bhīmasainikaḥ
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP sainikā bhayanāmno ye barhiṣman diṣṭakāriṇaḥ
BhP prajvārakālakanyābhyāṃ vicerur avanīm imām
BhP ta ekadā tu rabhasā purañjanapurīṃ nṛpa
BhP rurudhur bhaumabhogāḍhyāṃ jaratpannagapālitām
BhP kālakanyāpi bubhuje purañjanapuraṃ balāt
BhP yayābhibhūtaḥ puruṣaḥ sadyo niḥsāratām iyāt
BhP tayopabhujyamānāṃ vai yavanāḥ sarvatodiśam
BhP dvārbhiḥ praviśya subhṛśaṃ prārdayan sakalāṃ purīm
BhP tasyāṃ prapīḍyamānāyām abhimānī purañjanaḥ
BhP avāporuvidhāṃs tāpān kuṭumbī mamatākulaḥ
BhP kanyopagūḍho naṣṭaśrīḥ kṛpaṇo viṣayātmakaḥ
BhP naṣṭaprajño hṛtaiśvaryo gandharvayavanair balāt
BhP viśīrṇāṃ svapurīṃ vīkṣya pratikūlān anādṛtān
BhP putrān pautrānugāmātyān jāyāṃ ca gatasauhṛdām
BhP ātmānaṃ kanyayā grastaṃ pañcālān aridūṣitān
BhP durantacintām āpanno na lebhe tatpratikriyām
BhP kāmān abhilaṣan dīno yātayāmāṃś ca kanyayā
BhP vigatātmagatisnehaḥ putradārāṃś ca lālayan
BhP gandharvayavanākrāntāṃ kālakanyopamarditām
BhP hātuṃ pracakrame rājā tāṃ purīm anikāmataḥ
BhP bhayanāmno 'grajo bhrātā prajvāraḥ pratyupasthitaḥ
BhP dadāha tāṃ purīṃ kṛtsnāṃ bhrātuḥ priyacikīrṣayā
BhP tasyāṃ sandahyamānāyāṃ sapauraḥ saparicchadaḥ
BhP kauṭumbikaḥ kuṭumbinyā upātapyata sānvayaḥ
BhP yavanoparuddhāyatano grastāyāṃ kālakanyayā
BhP puryāṃ prajvārasaṃsṛṣṭaḥ purapālo 'nvatapyata
BhP na śeke so 'vituṃ tatra purukṛcchroruvepathuḥ
BhP gantum aicchat tato vṛkṣa koṭarād iva sānalāt
BhP śithilāvayavo yarhi gandharvair hṛtapauruṣaḥ
BhP yavanair aribhī rājann uparuddho ruroda ha
BhP duhitṝḥ putrapautrāṃś ca jāmijāmātṛpārṣadān
BhP svatvāvaśiṣṭaṃ yat kiñcid gṛhakośaparicchadam
BhP ahaṃ mameti svīkṛtya gṛheṣu kumatir gṛhī
BhP dadhyau pramadayā dīno viprayoga upasthite
BhP lokāntaraṃ gatavati mayy anāthā kuṭumbinī
BhP vartiṣyate kathaṃ tv eṣā bālakān anuśocatī
BhP na mayy anāśite bhuṅkte nāsnāte snāti matparā
BhP mayi ruṣṭe susantrastā bhartsite yatavāg bhayāt
BhP prabodhayati māvijñaṃ vyuṣite śokakarśitā
BhP vartmaitad gṛhamedhīyaṃ vīrasūr api neṣyati
BhP kathaṃ nu dārakā dīnā dārakīr vāparāyaṇāḥ
BhP vartiṣyante mayi gate bhinnanāva ivodadhau
BhP evaṃ kṛpaṇayā buddhyā śocantam atadarhaṇam
BhP grahītuṃ kṛtadhīr enaṃ bhayanāmābhyapadyata
BhP paśuvad yavanair eṣa nīyamānaḥ svakaṃ kṣayam
BhP anvadravann anupathāḥ śocanto bhṛśam āturāḥ
BhP purīṃ vihāyopagata uparuddho bhujaṅgamaḥ
BhP yadā tam evānu purī viśīrṇā prakṛtiṃ gatā
BhP vikṛṣyamāṇaḥ prasabhaṃ yavanena balīyasā
BhP nāvindat tamasāviṣṭaḥ sakhāyaṃ suhṛdaṃ puraḥ
BhP taṃ yajñapaśavo 'nena saṃjñaptā ye 'dayālunā
BhP kuṭhāraiś cicchiduḥ kruddhāḥ smaranto 'mīvam asya tat
BhP anantapāre tamasi magno naṣṭasmṛtiḥ samāḥ
BhP śāśvatīr anubhūyārtiṃ pramadāsaṅgadūṣitaḥ
BhP tām eva manasā gṛhṇan babhūva pramadottamā
BhP anantaraṃ vidarbhasya rājasiṃhasya veśmani
BhP upayeme vīryapaṇāṃ vaidarbhīṃ malayadhvajaḥ
BhP yudhi nirjitya rājanyān pāṇḍyaḥ parapurañjayaḥ
BhP tasyāṃ sa janayāṃ cakra ātmajām asitekṣaṇām
BhP yavīyasaḥ sapta sutān sapta draviḍabhūbhṛtaḥ
BhP ekaikasyābhavat teṣāṃ rājann arbudam arbudam
BhP bhokṣyate yadvaṃśadharair mahī manvantaraṃ param
BhP agastyaḥ prāg duhitaram upayeme dhṛtavratām
BhP yasyāṃ dṛḍhacyuto jāta idhmavāhātmajo muniḥ
BhP vibhajya tanayebhyaḥ kṣmāṃ rājarṣir malayadhvajaḥ
BhP ārirādhayiṣuḥ kṛṣṇaṃ sa jagāma kulācalam
BhP hitvā gṛhān sutān bhogān vaidarbhī madirekṣaṇā
BhP anvadhāvata pāṇḍyeśaṃ jyotsneva rajanīkaram
BhP tatra candravasā nāma tāmraparṇī vaṭodakā
BhP tatpuṇyasalilair nityam ubhayatrātmano mṛjan
BhP kandāṣṭibhir mūlaphalaiḥ puṣpaparṇais tṛṇodakaiḥ
BhP vartamānaḥ śanair gātra karśanaṃ tapa āsthitaḥ
BhP śītoṣṇavātavarṣāṇi kṣutpipāse priyāpriye
BhP sukhaduḥkhe iti dvandvāny ajayat samadarśanaḥ
BhP tapasā vidyayā pakva kaṣāyo niyamair yamaiḥ
BhP yuyuje brahmaṇy ātmānaṃ vijitākṣānilāśayaḥ
BhP āste sthāṇur ivaikatra divyaṃ varṣaśataṃ sthiraḥ
BhP vāsudeve bhagavati nānyad vedodvahan ratim
BhP sa vyāpakatayātmānaṃ vyatiriktatayātmani
BhP vidvān svapna ivāmarśa sākṣiṇaṃ virarāma ha
BhP sākṣād bhagavatoktena guruṇā hariṇā nṛpa
BhP viśuddhajñānadīpena sphuratā viśvatomukham
BhP pare brahmaṇi cātmānaṃ paraṃ brahma tathātmani
BhP vīkṣamāṇo vihāyekṣām asmād upararāma ha
BhP patiṃ paramadharmajñaṃ vaidarbhī malayadhvajam
BhP premṇā paryacarad dhitvā bhogān sā patidevatā
BhP cīravāsā vratakṣāmā veṇībhūtaśiroruhā
BhP babhāv upa patiṃ śāntā śikhā śāntam ivānalam
BhP ajānatī priyatamaṃ yadoparatam aṅganā
BhP susthirāsanam āsādya yathāpūrvam upācarat
BhP yadā nopalabhetāṅghrāv ūṣmāṇaṃ patyur arcatī
BhP āsīt saṃvignahṛdayā yūthabhraṣṭā mṛgī yathā
BhP ātmānaṃ śocatī dīnam abandhuṃ viklavāśrubhiḥ
BhP stanāv āsicya vipine susvaraṃ praruroda sā
BhP uttiṣṭhottiṣṭha rājarṣe imām udadhimekhalām
BhP dasyubhyaḥ kṣatrabandhubhyo bibhyatīṃ pātum arhasi
BhP evaṃ vilapantī bālā vipine 'nugatā patim
BhP patitā pādayor bhartū rudaty aśrūṇy avartayat
BhP citiṃ dārumayīṃ citvā tasyāṃ patyuḥ kalevaram
BhP ādīpya cānumaraṇe vilapantī mano dadhe
BhP tatra pūrvataraḥ kaścit sakhā brāhmaṇa ātmavān
BhP sāntvayan valgunā sāmnā tām āha rudatīṃ prabho
BhP brāhmaṇa uvāca
BhP kā tvaṃ kasyāsi ko vāyaṃ śayāno yasya śocasi
BhP jānāsi kiṃ sakhāyaṃ māṃ yenāgre vicacartha ha
BhP api smarasi cātmānam avijñātasakhaṃ sakhe
BhP hitvā māṃ padam anvicchan bhaumabhogarato gataḥ
BhP haṃsāv ahaṃ ca tvaṃ cārya sakhāyau mānasāyanau
BhP abhūtām antarā vaukaḥ sahasraparivatsarān
BhP sa tvaṃ vihāya māṃ bandho gato grāmyamatir mahīm
BhP vicaran padam adrākṣīḥ kayācin nirmitaṃ striyā
BhP pañcārāmaṃ navadvāram ekapālaṃ trikoṣṭhakam
BhP ṣaṭkulaṃ pañcavipaṇaṃ pañcaprakṛti strīdhavam
BhP pañcendriyārthā ārāmā dvāraḥ prāṇā nava prabho
BhP tejo'bannāni koṣṭhāni kulam indriyasaṅgrahaḥ
BhP vipaṇas tu kriyāśaktir bhūtaprakṛtir avyayā
BhP śaktyadhīśaḥ pumāṃs tv atra praviṣṭo nāvabudhyate
BhP tasmiṃs tvaṃ rāmayā spṛṣṭo ramamāṇo 'śrutasmṛtiḥ
BhP tatsaṅgād īdṛśīṃ prāpto daśāṃ pāpīyasīṃ prabho
BhP na tvaṃ vidarbhaduhitā nāyaṃ vīraḥ suhṛt tava
BhP na patis tvaṃ purañjanyā ruddho navamukhe yayā
BhP māyā hy eṣā mayā sṛṣṭā yat pumāṃsaṃ striyaṃ satīm
BhP manyase nobhayaṃ yad vai haṃsau paśyāvayor gatim
BhP ahaṃ bhavān na cānyas tvaṃ tvam evāhaṃ vicakṣva bhoḥ
BhP na nau paśyanti kavayaś chidraṃ jātu manāg api
BhP yathā puruṣa ātmānam ekam ādarśacakṣuṣoḥ
BhP dvidhābhūtam avekṣeta tathaivāntaram āvayoḥ
BhP evaṃ sa mānaso haṃso haṃsena pratibodhitaḥ
BhP svasthas tadvyabhicāreṇa naṣṭām āpa punaḥ smṛtim
BhP barhiṣmann etad adhyātmaṃ pārokṣyeṇa pradarśitam
BhP yat parokṣapriyo devo bhagavān viśvabhāvanaḥ
BhP prācīnabarhir uvāca
BhP bhagavaṃs te vaco 'smābhir na samyag avagamyate
BhP kavayas tad vijānanti na vayaṃ karmamohitāḥ
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP puruṣaṃ purañjanaṃ vidyād yad vyanakty ātmanaḥ puram
BhP ekadvitricatuṣpādaṃ bahupādam apādakam
BhP yo 'vijñātāhṛtas tasya puruṣasya sakheśvaraḥ
BhP yan na vijñāyate pumbhir nāmabhir vā kriyāguṇaiḥ
BhP yadā jighṛkṣan puruṣaḥ kārtsnyena prakṛter guṇān
BhP navadvāraṃ dvihastāṅghri tatrāmanuta sādhv iti
BhP buddhiṃ tu pramadāṃ vidyān mamāham iti yatkṛtam
BhP yām adhiṣṭhāya dehe 'smin pumān bhuṅkte 'kṣabhir guṇān
BhP sakhāya indriyagaṇā jñānaṃ karma ca yatkṛtam
BhP sakhyas tadvṛttayaḥ prāṇaḥ pañcavṛttir yathoragaḥ
BhP bṛhadbalaṃ mano vidyād ubhayendriyanāyakam
BhP pañcālāḥ pañca viṣayā yanmadhye navakhaṃ puram
BhP akṣiṇī nāsike karṇau mukhaṃ śiśnagudāv iti
BhP dve dve dvārau bahir yāti yas tadindriyasaṃyutaḥ
BhP akṣiṇī nāsike āsyam iti pañca puraḥ kṛtāḥ
BhP dakṣiṇā dakṣiṇaḥ karṇa uttarā cottaraḥ smṛtaḥ
BhP paścime ity adho dvārau gudaṃ śiśnam ihocyate
BhP khadyotāvirmukhī cātra netre ekatra nirmite
BhP rūpaṃ vibhrājitaṃ tābhyāṃ vicaṣṭe cakṣuṣeśvaraḥ
BhP nalinī nālinī nāse gandhaḥ saurabha ucyate
BhP ghrāṇo 'vadhūto mukhyāsyaṃ vipaṇo vāg rasavid rasaḥ
BhP āpaṇo vyavahāro 'tra citram andho bahūdanam
BhP pitṛhūr dakṣiṇaḥ karṇa uttaro devahūḥ smṛtaḥ
BhP pravṛttaṃ ca nivṛttaṃ ca śāstraṃ pañcālasaṃjñitam
BhP pitṛyānaṃ devayānaṃ śrotrāc chrutadharād vrajet
BhP āsurī meḍhram arvāgdvār vyavāyo grāmiṇāṃ ratiḥ
BhP upastho durmadaḥ prokto nirṛtir guda ucyate
BhP vaiśasaṃ narakaṃ pāyur lubdhako 'ndhau tu me śṛṇu
BhP hastapādau pumāṃs tābhyāṃ yukto yāti karoti ca
BhP antaḥpuraṃ ca hṛdayaṃ viṣūcir mana ucyate
BhP tatra mohaṃ prasādaṃ vā harṣaṃ prāpnoti tadguṇaiḥ
BhP yathā yathā vikriyate guṇākto vikaroti vā
BhP tathā tathopadraṣṭātmā tadvṛttīr anukāryate
BhP deho rathas tv indriyāśvaḥ saṃvatsararayo 'gatiḥ
BhP dvikarmacakras triguṇa dhvajaḥ pañcāsubandhuraḥ
BhP manoraśmir buddhisūto hṛnnīḍo dvandvakūbaraḥ
BhP pañcendriyārthaprakṣepaḥ saptadhātuvarūthakaḥ
BhP ākūtir vikramo bāhyo mṛgatṛṣṇāṃ pradhāvati
BhP ekādaśendriyacamūḥ pañcasūnāvinodakṛt
BhP saṃvatsaraś caṇḍavegaḥ kālo yenopalakṣitaḥ
BhP tasyāhānīha gandharvā gandharvyo rātrayaḥ smṛtāḥ
BhP haranty āyuḥ parikrāntyā ṣaṣṭyuttaraśatatrayam
BhP kālakanyā jarā sākṣāl lokas tāṃ nābhinandati
BhP svasāraṃ jagṛhe mṛtyuḥ kṣayāya yavaneśvaraḥ
BhP ādhayo vyādhayas tasya sainikā yavanāś carāḥ
BhP bhūtopasargāśurayaḥ prajvāro dvividho jvaraḥ
BhP evaṃ bahuvidhair duḥkhair daivabhūtātmasambhavaiḥ
BhP kliśyamānaḥ śataṃ varṣaṃ dehe dehī tamovṛtaḥ
BhP prāṇendriyamanodharmān ātmany adhyasya nirguṇaḥ
BhP śete kāmalavān dhyāyan mamāham iti karmakṛt
BhP yadātmānam avijñāya bhagavantaṃ paraṃ gurum
BhP puruṣas tu viṣajjeta guṇeṣu prakṛteḥ svadṛk
BhP guṇābhimānī sa tadā karmāṇi kurute 'vaśaḥ
BhP śuklaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ lohitaṃ vā yathākarmābhijāyate
BhP śuklāt prakāśabhūyiṣṭhā lokān āpnoti karhicit
BhP duḥkhodarkān kriyāyāsāṃs tamaḥśokotkaṭān kvacit
BhP kvacit pumān kvacic ca strī kvacin nobhayam andhadhīḥ
BhP devo manuṣyas tiryag vā yathākarmaguṇaṃ bhavaḥ
BhP kṣutparīto yathā dīnaḥ sārameyo gṛhaṃ gṛham
BhP caran vindati yaddiṣṭaṃ daṇḍam odanam eva vā
BhP tathā kāmāśayo jīva uccāvacapathā bhraman
BhP upary adho vā madhye vā yāti diṣṭaṃ priyāpriyam
BhP duḥkheṣv ekatareṇāpi daivabhūtātmahetuṣu
BhP jīvasya na vyavacchedaḥ syāc cet tattatpratikriyā
BhP yathā hi puruṣo bhāraṃ śirasā gurum udvahan
BhP taṃ skandhena sa ādhatte tathā sarvāḥ pratikriyāḥ
BhP naikāntataḥ pratīkāraḥ karmaṇāṃ karma kevalam
BhP dvayaṃ hy avidyopasṛtaṃ svapne svapna ivānagha
BhP arthe hy avidyamāne 'pi saṃsṛtir na nivartate
BhP manasā liṅgarūpeṇa svapne vicarato yathā
BhP athātmano 'rthabhūtasya yato 'narthaparamparā
BhP saṃsṛtis tadvyavacchedo bhaktyā paramayā gurau
BhP vāsudeve bhagavati bhaktiyogaḥ samāhitaḥ
BhP sadhrīcīnena vairāgyaṃ jñānaṃ ca janayiṣyati
BhP so 'cirād eva rājarṣe syād acyutakathāśrayaḥ
BhP śṛṇvataḥ śraddadhānasya nityadā syād adhīyataḥ
BhP yatra bhāgavatā rājan sādhavo viśadāśayāḥ
BhP bhagavadguṇānukathana śravaṇavyagracetasaḥ
BhP tasmin mahanmukharitā madhubhic caritrapīyūṣaśeṣasaritaḥ paritaḥ sravanti
BhP tā ye pibanty avitṛṣo nṛpa gāḍhakarṇais tān na spṛśanty aśanatṛḍbhayaśokamohāḥ
BhP etair upadruto nityaṃ jīvalokaḥ svabhāvajaiḥ
BhP na karoti harer nūnaṃ kathāmṛtanidhau ratim
BhP prajāpatipatiḥ sākṣād bhagavān giriśo manuḥ
BhP dakṣādayaḥ prajādhyakṣā naiṣṭhikāḥ sanakādayaḥ
BhP marīcir atryaṅgirasau pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ
BhP bhṛgur vasiṣṭha ity ete madantā brahmavādinaḥ
BhP adyāpi vācaspatayas tapovidyāsamādhibhiḥ
BhP paśyanto 'pi na paśyanti paśyantaṃ parameśvaram
BhP śabdabrahmaṇi duṣpāre caranta uruvistare
BhP mantraliṅgair vyavacchinnaṃ bhajanto na viduḥ param
BhP sarveṣām eva jantūnāṃ satataṃ dehapoṣaṇe
BhP asti prajñā samāyattā ko viśeṣas tadā nṛṇām
BhP labdhvehānte manuṣyatvaṃ hitvā dehādyasadgraham
BhP ātmasṛtyā vihāyedaṃ jīvātmā sa viśiṣyate
BhP yadā yasyānugṛhṇāti bhagavān ātmabhāvitaḥ
BhP sa jahāti matiṃ loke vede ca pariniṣṭhitām
BhP tasmāt karmasu barhiṣmann ajñānād arthakāśiṣu
BhP mārthadṛṣṭiṃ kṛthāḥ śrotra sparśiṣv aspṛṣṭavastuṣu
BhP svaṃ lokaṃ na vidus te vai yatra devo janārdanaḥ
BhP āhur dhūmradhiyo vedaṃ sakarmakam atadvidaḥ
BhP āstīrya darbhaiḥ prāgagraiḥ kārtsnyena kṣitimaṇḍalam
BhP stabdho bṛhadvadhān mānī karma nāvaiṣi yat param
BhP tat karma haritoṣaṃ yat sā vidyā tanmatir yayā
BhP harir dehabhṛtām ātmā svayaṃ prakṛtir īśvaraḥ
BhP tatpādamūlaṃ śaraṇaṃ yataḥ kṣemo nṛṇām iha
BhP sa vai priyatamaś cātmā yato na bhayam aṇv api
BhP iti veda sa vai vidvān yo vidvān sa gurur hariḥ
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP praśna evaṃ hi sañchinno bhavataḥ puruṣarṣabha
BhP atra me vadato guhyaṃ niśāmaya suniścitam
BhP kṣudraṃ caraṃ sumanasāṃ śaraṇe mithitvā
BhP raktaṃ ṣaḍaṅghrigaṇasāmasu lubdhakarṇam
BhP agre vṛkān asutṛpo 'vigaṇayya yāntaṃ
BhP pṛṣṭhe mṛgaṃ mṛgaya lubdhakabāṇabhinnam
BhP  asyārthaḥ sumanaḥsamadharmaṇāṃ strīṇāṃ śaraṇa āśrame puṣpamadhugandhavat
kṣudratamaṃ kāmyakarmavipākajaṃ kāmasukhalavaṃ jaihvyaupasthyādi vicinvantaṃ
mithunībhūya tadabhiniveśitamanasaṃ ṣaḍaṅghrigaṇasāmagītavad atimanoharavanitādijanālāpeṣv
atitarām atipralobhitakarṇam agre vṛkayūthavad ātmana āyur harato 'horātrān tān
kālalavaviśeṣān avigaṇayya gṛheṣu viharantaṃ pṛṣṭhata eva parokṣam anupravṛtto
lubdhakaḥ kṛtānto 'ntaḥ śareṇa yam iha parāvidhyati tam imam ātmānam aho rājan bhinnahṛdayaṃ draṣṭum arhasīti
BhP sa tvaṃ vicakṣya mṛgaceṣṭitam ātmano 'ntaś
BhP cittaṃ niyaccha hṛdi karṇadhunīṃ ca citte
BhP jahy aṅganāśramam asattamayūthagāthaṃ
BhP prīṇīhi haṃsaśaraṇaṃ virama krameṇa
BhP rājovāca
BhP śrutam anvīkṣitaṃ brahman bhagavān yad abhāṣata
BhP naitaj jānanty upādhyāyāḥ kiṃ na brūyur vidur yadi
BhP saṃśayo 'tra tu me vipra sañchinnas tatkṛto mahān
BhP ṛṣayo 'pi hi muhyanti yatra nendriyavṛttayaḥ
BhP karmāṇy ārabhate yena pumān iha vihāya tam
BhP amutrānyena dehena juṣṭāni sa yad aśnute
BhP iti vedavidāṃ vādaḥ śrūyate tatra tatra ha
BhP karma yat kriyate proktaṃ parokṣaṃ na prakāśate
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP yenaivārabhate karma tenaivāmutra tat pumān
BhP bhuṅkte hy avyavadhānena liṅgena manasā svayam
BhP śayānam imam utsṛjya śvasantaṃ puruṣo yathā
BhP karmātmany āhitaṃ bhuṅkte tādṛśenetareṇa vā
BhP mamaite manasā yad yad asāv aham iti bruvan
BhP gṛhṇīyāt tat pumān rāddhaṃ karma yena punar bhavaḥ
BhP yathānumīyate cittam ubhayair indriyehitaiḥ
BhP evaṃ prāgdehajaṃ karma lakṣyate cittavṛttibhiḥ
BhP nānubhūtaṃ kva cānena dehenādṛṣṭam aśrutam
BhP kadācid upalabhyeta yad rūpaṃ yādṛg ātmani
BhP tenāsya tādṛśaṃ rāja liṅgino dehasambhavam
BhP śraddhatsvānanubhūto 'rtho na manaḥ spraṣṭum arhati
BhP mana eva manuṣyasya pūrvarūpāṇi śaṃsati
BhP bhaviṣyataś ca bhadraṃ te tathaiva na bhaviṣyataḥ
BhP adṛṣṭam aśrutaṃ cātra kvacin manasi dṛśyate
BhP yathā tathānumantavyaṃ deśakālakriyāśrayam
BhP sarve kramānurodhena manasīndriyagocarāḥ
BhP āyānti bahuśo yānti sarve samanaso janāḥ
BhP sattvaikaniṣṭhe manasi bhagavatpārśvavartini
BhP tamaś candramasīvedam uparajyāvabhāsate
BhP nāhaṃ mameti bhāvo 'yaṃ puruṣe vyavadhīyate
BhP yāvad buddhimano'kṣārtha guṇavyūho hy anādimān
BhP suptimūrcchopatāpeṣu prāṇāyanavighātataḥ
BhP nehate 'ham iti jñānaṃ mṛtyuprajvārayor api
BhP garbhe bālye 'py apauṣkalyād ekādaśavidhaṃ tadā
BhP liṅgaṃ na dṛśyate yūnaḥ kuhvāṃ candramaso yathā
BhP arthe hy avidyamāne 'pi saṃsṛtir na nivartate
BhP dhyāyato viṣayān asya svapne 'narthāgamo yathā
BhP evaṃ pañcavidhaṃ liṅgaṃ trivṛt ṣoḍaśa vistṛtam
BhP eṣa cetanayā yukto jīva ity abhidhīyate
BhP anena puruṣo dehān upādatte vimuñcati
BhP harṣaṃ śokaṃ bhayaṃ duḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ cānena vindati
BhP bhaktiḥ kṛṣṇe dayā jīveṣv akuṇṭhajñānam ātmani
BhP yadi syād ātmano bhūyād apavargas tu saṃsṛteḥ
BhP yathā tṛṇajalūkeyaṃ nāpayāty apayāti ca
BhP na tyajen mriyamāṇo 'pi prāgdehābhimatiṃ janaḥ
BhP adṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭavan naṅkṣed bhūtaṃ svapnavad anyathā
BhP bhūtaṃ bhavad bhaviṣyac ca suptaṃ sarvarahorahaḥ
BhP yāvad anyaṃ na vindeta vyavadhānena karmaṇām
BhP mana eva manuṣyendra bhūtānāṃ bhavabhāvanam
BhP yadākṣaiś caritān dhyāyan karmāṇy ācinute 'sakṛt
BhP sati karmaṇy avidyāyāṃ bandhaḥ karmaṇy anātmanaḥ
BhP atas tad apavādārthaṃ bhaja sarvātmanā harim
BhP paśyaṃs tadātmakaṃ viśvaṃ sthityutpattyapyayā yataḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP bhāgavatamukhyo bhagavān nārado haṃsayor gatim
BhP pradarśya hy amum āmantrya siddhalokaṃ tato 'gamat
BhP prācīnabarhī rājarṣiḥ prajāsargābhirakṣaṇe
BhP ādiśya putrān agamat tapase kapilāśramam
BhP tatraikāgramanā dhīro govindacaraṇāmbujam
BhP vimuktasaṅgo 'nubhajan bhaktyā tatsāmyatām agāt
BhP etad adhyātmapārokṣyaṃ gītaṃ devarṣiṇānagha
BhP yaḥ śrāvayed yaḥ śṛṇuyāt sa liṅgena vimucyate
BhP etan mukundayaśasā bhuvanaṃ punānaṃ
BhP devarṣivaryamukhaniḥsṛtam ātmaśaucam
BhP yaḥ kīrtyamānam adhigacchati pārameṣṭhyaṃ
BhP nāsmin bhave bhramati muktasamastabandhaḥ
BhP adhyātmapārokṣyam idaṃ mayādhigatam adbhutam
BhP evaṃ striyāśramaḥ puṃsaś chinno 'mutra ca saṃśayaḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP ye tvayābhihitā brahman sutāḥ prācīnabarhiṣaḥ
BhP te rudragītena hariṃ siddhim āpuḥ pratoṣya kām
BhP kiṃ bārhaspatyeha paratra vātha kaivalyanāthapriyapārśvavartinaḥ
BhP āsādya devaṃ giriśaṃ yadṛcchayā prāpuḥ paraṃ nūnam atha pracetasaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP pracetaso 'ntar udadhau pitur ādeśakāriṇaḥ
BhP apayajñena tapasā purañjanam atoṣayan
BhP daśavarṣasahasrānte puruṣas tu sanātanaḥ
BhP teṣām āvirabhūt kṛcchraṃ śāntena śamayan rucā
BhP suparṇaskandham ārūḍho meruśṛṅgam ivāmbudaḥ
BhP pītavāsā maṇigrīvaḥ kurvan vitimirā diśaḥ
BhP kāśiṣṇunā kanakavarṇavibhūṣaṇena
BhP bhrājatkapolavadano vilasatkirīṭaḥ
BhP aṣṭāyudhair anucarair munibhiḥ surendrair
BhP āsevito garuḍakinnaragītakīrtiḥ
BhP pīnāyatāṣṭabhujamaṇḍalamadhyalakṣmyā
BhP spardhacchriyā parivṛto vanamālayādyaḥ
BhP barhiṣmataḥ puruṣa āha sutān prapannān
BhP parjanyanādarutayā saghṛṇāvalokaḥ
BhP śrībhagavān uvāca
BhP varaṃ vṛṇīdhvaṃ bhadraṃ vo yūyaṃ me nṛpanandanāḥ
BhP sauhārdenāpṛthagdharmās tuṣṭo 'haṃ sauhṛdena vaḥ
BhP yo 'nusmarati sandhyāyāṃ yuṣmān anudinaṃ naraḥ
BhP tasya bhrātṛṣv ātmasāmyaṃ tathā bhūteṣu sauhṛdam
BhP ye tu māṃ rudragītena sāyaṃ prātaḥ samāhitāḥ
BhP stuvanty ahaṃ kāmavarān dāsye prajñāṃ ca śobhanām
BhP yad yūyaṃ pitur ādeśam agrahīṣṭa mudānvitāḥ
BhP atho va uśatī kīrtir lokān anu bhaviṣyati
BhP bhavitā viśrutaḥ putro 'navamo brahmaṇo guṇaiḥ
BhP ya etām ātmavīryeṇa trilokīṃ pūrayiṣyati
BhP kaṇḍoḥ pramlocayā labdhā kanyā kamalalocanā
BhP tāṃ cāpaviddhāṃ jagṛhur bhūruhā nṛpanandanāḥ
BhP kṣutkṣāmāyā mukhe rājā somaḥ pīyūṣavarṣiṇīm
BhP deśinīṃ rodamānāyā nidadhe sa dayānvitaḥ
BhP prajāvisarga ādiṣṭāḥ pitrā mām anuvartatā
BhP tatra kanyāṃ varārohāṃ tām udvahata mā ciram
BhP apṛthagdharmaśīlānāṃ sarveṣāṃ vaḥ sumadhyamā
BhP apṛthagdharmaśīleyaṃ bhūyāt patny arpitāśayā
BhP divyavarṣasahasrāṇāṃ sahasram ahataujasaḥ
BhP bhaumān bhokṣyatha bhogān vai divyāṃś cānugrahān mama
BhP atha mayy anapāyinyā bhaktyā pakvaguṇāśayāḥ
BhP upayāsyatha maddhāma nirvidya nirayād ataḥ
BhP gṛheṣv āviśatāṃ cāpi puṃsāṃ kuśalakarmaṇām
BhP madvārtāyātayāmānāṃ na bandhāya gṛhā matāḥ
BhP navyavad dhṛdaye yaj jño brahmaitad brahmavādibhiḥ
BhP na muhyanti na śocanti na hṛṣyanti yato gatāḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP evaṃ bruvāṇaṃ puruṣārthabhājanaṃ janārdanaṃ prāñjalayaḥ pracetasaḥ
BhP taddarśanadhvastatamorajomalā girāgṛṇan gadgadayā suhṛttamam
BhP pracetasa ūcuḥ
BhP namo namaḥ kleśavināśanāya nirūpitodāraguṇāhvayāya
BhP manovacovegapurojavāya sarvākṣamārgair agatādhvane namaḥ
BhP śuddhāya śāntāya namaḥ svaniṣṭhayā manasy apārthaṃ vilasaddvayāya
BhP namo jagatsthānalayodayeṣu gṛhītamāyāguṇavigrahāya
BhP namo viśuddhasattvāya haraye harimedhase
BhP vāsudevāya kṛṣṇāya prabhave sarvasātvatām
BhP namaḥ kamalanābhāya namaḥ kamalamāline
BhP namaḥ kamalapādāya namas te kamalekṣaṇa
BhP namaḥ kamalakiñjalka piśaṅgāmalavāsase
BhP sarvabhūtanivāsāya namo 'yuṅkṣmahi sākṣiṇe
BhP rūpaṃ bhagavatā tv etad aśeṣakleśasaṅkṣayam
BhP āviṣkṛtaṃ naḥ kliṣṭānāṃ kim anyad anukampitam
BhP etāvat tvaṃ hi vibhubhir bhāvyaṃ dīneṣu vatsalaiḥ
BhP yad anusmaryate kāle svabuddhyābhadrarandhana
BhP yenopaśāntir bhūtānāṃ kṣullakānām apīhatām
BhP antarhito 'ntarhṛdaye kasmān no veda nāśiṣaḥ
BhP asāv eva varo 'smākam īpsito jagataḥ pate
BhP prasanno bhagavān yeṣām apavargaḥ gurur gatiḥ
BhP varaṃ vṛṇīmahe 'thāpi nātha tvat parataḥ parāt
BhP na hy antas tvadvibhūtīnāṃ so 'nanta iti gīyase
BhP pārijāte 'ñjasā labdhe sāraṅgo 'nyan na sevate
BhP tvadaṅghrimūlam āsādya sākṣāt kiṃ kiṃ vṛṇīmahi
BhP yāvat te māyayā spṛṣṭā bhramāma iha karmabhiḥ
BhP tāvad bhavatprasaṅgānāṃ saṅgaḥ syān no bhave bhave
BhP tulayāma lavenāpi na svargaṃ nāpunarbhavam
BhP bhagavatsaṅgisaṅgasya martyānāṃ kim utāśiṣaḥ
BhP yatreḍyante kathā mṛṣṭās tṛṣṇāyāḥ praśamo yataḥ
BhP nirvairaṃ yatra bhūteṣu nodvego yatra kaścana
BhP yatra nārāyaṇaḥ sākṣād bhagavān nyāsināṃ gatiḥ
BhP saṃstūyate satkathāsu muktasaṅgaiḥ punaḥ punaḥ
BhP teṣāṃ vicaratāṃ padbhyāṃ tīrthānāṃ pāvanecchayā
BhP bhītasya kiṃ na roceta tāvakānāṃ samāgamaḥ
BhP vayaṃ tu sākṣād bhagavan bhavasya priyasya sakhyuḥ kṣaṇasaṅgamena
BhP suduścikitsyasya bhavasya mṛtyor bhiṣaktamaṃ tvādya gatiṃ gatāḥ sma
BhP yan naḥ svadhītaṃ guravaḥ prasāditā viprāś ca vṛddhāś ca sadānuvṛttyā
BhP āryā natāḥ suhṛdo bhrātaraś ca sarvāṇi bhūtāny anasūyayaiva
BhP yan naḥ sutaptaṃ tapa etad īśa nirandhasāṃ kālam adabhram apsu
BhP sarvaṃ tad etat puruṣasya bhūmno vṛṇīmahe te paritoṣaṇāya
BhP manuḥ svayambhūr bhagavān bhavaś ca ye 'nye tapojñānaviśuddhasattvāḥ
BhP adṛṣṭapārā api yanmahimnaḥ stuvanty atho tvātmasamaṃ gṛṇīmaḥ
BhP namaḥ samāya śuddhāya puruṣāya parāya ca
BhP vāsudevāya sattvāya tubhyaṃ bhagavate namaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti pracetobhir abhiṣṭuto hariḥ prītas tathety āha śaraṇyavatsalaḥ
BhP anicchatāṃ yānam atṛptacakṣuṣāṃ yayau svadhāmānapavargavīryaḥ
BhP atha niryāya salilāt pracetasa udanvataḥ
BhP vīkṣyākupyan drumaiś channāṃ gāṃ gāṃ roddhum ivocchritaiḥ
BhP tato 'gnimārutau rājann amuñcan mukhato ruṣā
BhP mahīṃ nirvīrudhaṃ kartuṃ saṃvartaka ivātyaye
BhP bhasmasāt kriyamāṇāṃs tān drumān vīkṣya pitāmahaḥ
BhP āgataḥ śamayām āsa putrān barhiṣmato nayaiḥ
BhP tatrāvaśiṣṭā ye vṛkṣā bhītā duhitaraṃ tadā
BhP ujjahrus te pracetobhya upadiṣṭāḥ svayambhuvā
BhP te ca brahmaṇa ādeśān māriṣām upayemire
BhP yasyāṃ mahadavajñānād ajany ajanayonijaḥ
BhP cākṣuṣe tv antare prāpte prāksarge kālavidrute
BhP yaḥ sasarja prajā iṣṭāḥ sa dakṣo daivacoditaḥ
BhP yo jāyamānaḥ sarveṣāṃ tejas tejasvināṃ rucā
BhP svayopādatta dākṣyāc ca karmaṇāṃ dakṣam abruvan
BhP taṃ prajāsargarakṣāyām anādir abhiṣicya ca
BhP yuyoja yuyuje 'nyāṃś ca sa vai sarvaprajāpatīn
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP tata utpannavijñānā āśv adhokṣajabhāṣitam
BhP smaranta ātmaje bhāryāṃ visṛjya prāvrajan gṛhāt
BhP dīkṣitā brahmasatreṇa sarvabhūtātmamedhasā
BhP pratīcyāṃ diśi velāyāṃ siddho 'bhūd yatra jājaliḥ
BhP tān nirjitaprāṇamanovacodṛśo jitāsanān śāntasamānavigrahān
BhP pare 'male brahmaṇi yojitātmanaḥ surāsureḍyo dadṛśe sma nāradaḥ
BhP tam āgataṃ ta utthāya praṇipatyābhinandya ca
BhP pūjayitvā yathādeśaṃ sukhāsīnam athābruvan
BhP pracetasa ūcuḥ
BhP svāgataṃ te surarṣe 'dya diṣṭyā no darśanaṃ gataḥ
BhP tava caṅkramaṇaṃ brahmann abhayāya yathā raveḥ
BhP yad ādiṣṭaṃ bhagavatā śivenādhokṣajena ca
BhP tad gṛheṣu prasaktānāṃ prāyaśaḥ kṣapitaṃ prabho
BhP tan naḥ pradyotayādhyātma jñānaṃ tattvārthadarśanam
BhP yenāñjasā tariṣyāmo dustaraṃ bhavasāgaram
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti pracetasāṃ pṛṣṭo bhagavān nārado muniḥ
BhP bhagavaty uttamaśloka āviṣṭātmābravīn nṛpān
BhP nārada uvāca
BhP taj janma tāni karmāṇi tad āyus tan mano vacaḥ
BhP nṛṇāṃ yena hi viśvātmā sevyate harir īśvaraḥ
BhP kiṃ janmabhis tribhir veha śaukrasāvitrayājñikaiḥ
BhP karmabhir vā trayīproktaiḥ puṃso 'pi vibudhāyuṣā
BhP śrutena tapasā vā kiṃ vacobhiś cittavṛttibhiḥ
BhP buddhyā vā kiṃ nipuṇayā balenendriyarādhasā
BhP kiṃ vā yogena sāṅkhyena nyāsasvādhyāyayor api
BhP kiṃ vā śreyobhir anyaiś ca na yatrātmaprado hariḥ
BhP śreyasām api sarveṣām ātmā hy avadhir arthataḥ
BhP sarveṣām api bhūtānāṃ harir ātmātmadaḥ priyaḥ
BhP yathā taror mūlaniṣecanena tṛpyanti tatskandhabhujopaśākhāḥ
BhP prāṇopahārāc ca yathendriyāṇāṃ tathaiva sarvārhaṇam acyutejyā
BhP yathaiva sūryāt prabhavanti vāraḥ punaś ca tasmin praviśanti kāle
BhP bhūtāni bhūmau sthirajaṅgamāni tathā harāv eva guṇapravāhaḥ
BhP etat padaṃ taj jagadātmanaḥ paraṃ sakṛd vibhātaṃ savitur yathā prabhā
BhP yathāsavo jāgrati suptaśaktayo dravyakriyājñānabhidābhramātyayaḥ
BhP yathā nabhasy abhratamaḥprakāśā bhavanti bhūpā na bhavanty anukramāt
BhP evaṃ pare brahmaṇi śaktayas tv amū rajas tamaḥ sattvam iti pravāhaḥ
BhP tenaikam ātmānam aśeṣadehināṃ kālaṃ pradhānaṃ puruṣaṃ pareśam
BhP svatejasā dhvastaguṇapravāham ātmaikabhāvena bhajadhvam addhā
BhP dayayā sarvabhūteṣu santuṣṭyā yena kena vā
BhP sarvendriyopaśāntyā ca tuṣyaty āśu janārdanaḥ
BhP apahatasakalaiṣaṇāmalātmany aviratam edhitabhāvanopahūtaḥ
BhP nijajanavaśagatvam ātmano 'yan na sarati chidravad akṣaraḥ satāṃ hi
BhP na bhajati kumanīṣiṇāṃ sa ijyāṃ harir adhanātmadhanapriyo rasajñaḥ
BhP śrutadhanakulakarmaṇāṃ madair ye vidadhati pāpam akiñcaneṣu satsu
BhP śriyam anucaratīṃ tadarthinaś ca dvipadapatīn vibudhāṃś ca yat svapūrṇaḥ
BhP na bhajati nijabhṛtyavargatantraḥ katham amum udvisṛjet pumān kṛtajñaḥ
BhP maitreya uvāca
BhP iti pracetaso rājann anyāś ca bhagavatkathāḥ
BhP śrāvayitvā brahmalokaṃ yayau svāyambhuvo muniḥ
BhP te 'pi tanmukhaniryātaṃ yaśo lokamalāpaham
BhP harer niśamya tatpādaṃ dhyāyantas tadgatiṃ yayuḥ
BhP etat te 'bhihitaṃ kṣattar yan māṃ tvaṃ paripṛṣṭavān
BhP pracetasāṃ nāradasya saṃvādaṃ harikīrtanam
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ya eṣa uttānapado mānavasyānuvarṇitaḥ
BhP vaṃśaḥ priyavratasyāpi nibodha nṛpasattama
BhP yo nāradād ātmavidyām adhigamya punar mahīm
BhP bhuktvā vibhajya putrebhya aiśvaraṃ samagāt padam
BhP imāṃ tu kauṣāraviṇopavarṇitāṃ kṣattā niśamyājitavādasatkathām
BhP pravṛddhabhāvo 'śrukalākulo muner dadhāra mūrdhnā caraṇaṃ hṛdā hareḥ
BhP vidura uvāca
BhP so 'yam adya mahāyogin bhavatā karuṇātmanā
BhP darśitas tamasaḥ pāro yatrākiñcanago hariḥ
BhP śrīśuka uvāca
BhP ity ānamya tam āmantrya viduro gajasāhvayam
BhP svānāṃ didṛkṣuḥ prayayau jñātīnāṃ nirvṛtāśayaḥ
BhP etad yaḥ śṛṇuyād rājan rājñāṃ haryarpitātmanām
BhP āyur dhanaṃ yaśaḥ svasti gatim aiśvaryam āpnuyāt
